Bhartṛhari Vākyapadīya

t kāṇḍa

anādinidhanam brahma śabdatattvaṃ yad akṣaram 
vivartate arthabhāvena prakriyā jagato yataḥ ।। 

ekam eva yad āmnātaṃ bhinnaśaktivyapāśrayāt 
apṛthaktve api śaktibhyaḥ pṛthaktveneva vartate ।। 

adhyāhitakalāṃ yasya kālaśaktim upāśritāḥ 
janmādayo vikārāḥ ṣaḍ bhāvabhedasya yonayaḥ ।। 

ekasya sarvabījasya yasya ceyam anekadhā 
bhoktṛbhoktavyarūpeṇa bhogarūpeṇa ca sthitiḥ ।। 

prāptyupāyo anukāraś ca tasya vedo maharṣibhiḥ 
eko apy anekavartmeva samāmnātaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।। 

bhedānāṃ bahumārgatvaṃ karmaṇy ekatra cāṇgatā 
śabdānāṃ yataśaktitvaṃ tasya śākhāsu dṛṣyate ।। 

smṛtayo bahurūpās ca dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaprayojanāḥ 
tam evāśritya liṅgebhyo vedavidbhiḥ prakalpitāḥ ।। 

tasyārthavādarūpāṇi niśritāḥ svavikalpajāḥ 
ekatvināṃ dvaitināṃ ca pravādā bahudhāgatā ।। 

satyā visuddhis tatroktā vidyaivekapadāgamā 
yuktā praṇavarūpeṇa sarvavādāvirodhinā ।। 

vidhātus tasya lokānām aṅgopāṅganibandhanāḥ 
vidyābhedāḥ pratāyante jnānasaṃskārahetavaḥ ।। 

āsannaṃ brahmaṇas tasya tapasām uttamaṃ tapaḥ 
prathamaṃ chandasām aṅgam āhur vyākaraṇaṃ budhāḥ ।। 

prāptarūpavibhāgāyā yo vācaḥ paramo rasaḥ 
yat tat puṇyatamaṃ jyotis tasya mārgo ayam ānjasasḥ ।। 

arthapravṛttitattvānāṃ śabdā eva nibandhanam 
tattvāvabodjaḥ śabdānaṃ nāsti vyākaraṇād ṛte ।। 

tad dvāram apavargasya vāṅmalānāṃ cikitsitam 
pavitraṃ sarvavidyānām adhividyaṃ prakāsate ।। 

yathārthajātayaḥ sarvāḥ sabākṛtinibandhanāḥ 
tathaiva loke vidyānām esā vidyā parāyanam ।। 

idam ādyaṃ padasthānaṃ siddhisopānaparvaṇām 
iyaṃ sā mokṣamāṇānām ajihmā rājapaddhatiḥ ।। 

atrātītaviparyāsaḥ kevalām anupasyati 
chandasyas chandasāṃ yonim ātmā chandomayīṃ tanum ।। 

pratyasthamitabhedāyā yad vāco rūpam uttamam 
yad asminn eva tamasi jyotiḥ suddhaṃ vivartate ।। 

vaikṛtaṃ samati krāntā mūrtivyāpāradarśanam 
vyatītyālokatamasī prakāśaṃ yam upāsate ।। 

yatra vāco nimettāni cihnānīvākṣarasmṛteḥ 
śabdapūrveṇa yogena bhāsante pratibimbavat ।। 

atharvaṇām aṅgirasāṃ sāṃnām ṛgyajuṣasya ca 
yasminn uccāvacā varṇāḥ pṛthaksthitaparigrahāḥ ।। 

yad ekaṃ prakriyābhedair bahudhā pravibhajyate 
tad vyākaraṇaṃ āgamya paraṃ brahmādhigamyate ।। 

nityāḥ śabdārthasaṃbandhās tatrāmnātā maharṣibhiḥ 
sūtrāṇāṃ sānutantrāṇāṃ bhāṣyāṇāṃ ca praṇetṛbhiḥ ।। 

apoddhārapadārthāḥ ye ye cārthāḥ sthitalakṣaṇāḥ 
anvākhyeyāś ca ye śabdā ye cāpi pratipādakāḥ ।। 

kāryakāraṇabhāvena yogyabhāvena ca sthitāḥ 
dharme ye pratyaye cāṅgaṃ saṃbandhāḥ sādhvasādhuṣu ।। 

te liṅgaiś ca svaśabdaiś ca śāstre asminn upavarṇitāḥ 
smṛtyartham anugamyante ke cid eva yathāgamam ।। 

śiṣṭebhya āgamāt siddhāḥ sādhavo dharmasādhanam 
arthapratyāyanābhede viparītās tv asādhavaḥ ।। 

nityatve kṛtakatve vā teṣām ādir na vidyate 
prāṇinām iva sā caiṣā vyavasthānityatocyate ।। 

nānarthikām imāṃ kaś cid vyavasthāṃ kartum arhati 
tasmān nibadhyate śiṣṭaiḥ sādhutvaviṣayā smṛtiḥ ।। 

na cāgamād ṛte dharmas tarkeṇa vyavatiṣṭhate 
ṛṣīṇām api yaj jñānaṃ tad apy āgamapūrvakam ।। 

dharmasya cāvyavacchinnāḥ panthāno ye vyavasthitāḥ 
na tāṃl lokaprasiddhatvāt kaś cit tarkeṇa bādhate ।। 

avasthādeśakālānāṃ bhedād bhinnāsu śaktiṣu 
bhāvānām anumānena prasiddhir atidurlabhā ।। 

nirjñātaśakter dravyasya tāṃ tān arthakriyāṃ prati 
viśiṣṭadravyasaṃbandhe sā śaktiḥ pratibadhyate ।। 

yatnenānumito apy arthaḥ kuśalair anumātṛbhiḥ 
abhiyuktatarair anyair anyathaivopapādyate ।। 

pareṣām asamākhyeyam abhyāsād eva jāyate 
maṇirūpyādivijñānaṃ tadvidāṃ nānumānikam ।। 

pratyakṣam anumānaṃ ca vyatikramya vyavasthitāḥ 
pitṛrakṣaḥpiśācānāṃ karmajā eva siddhayaḥ ।। 

āvirbhūtaprakāśānām anupaplutacetasām 
atītānāgatajñānaṃ pratyakṣān na viśiṣyate ।। 

atīndriyān asaṃvedyān paśyanty ārṣeṇa cakṣuṣā 
ye bhāvān vacanaṃ teṣāṃ nānumānena bādhate ।। 

yo yasya svam iva jñānaṃ darśanaṃ nātiśaṅkate 
sthitaṃ pratyakṣapakṣe taṃ katham anyo nivartayet ।। 

idaṃ puṇyam idaṃ pāpam ity etasmin padadvaye 
ācaṇḍālamanuṣyāṇām alpaṃ śāstraprayojanam ।। 

caitanyam iva yaś cāyam avicchedena vartate 
āgamas tam upāsīno hetuvādair na bādhyate ।। 

hastasparśād ivāndhena viṣame pathi dhāvatā 
anumānapradhānena vinipāto na durlabhaḥ ।। 

tasmād akṛtakaṃ śāstraṃ smṛtiṃ ca sanibandhanām 
āśrityārabhyate śiṣṭaiḥ sādhutvaviṣayā smṛtiḥ ।। 

dvāv upādānaśabdeṣu śabdau śabdavido viduḥ 
eko nimittaṃ śabdānām aparo arthe prayujyate ।। 

avibhakto vibhaktebhyo jāyate arthasya vācakaḥ 
śabdas tatrārtharūpātmā saṃbandham upagacchati ।। 

ātmabhedaṃ tayoḥ ke cid astīty āhuḥ purāṇagāḥ 
buddhibhedād abhinnasya bhedam eke pracakṣate ।। 

araṇisthaṃ yathā jyotiḥ prakāśāntarakāraṇam 
tadvac chabdo api buddhisthaḥ śrutīnāṃ kāraṇaṃ pṛthak ।। 

vitarkitaḥ purā buddhyā kva cid arthe niveśitaḥ 
karaṇebhyo vivṛttena dhvaninā so anugṛhyate ।। 

nādasya kramajātatvān na pūrvo na paraś ca saḥ 
akramaḥ kramarūpeṇa bhedavān iva jāyate ।। 

pratibimbaṃ yathānyatra sthitaṃ toyakriyāvaśāt 
tatpravṛttim ivānveti sa dharmaḥ sphoṭanādayoḥ ।। 

ātmarūpaṃ yathā jñāne jñeyarūpaṃ ca dṛśyate 
artharūpaṃ tathā śabde svarūpaṃ ca prakāśate ।। 

āṇḍabhāvam ivāpanno yaḥ kratuḥ śabdasaṃjñakaḥ 
vṛttis tasya kriyārūpā bhāgaśo bhajate kramam ।। 

yathaikabuddhiviṣayā mūrtir ākriyate paṭe 
mūrtyantarasya tritayam evaṃ śabde api dṛśyate ।। 

yathā prayoktuḥ prāg buddhiḥ śabdeṣv eva pravartate 
vyavasāyo grahītṝṇām evaṃ teṣv eva jāyate ।। 

arthopasarjanībhūtān abhidheyeṣu keṣu cit 
caritārthān parārthatvān na lokaḥ pratipadyate ।। 

grāhyatvaṃ grāhakatvaṃ ca dve śaktī tejaso yathā 
tathaiva sarvaśabdānām ete pṛthag avasthite ।। 

viṣayatvam anāpannaiḥ śabdair nārthaḥ prakāśyate 
na sattayaiva te arthānām agṛhītāḥ prakāśakāḥ ।। 

ato anirjñātarūpatvāt kim āhety abhidhīyate 
nendriyāṇāṃ prakāśye arthe svarūpaṃ gṛhyate tathā ।। 

bhedenāvagṛhītau dvau śabdadharmāv apoddhṛtau 
bhedakāreṣu hetutvam avirodhena gacchataḥ ।। 

vṛddhyādayo yathā śabdāḥ svarūpopanibandhanāḥ 
ādaicpratyāyitaiḥ śabdaiḥ saṃbandhaṃ yānti saṃjñibhiḥ ।। 

agniśabdas tathaivāyam agniśabdanibandhanaḥ 
agniśrutyaiti saṃbandham agniśabdābhidheyayā ।। 

yo ya uccāryate śabdo niyataṃ na sa kāryabhāk 
anyapratyāyane śaktir na tasya pratibadhyate ।। 

uccaran paratantratvād guṇaḥ kāryair na yujyate 
tasmāt tadarthaiḥ kāryāṇāṃ saṃbandhaḥ parikalpyate ।। 

sāmānyam āśritaṃ yad yad upamānopameyayoḥ 
tasya tasyopamāneṣu dharmo anyo vyatiricyate ।। 

guṇaḥ prakarṣahetur yaḥ svātantryeṇopadiśyate 
tasyāśritād guṇād eva prakṛṣṭatvaṃ pratīyate ।। 

tasyābhidheyabhāvena yaḥ śabdaḥ samavasthitaḥ 
tasāpy uccāraṇe rūpam anyat tasmād vivicyate ।। 

prāk samjñinābhisaṃbandhāt saṃjñā rūpapadārthikā 
ṣaṣṭyāś ca prathamāyāś ca nimittatvāya kalpate ।। 

tatrārthavattvāt prathamā saṃjñāśabdād vidhīyate 
asyete vyatirekaś ca tadarthād eva jāyate ।। 

svaṃ rūpam iti kaiś cit tu vyaktiḥ saṃjñopadiśyate 
jāteḥ kāryāṇi saṃsṛṣṭā jātis tu pratipadyate ।। 

saṃjñinīṃ vyaktim icchanti sūtre grāhyām athāpare 
jātipratyāyitā vyaktiḥ pradeśeṣūpatiṣṭhate ।। 

kāryatve nityatāyāṃ vā ke cid ekatvavādinaḥ 
kāryatve nityatāyāṃ vā ke cin nānātvavādinaḥ ।। 

padabhede api varṇānām ekatvaṃ na nivartate 
vākyeṣu padam ekaṃ ca bhinneṣv apy upalabhyate ।। 

na varṇavyatirekeṇa padam anyac ca vidyate 
vākyaṃ varṇapadābhyāṃ ca pravibhāgo na kaś cana ।। 

pade na varṇā vidyante varṇeṣv avayavā na ca 
vākyāt padānām atyantaṃ pravibhāgo na kaś cana ।। 

bhinnadarśanam āśritya vyavahāro anugamyate 
tatra yan mukhyam ekeṣāṃ tatrānyeṣāṃ viparyayaḥ ।। 

sphotasyābhinnakālasya dhvanikālānupātinaḥ 
grahaṇopādhibhedena vṛttibhedaṃ pracakṣate ।। 

svabhāvabhedān nityatve hrasvadīrghaplutādiṣu 
prākṛtasya dhvaneḥ kālaḥ śabdasyety upacaryate ।। 

śabdasya grahaṇe hetuḥ prākṛto dhvanir iṣyate 
sthitibhedanimittatvaṃ vaikṛtaḥ pratipadyate ।। 

śabdasyordhvam abhivyakter vṛttibhedaṃ tu vaikṛtaḥ 
dhvanayaḥ samupohante sphoṭātmā tair na bhidyate ।। 

indriyasyaivasaṃskāraḥ śabdasyaivobhavasya vā 
kriyate dhvanibhir vādās trayo abhivyaktivādinām ।। 

indriyasyaiva saṃskāraḥ samādhānāñjanādibhiḥ 
viṣayasya tu saṃskāraḥ tadgandhapratipattaye ।। 

cakṣuṣaḥ prāpyakāritve tejasā tu dvayor api 
viṣayendriyayor iṣṭā saṃskāraḥ sa kramo dhvaneḥ ।। 

sphoṭarūpāvibhāgena dhvaner grahaṇam iṣyate 
kaiś cit dhvanir asaṃvedyaḥ svatantro anyaiḥ prakalpitaḥ ।। 

yathānuvākaḥ śloko vā soḍhatvam upagacchate 
āvṛttyā na tu sa granthaḥ pratyāvṛtti nirūpyate ।। 

pratyayair anupākhyeyair grahaṇānuguṇais tathā 
dhvaniprakāśite śabde svarūpam avadhāryate ।। 

nādair āhitabījāyām antyena dhvaninā saha 
āvṛttaparipākāyāṃ buddhau śabdo avadhāryate ।। 

asataś cāntarāle yāñ chabdān astīti manyate 
pratipattur aśaktiḥ sā grahaṇopāya eva saḥ ।। 

bhedānukāro jñānasya vācaś copaplavo dhruvaḥ 
kramopasṛṣṭarūpā vāg jñānaṃ jñeyavyapāśrayam ।। 

jñeyena na vinā jñānaṃ vyavahāre avatiṣṭhate 
nālabdhakramayā vācā kaś cid artho abhidhīyate ।। 

yathādyasaṃkhyāgrahaṇam upāyaḥ pratipattaye 
saṃkhyāntarāṇāṃ bhede api tathā śabdāntaraśrutiḥ ।। 

pratyekaṃ vyañjakā bhinna varṇavākyapadeṣu ye 
teṣām atyantabhede api saṃkīrṇā iva śaktayaḥ ।। 

yathaiva darśanaiḥ pūrvair dūrāt saṃtamase api vā 
anyathākṛtya viṣayam anyathaivādhyavasyati ।। 

vyajyamāne tathā vākye vākyābhivyaktihetubhiḥ 
bhāgāvagraharūpeṇa pūrvaṃ buddhiḥ pravartate ।। 

yathānupūrvīniyamo vikāre kṣīrabījayoḥ 
tathaiva pratipattṝṇāṃ niyato buddhiṣu kramaḥ ।। 

bhāgavatsv api teṣv eva rūpabhedo dhvaneḥ kramāt 
nirbhāgeṣv abhyupāyo vā bhāgabhedaprakalpanam ।। 

anekavyaktyabhivyaṅgyā jātiḥ sphoṭa iti smṛtā 
kaiś cit vyaktaya evāsya dhvanitvena prakalpitāḥ ।। 

avikārasya śabdasya nimittair vikṛto dhvaniḥ 
upalabdhau nimittatvam upayāti prakāśavat ।। 

na cānityeṣv abhivyaktir niyamena vyavasthitā 
āśrayair api nityānāṃ jātīnāṃ vyaktir iṣyate ।। 

deśādibhiś ca saṃbandho dṛṣṭaḥ kāyavatām api 
deśabhedavikalpe api na bhedo dhvaniśabdayoḥ ।। 

grahaṇagrāhyayoḥ siddhā yogyatā niyatā yathā 
vyaṅgyavyañjakabhāve api tathaiva sphoṭanādayoḥ ।। 

sadṛśagrahaṇānāṃ ca gandhādīnāṃ prakāśakam 
nimittaṃ niyataṃ loke pratidravyam avasthitam ।। 

prakāśakānāṃ bhedāṃś ca prakāśyo artho anuvartate 
tailodakādibhede tat pratyakṣaṃ pratibimbake ।। 

viruddhaparimāṇeṣu vajrādarśatalādiṣu 
parvatādisarūpāṇāṃ bhāvānāṃ nāsti saṃbhavaḥ ।। 

tasmād abhinnakāleṣu varṇavākyapadādiṣu 
vṛttikālaḥ svakālaś ca nādabhedād vibhajyate ।। 

yaḥ saṃyogavibhāgābhyāṃ karaṇair upajanyate 
sa sphoṭaḥ śabdajāḥ śabdā dhvanayo anyair udāhṛtāḥ ।। 

alpe mahati vā śabde sphoṭakālo na bhidyate 
paras tu śabdasaṃtānaḥ pracayāpacayātmakaḥ ।। 

dūrāt prabheva dīpasya dhvanimātraṃ tu lakṣyate 
ghaṇṭādūnāṃ ca śabdeṣu vyakto bhedaḥ sa dṛśyate ।। 

dravyābhighātāt pracitau bhinnau dīrghaplutāv api 
kampe tūparate jātā nādā vṛtter viśeṣakāḥ ।। 

anavasthitakampe api karaṇe dhvanayo apare 
sphoṭād evopajāyante jvālā jvālāntarād iva ।। 

vāyor aṇūnāṃ jñānasya śabdatvāpattir iṣyate 
kaiś cid darśanabhedo hi pravādeṣv anavasthitaḥ ।। 

labdhakriyāḥ prayatnena vaktur icccānuvartinā 
sthāneṣv abhihato vāyuḥ śabdatvaṃ pratipadyate ।। 

tasya kāraṇasāmarthyād vegapracayadharmaṇaḥ 
saṃnipātād vibhajyante sāravatyo api mūrtayaḥ ।। 

aṇavaḥ sarvaśaktitvād bhedasaṃsargavṛttayaḥ 
chāyātapatamaḥśabdabhāvena pariṇāminaḥ ।। 

svaśaktau vyajyamānāyāṃ prayatnena samīritāḥ 
abhrāṇīva pracīyante śabdākhyāḥ paramāṇavaḥ ।। 

athāyam āntaro jñātā sūkṣmavāgātmani sthitaḥ 
vyaktaye svasya rūpasya śabdatvena vivartate ।। 

sa manobhāvam āpadya tejasā pākam āgataḥ 
vāyum āviśati prāṇam athāsau samudīryate ।। 

antaḥkaraṇatattvasya vāyur āśrayatāṃ gataḥ 
taddharmeṇa samāviṣṭas tejasaiva vivartate ।। 

vibhajan svātmano granthīñ chrutirūpaiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ 
prāṇo varṇān abhivyajya varṇeṣv evopalīyate ।। 

ātmā buddhyā samarthyārthān mano yuṅkte vivakṣayā 
manaḥ kāyāgnim āhanti sa prerayati mārutam ।। 

ajasravṛttir yaḥ śabdaḥ sūkṣmatvān nopalabhyate 
vyajanād vāyur iva sa svanimittāt pratīyate ।। 

tasya prāṇe ca yā śaktir yā ca buddhau vyavasthitā 
vivartamānā sthāniṣu saiṣā bhedaṃ prapadyate ।। 

śabdeṣv evāśritā śaktir viśvasyāsya nibandhanī 
yannetraḥ pratibhātmāyaṃ bhedarūpaḥ pratāyate ।। 

śabdādibhedaḥ śabdena vyākhyāto rūpyate yataḥ 
tasmād arthavidhāḥ sarvāḥ śabdamātrāsu niśritāḥ ।। 

śabdasyapariṇāmo ayam ity āmnāyavido viduḥ 
chandobhya eva prathamam etad viśvaṃ pravartate ।। 

vibhajya bahudhātmānaṃ sa cchandasyaḥ prajāpatiḥ 
chandomayībhir mātrābhir bahudhaiva viveśa tam ।। 

sādhvī vāg bhūyasī yeṣu puruṣeṣu vyavasthitā 
adhikaṃ vartate teṣu puṇyaṃ rūpaṃ prajāpateḥ ।। 

prājāpatyaṃ mahat tejas tatpātrair iva saṃvṛttam 
śarīrabhede viduṣāṃ svāṃ yonim upadhāvati ।। 

yad etan maṇḍalaṃ bhāsvad dhāma citrasya rādhasaḥ 
tadbhāvam abhisaṃbhūya vidyāyāṃ pravilīyate ।। 

itikartavyatā loke sarvā śabdavyapāśrayā 
yāṃ pūrvāhitasaṃskāro bālo api pratipadyate ।। 

ādyaḥ kāraṇavinyāsaḥ prāṇasyordhvaṃ samīraṇam 
sthānānām abhighātaś ca na vinā śabdabhāvanām ।। 

na so asti pratyayo loke yaḥ śabdānugamād ṛte 
anuviddham iva jñānaṃ sarvaṃ śabdena bhāsate ।। 

vāgrūpatā cet utkrāmed avabodhasya śāśvatī 
na prakāśaḥ prakāśeta sā hi pratyavamarśinī ।। 

sā sarvavidyāśilpānāṃ kalānāṃ copabandhanī 
tadvaśād abhiniṣpannaṃ sarvaṃ vastu vibhajyate ।। 

saiṣā saṃsāriṇāṃ saṃjñā bahir antaś ca vartate 
tanmātrām avyatikrāntaṃ caitanyaṃ sarvajātiṣu ।। 

arthakriyāsu vāk sarvān samīhayati dehinaḥ 
tadutkrāntau visaṃjño ayaṃ dṛśyate kāṣṭakuḍyavat ।। 

bhedodgrāhavivartena labdhākāraparigrahā 
āmnātā sarvavidyāsu vāg eva prakṛtiḥ parā ।। 

ekatvam anatikrāntā vāṅnetrā vāṅnibandhanāḥ 
pṛthak pratyavabhāsante vāgvibhāgā gavādayaḥ ।। 

ṣaḍdvāraṃ ṣaḍadhiṣṭhānāṃ [ṣaṭpra]bodhāṃ ṣaḍavyayām 
te mṛtyum ativartante ye vai vācam upāsate ।। 

pravibhāge yathā kartā tayā kārye pravartate 
avibhāge tathā saiva kāryatvenāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

pravibhajyātmanātmānaṃ sṛṣṭvā bhāvān pṛthagvidhān 
sarveśvaraḥ sarvamayaḥ svapne bhoktā pravartate ।। 

svamātrā paramātrā vā śrutyā prakramyate yathā 
tathaiva rūḍhatām eti tayā hy artho vidhīyate ।। 

atyantam atathābhūte nimitte śrutyapāśrayāt 
dṛśyate alātacakrādau vastvākāranirūpaṇā ।। 

api prayoktur ātmānaṃ śabdam antar avasthitam 
prāhur mahāntam ṛṣabhaṃ yena sāyujyam iṣyate ।। 

tasmād yaḥ śabdasaṃskāraḥ sā siddhiḥ paramātmanaḥ 
tasya pravṛttitattvajñas tad brahmāmṛtam aśnute ।। 

prāṇavṛttim atikrānte vācas tattve vyavasthitaḥ 
kramasaṃhārayogena saṃhṛtyātmānam ātmani ।। 

vācaḥ saṃskāram ādhāya vācaṃ jñāne niveśya ca 
vibhajya bandhanāny asyāḥ kṛtvā tāṃ chinnabandhanām ।। 

jyotir āntaram āsādya cchinnagranthiparigrahaḥ 
kāraṇajyotiṣaikatvaṃ chittvā granthīn pravartate ।। 

na jātv akartṛkam kaś cid āgamaṃ pratipadyate 
bījaṃ sarvāgamāpāye trayy evāto vyavasthitā ।। 

astaṃ yāteṣu vādeṣu kartṛṣv anyeṣv asatsv api 
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ loko na vyativartate ।। 

jñāne svābhāvike nārthaḥ śāstraiḥ kaś cana vidyate 
dharmo jñānasya hetuś cet tasyāmnāyo nibandhanam ।। 

vedaśāstrāvirodhī ca tarkaś cakśur apaśyatām 
rūpamātrād dhi vākyārthaḥ kevalaṃ nātitiṣṭhati ।। 

sato avivakṣā pārārthyaṃ vyaktir arthasya laiṅgikī 
iti nyāyo bahuvidhas tarkeṇa pravibhajyate ।। 

śabdānām eva sā śaktis tarko yaḥ puruṣāśrayaḥ 
sa śabdānugato nyāyo anāgameṣv anibandhanaḥ ।। 

yad udumbaravarṇānāṃ ghaṭīnāṃ maṇḍalaṃ mahat 
pītaṃ na gamayet svargaṃ kiṃ tat kratugataṃ nayet ।। 

rūpādayo yathā dṛṣṭāḥ paryarthaṃ yataśaktayaḥ 
śabdās tathaiva dṛśyante viṣāpaharaṇādiṣu ।। 

yathaiṣāṃ tatra sāmarthyaṃ dharme apy evaṃ pratīyatām 
sādhūnāṃ sādhubhis tasmād vācyam abhyudayārthinām ।। 

sarvo adṛṣṭaphalān arthān āgamāt pratipadyate 
viparītaṃ ca sarvatra śakyate vaktum āgame ।। 

sādhutvajñānaviṣayā seyaṃ vyākaraṇasmṛtiḥ 
avicchedena śiṣṭānām idaṃ smṛtinibandhanam ।। 

vaikharyā madhyamāyāś ca paśyantyāś caitad adbhutam 
anekatīrthabhedāyās trayyā cācaḥ paraṃ param ।। 

gaur iva prakṣaraty ekā rasam uttamaśālinī 
divyādivyena rūpeṇa bhāratī gauḥ śucismitā ।। 

etayor antaraṃ paśya sūkṣmayoḥ spandamānayoḥ 
prāṇāpānāntare nityam ekā sarvasya tiṣṭhati ।। 

anyā tv apreryamāṇaiva vinā prāṇena vartate 
jāyate hi tataḥ prāṇo vācam āpyāyayan punaḥ ।। 

prāṇenāpyāyitā saivaṃ vyavahāranibandhanī 
sarvasyocchvāsam āsādya na vāg vadati karhi cit ।। 

ghoṣiṇī jātanirghoṣā aghoṣā ca pravartate 
tayor api ca ghoṣiṇyā nirghoṣaiva garīyasī ।। 

sthāneṣu vivṛte vāyau kṛtavarṇaparigrahā 
vaikharī vāk prayoktṝṇāṃ prāṇavṛttinibandhanā ।। 

kevalaṃ buddhyupādānakramarūpānupātinī 
prāṇavṛttim atikramya madhyamā vāk pravartate ।। 

avibhāgā tu paśyantī sarvataḥ saṃhṛtakramā 
svarūpajyotir evāntaḥ sūkṣmā vāg anapāyinī ।। 

pīyūṣāpūryamāṇāpi nityam āgantubhir malaiḥ 
antyā kaleva somasya nātyantam abhidhīyate ।। 

yasyāṃ dṛṣṭasvarūpāyām adhikāro nivartate 
puruṣe ṣoḍaśakale tām āhur amṛtāṃ kalām ।। 

prāptoparāgarūpā sā viplavair anuṣaṅgibhiḥ 
vaikharī sattvamātreva guṇair na vyavakīryate ।। 

tadvibhāgāvibhāgābhyāṃ kriyamāṇām avasthitam 
svabhāvajñais tu bhāvānāṃ dṛśyante śabdaśaktayaḥ ।। 

anādim avyavacchinnāṃ śrutim āhur akartṛkām 
śiṣṭair nibadhyamānā tu na vyavacchidyate smṛtiḥ ।। 

avibhāgād vivṛttānām abhikhyā svapnavac chrutau 
bhāvatattvaṃ tu vijñāya liṅgebhyo vihitā smṛtiḥ ।। 

kāyavāgbuddhiviṣayā ye malāḥ samavasthitāḥ 
cikitsālakṣaṇādhyātmaśāstrais teṣāṃ viśuddhayaḥ ।। 

śabdaḥ saṃskārahīno yo gaur iti prayuyukṣyate 
tam apabhraṃśam icchanti viśiṣṭārthaniveśinam ।। 

asvagoṇyādayaḥ śabdāḥ sādhavo viṣayāntare 
nimittabhedāt sarvatra sādhutvaṃ ca vyavasthitam ।। 

te sādhuṣv anumānena pratyayotpattihetavaḥ 
tādātmyam upagamyeva śabdārthasya prakāśakāḥ ।। 

na śiṣṭair anugamyante paryāyā iva sādhavaḥ 
te yataḥ smṛtiśāstreṇa tasmāt sākṣād avācakāḥ ।। 

aṃbvaṃbv iti yathā bālaḥ śikṣamāṇo apabhāṣate 
avyaktaṃ tadvidāṃ tena vyaktau bhavati niścayaḥ ।। 

evaṃ sādhau prayoktavye yo apabhraṃśaḥ prayujyate 
tena sādhuvyavahitaḥ kaś cid artho abhidhīyate ।। 

pāraṃparyād apabhraṃśā viguṇeṣv abhidhātṛṣu 
prasiddhim āgatā yena teṣāṃ sādhur avācakaḥ ।। 

daivī vāg vyatikīrṇeyam aśaktair abhidhātṛbhiḥ 
anityadarśināṃ tv asmin vāde buddhiviparyayaḥ ।। 

ubhayeṣām avicchedād anyaśabdavivakṣayā 
yo anyaḥ prayujyate śabdo na so arthasyābhidhāyakaḥ ।। 

ākhyātaṃ śabdasaṃghāto jātiḥ saṃghātavartinī 
eko anavayavaḥ śabdaḥ kramo buddhyanusaṃhṛtiḥ ।। 

padam ādyaṃ pṛthak sarvaṃ padaṃ sāpekṣam ity api 
vākyaṃ prati matir bhinnā bahudhā nyāyadarśinām ।। 

nighātādivyavasthārthaṃ śāstre yat paribhāṣitam 
sākāṅkṣāvayavaṃ tena na sarvaṃ tulyalakṣaṇaṃ ।। 

sākāṅkṣāvayavaṃ bhede parānākāṅkṣaśabdakam 
karmapradhānaṃ guṇavad ekārthaṃ vākyam ucyate ।। 

saṃbodhanapadaṃ yac ca tat kriyāyā viśeṣakam 
tathā tiṅantaṃ tatrāhus tiṅantasya viśeṣakam ।। 

yathānekam api ktvāntaṃ tiṅantasya viśeṣakam 
tathā tiṅantaṃ tatrāhus tiṅantasya viśeṣakam ।। 

yathaika eva sarvārthaprakāśaḥ pravibhajyate 
dṛśyabhedānukāreṇa vākyārthāvagamas tathā ।। 

citrasyaikasya rūpasya yathā bhedanidarśanaiḥ 
nīlādibhiḥ samākhyānaṃ kriyate bhinnalakṣaṇaiḥ ।। 

tathaivaikasya vākyasya nirākāṅkṣasya sarvataḥ 
śabdāntaraiḥ samākhyānaṃ sākāṅkṣair anugamyate ।। 

yathā pade vibhajyante prakṛtipratyayādayaḥ 
apoddhāras tathā vākye padānām upapadyate ।। 

varṇāntarasarūpatvaṃ varṇabhāgeṣu dṛṣyate 
padāntarasarūpāś ca padabhāgā iva sthitāḥ ।। 

bhāgair anarthakair yuktā vṛṣabhodakayāvakāḥ 
anvayavyatirekau tu vyavahāranibandhanam ।। 

śabdasya na vibhāgo asti kuto arthasya bhaviṣyati 
vibhāgaiḥ prakriyābhedam avidvān pratipadyate ।। 

brāhmaṇārtho yathā nāsti kaś cid brāhmaṇakambale 
devadattādayo vākye thataiva syur anarthakāḥ ।। 

sāmānyārthas tirobhūto na viśeṣe avatiṣṭhate 
upāttasya kutas tyāgo nivṛttaḥ kvāvatiṣṭhatām ।। 

aśābdo yadi vākyārthaḥ padārtho api tathā bhavet 
evaṃ sati ca saṃbandhaḥ śabdasyārthena hīyate ।। 

viśeśaśabdāḥ keṣāṃ cit sāmānyapratirūpakāḥ 
śabdāntarābhisaṃbandhād vyajyante pratipattṛṣu ।। 

teṣāṃ tu kṛtsno vākyārthaḥ pratibhedaṃ samāpyate 
vyaktopavyañjanā siddhir arthasya pratipatṛṣu ।। 

sa vyaktaḥ kramavāñ chabda upāṃśu yam adhīyate 
akramas tu vitatyeva buddhir yatrāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

yathotkṣepaviśeṣe api karmabhedo na gṛhyate 
āvṛttau vyajyate jātiḥ karmabhir bhramaṇādibhiḥ ।। 

varṇavākyapadeṣv evaṃ tulyopavyañjanā śrutiḥ 
atyantabhede tattvasya sarūpeva pratīyate ।। 

nityeṣu ca kutaḥ pūrvaṃ paraṃ vā paramārthataḥ 
ekasyaiva tu sā śaktir yad evam avabhāsate ।। 

ciraṃ kṣipram iti jñāne kālabhedād ṛte yathā 
bhinnakāle prakāśete sa dharmo hrasvadīrghayoḥ ।। 

na nityaḥ kramamātrābhiḥ kālo bhedam ihārhati 
vyāvartinīnāṃ mātrāṇām abhāve kīdṛśaḥ kramaḥ ।। 

tābhyo yā jāyate buddhir ekā sā bhāgavarjitā 
sā hi svaśaktyā bhinneva kramapratyavamarśinī ।। 

kramollekhānuṣaṅgeṇa tasyāṃ yad bījam āhitam 
tattvanānātvayos tasya niruktir nāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

bhāvanāsamaye tv etat kramasāmarthyam akramam 
vyāvṛttabhedo yenārtho bhedavān upalabhyate ।। 

padāni vākye tāny eva varṇās te ca pade yadi 
varṇeṣu varṇabhāgānāṃ bhedaḥ syāt paramāṇuvat ।। 

bhāgānām anupaśleṣān na varṇo na padaṃ bhavet 
teṣām avyapadeśyatvāt kim anyad vyapadiśyatām ।। 

yad antaḥśabdatattvaṃ tu bhāgair ekaṃ prakāśitam 
tam āhur apare śabdaṃ tasya vākye tathaikatām ।। 

arthabhāgais tathā teṣām antaro arthaḥ prakāśyate 
ekasyaivātmano bhedau śabdārthāv apṛthaksthitau ।। 

prakāśakaprakāśyatvaṃ kāryakāraṇarūpatā 
antarmātrātmanas tasya śabdatattvasya sarvadā ।। 

tasyaivāstitvanāstitve sāmarthye samavasthite 
akrame kramanirbhāse vyavahāranibandhane ।। 

saṃpratyayapramāṇatvāt padārthāstitvakalpane 
padārthābhyuccaye tyāgād ānarthakyaṃ prasajyate ।। 

rājaśabdena rājārtho bhinnarūpeṇa gamyate 
vṛttāv ākhyātasadṛśaṃ padam anyat prayujyate ।। 

yathāśvakarṇa ity ukte vinaivāśvena gamyate 
kaś cid eva viśiṣṭo arthaḥ sarveṣu pratyayas tathā ।। 

vākyeṣu arthāntaragataḥ sādṛśyaparikalpane 
keṣāṃ cit rūḍhiśabdatvaṃ śāstra evānugamyate ।। 

upādāyāpi ye heyās tān upāyān pracakṣate 
upāyānāṃ ca niyamo nāvaśyam avatiṣṭhate ।। 

arthaṃ kathaṃ cit puruṣaḥ kaś cit saṃpratipadyate 
saṃsṛṣṭā vā vibhaktā cā bhedā vākyanibandhanāḥ ।। 

so ayam ity abhisaṃbandho buddhyā prakramyate yadā 
vākyārthasya tadaiko api varṇaḥ pratyāyakaḥ kva cit ।। 

kevalena padenārtho yāvān evābhidhīyate 
vākyasthaṃ tāvato arthasya tad āhur abhidhāyakam ।। 

saṃbandhe sati yat tv anyad ādhikyam upajāyate 
vākyārtam eva taṃ prāhur anekapadasaṃśrayam ।। 

sa tv anekapadastho api pratibhedaṃ samāpyate 
jātivat samudāye api saṃkhyāvat kalpyate aparaiḥ ।। 

sarvabhedānuguṇyaṃ tu sāmānyam apare viduḥ 
tad arthāntarasaṃsargād bhajate bhedarūpatām ।। 

bhedān ākāṅkṣatas tasya yā pariplavamāmatā 
avacchinatti saṃbandhas tāṃ viśeṣe niveśayan ।। 

kāryānumeyaḥ saṃbandho rūpaṃ tasya na vidyate 
asattvabhūtam atyantam atas taṃ pratijānate ।। 

niyataṃ sādhane sādhyaṃ kriyā niyatasādhanā 
sa saṃnidhānamātreṇa niyamaḥ saṃprakāśate ।। 

guṇabhāvena sākāṅkṣaṃ tatra nāma pravartate 
sādhyatvena nimittāni kriyāpadam apekṣate ।। 

santa eva viśeṣā ye padārtheṣv avibhāvitāḥ 
te kramād anugamyante na vākyam abhidhāyakam ।। 

śabdānāṃ kramamātre ca nānyaḥ śabdo asti vācakaḥ 
kramo hi dharmaḥ kālasya tena vākyaṃ na vidyate ।। 

ye ca saṃbhavino bhedāḥ padārtheṣv avibhāvitāḥ 
te saṃnidhāne vyajyante na tu varṇeṣv ayaṃ kramaḥ ।। 

varṇānāṃ ca padānāṃ ca kramamātraniveśinī 
padākhyā vākyasaṃjñā ca śabdatvaṃ neṣyate tayoḥ ।। 

samāne api tu śabdatve dṛṣṭaḥ saṃpratyayaḥ padāt 
prativarṇaṃ tv asau nāsti padasyārtham ato viduḥ ।। 

yathā sāvayavā varṇā vinā vācyena kena cit 
arthavantaḥ samuditā vākyam apy evam iṣyate ।। 

anarthakāny apāyatvāt padārthenārthavanti vā 
krameṇoccaritāny āhur vākyārthaṃ bhinnalakṣaṇam ।। 

nityatve samudāyānāṃ jāter vā parikalpane 
ekasyaikārthatām āhur vākyasyāvyabhicāriṇīm ।। 

abhedapūrvakābhedāḥ kalpitā vākyavādibhiḥ 
bhedapūrvān abhedāṃs tu manyante padadarśinaḥ ।। 

padaprakṛtibhāvaś ca vṛttibhedena varṇyate 
padānāṃ saṃhitā yoniḥ saṃhitā vā padāśrayā ।। 

padāmnāyaś ca yady anyaḥ saṃhitāyā nidarśakaḥ 
nityas tatra kathaṃ kāryaṃ padaṃ lakṣaṇadarśanāt ।। 

prativarṇam asaṃvedyaḥ padārthapratyayo yathā 
padeśv evam asaṃvedyaṃ vākyārthasya nirūpaṇam ।। 

vākyārthaḥ saṃniviśate padeṣu sahavṛttiṣu 
yathā tathaiva varṇeṣu padārthaḥ sahavṛttiṣu ।। 

sūkṣmaṃ grāhyaṃ yathānyena saṃsṛṣṭaṃ saha gṛhyate 
varṇo apy anyena varṇena saṃbaddho vācakas tathā ।। 

padasyoccāraṇād artho yathā kaś cin nirūpyate 
varṇānām api sāṃnidhyāt tathā so arthaḥ pratīyate ।। 

prāptasya yasya sāmarthyān niyamārthā punaḥ śrutiḥ 
tenātyantaṃ viśeṣeṇa sāmānyaṃ yadi bādhyate ।। 

yajeteti tato dravyaṃ prāptaṃ sāmarthyalakṣaṇam 
vrīhiśrutyā nivarteta na syāt pratinidhis tathā ।। 

tasmād vrīhitvam adhikaṃ vrīhiśabdaḥ prakalpayet 
dravyatvam aviruddhatvāt prāptyarthaḥ san na bādhate ।। 

tena cāpi vyavacchinne dravyatve sahacāriṇi 
asaṃbhavād viśeṣāṇāṃ tatrānyeṣām adarśanam ।। 

na ca sāmānyavat sarve kriyāśabdena lakṣitāḥ 
viśeṣā na hi sarveṣāṃ satāṃ śabdo abhidhāyakaḥ ।। 

śuklādayo guṇāḥ santo yathā tatrāvivakṣitāḥ 
tathāvivakṣā bhedānāṃ dravyatvasahacāriṇām ।। 

asaṃnidhau pratinidhir mā bhūn nityasya karmaṇaḥ 
kāmyasya vā pravṛttasya lopa ity upapadyate ।। 

viśiṣṭaiva kriyā yena vākyārthaḥ parikalpyate 
dravyābhāve pratinidhau tasya tat syāt kriyāntaram ।। 

nirjñātārthaṃ padaṃ yac ca tadarthe pratipādite 
pikādi yad avijñātaṃ tat kim ity anuyujyate ।। 

sāmarthyaprāpitaṃ yac ca vyaktyartham anuṣajyate 
śrutir evānuṣaṅgeṇa bādhikā liṅgavākyayoḥ ।। 

aprāpto yas tu śuklādiḥ saṃnidhānena gamyate 
sa yatnaprāpito vākye śrutidharmavilakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

abhinnam eva vākyaṃ tu yady abhinnārtham iṣyate 
tat sarvaṃ śrutibhūtatvān na śrutyaiva virotsyate ।। 

vākyānāṃ samudāyaś ca ya ekārthaprasiddhaye 
sākāṅkṣāvayavas tatra vākyārtho api na vidyate ।। 

prāsaṅgikam idaṃ kāryam idaṃ tantreṇa labhyate 
idam āvṛttibhedābhyām atra bādhasamuccayau ।। 

ūho asmin viṣaye nyāyyaḥ saṃbandho asya na bādhyate 
sāmānyasyātideśo ayaṃ viśeṣo atrātidiśyate ।। 

arthitvam atra sāmarthyam asminn artho na bhidyate 
śāstrāt prāptādhikāro ayaṃ vyudāso asya kriyāntare ।। 

iyaṃ śrutyā kramaprāptir iyam uccāraṇād iti 
kramo ayam atra balavān asmiṃs tu na vivakṣitaḥ ।। 

idaṃ parāṅgaiḥ saṃbaddham aṅgānām aprayojakam 
prayojakam idaṃ teṣām atredaṃ nāntarīyakam ।। 

idaṃ pradhānaṃ śeṣo ayaṃ viniyogakramas tv ayam 
sākṣād asyopakārīdam idam ārād viśeṣakam ।। 

śaktivyāpārabhedo asmin phalam atra tu bhidyate 
saṃbandhāj jātabhedo ayaṃ bhedas tatrāvivakṣitaḥ ।। 

prasajyapratiṣedho ayaṃ paryudāso ayam atra tu 
idaṃ gauṇam idaṃ mukhyaṃ vyāpīdaṃ guru laghv idam ।। 

bhedenāṅgāṅgibhāvo asya bahubhedaṃ vikalpyate 
idaṃ niyamyate asyātra yogyatvam upajāyate ।। 

asya vākyāntare dṛṣṭāl liṅgād bhedo anumīyate 
ayaṃ śabdair apoddhṛtya padārthaḥ pravibhajyate ।। 

iti vākyeṣu ye dharmāḥ padārthopanibandhanāḥ 
sarve tena prakalperan padaṃ cet syad avācakam ।। 

avibhakte api vākyārthe śaktibhedād apoddhṛte 
vākyāntaravibhāgena yathoktaṃ na virudhyate ।। 

yathaivaikasya gandhasya bhedena parikalpanā 
puṣpādiṣu tathā vākye apy arthabhedo abhidhīyate ।। 

gavaye narasiṃhe vāpy ekajñānāvṛte yathā 
bhāgaṃ jātyantarasyaiva sadṛśaṃ pratipadyate ।। 

aprasiddhaṃ tu yaṃ bhāgam adṛṣṭam anupaśyati 
tāvaty asaṃvidaṃ mūḍhaḥ sarvatra pratipadyate ।। 

tathā pikādiyogena vākye atyantavilakṣaṇe 
sadṛśasyeva saṃjñānam asato arthasya manyate ।। 

ekasya bhāge sādṛśyaṃ bhāge bhedaś ca lakṣyate 
nirbhāgasya prakāśasya nirbhāgeṇaiva cetasā ।। 

tathaiva bhāge sādṛśyaṃ bhāge bhedo avasīyate 
bhāgābhāve api vākyānām atyantaṃ bhinnadharmaṇām ।। 

rūpanāśe padānāṃ syāt kathaṃ cāvadhikalpanā 
agṛhītāvadhau śabde kathaṃ cārtho vivicyate ।। 

saṃsarga iva rūpāṇāṃ śabde anyatra vyavasthitaḥ 
nānārūpeṣu tadrūpaṃ tantreṇāparam iṣyate ।। 

tasminn abhede bhedānāṃ saṃsarga iva vartate 
rūpaṃ rūpāntarāt tasmād ananyat pravibhajyate ।। 

śāstre pratyāyakasyāpi kvacid ekatvam āśritam 
pratyāyyena kvacid bhedo grahaṇagrāhyayoḥ sthitaḥ ।। 

ū ity abhedam āśritya yathāsaṃkhyaṃ prakalpitam 
lṛluṭor grahaṇe bhedo grāhyābhyāṃ parikalpitaḥ ।। 

yasyety etad aṇo rūpaṃ saṃjñinām abhidhāyakam 
na hi pratīyamānena grahaṇasyāsti saṃbhavaḥ ।। 

ū ity etad abhinnaṃ ca bhinnavākyanibandhanam 
bhedena grahaṇaṃ yasya pararūpam iva dvayoḥ ।। 

plutasyāṅgavivṛddhiṃ ca samāhāram acos tathā 
vyudasyatā punar bhedaḥ śabdeṣv atyantam āśritaḥ ।। 

ardharcādiṣu śabdeṣu rūpabhedaḥ kramād yathā 
tantrāt tathaikaśabdatve bhinnānāṃ śrutir anyathā ।। 

saṃhitāviṣaye varṇāḥ svarūpeṇāvikāriṇaḥ 
śabdāntaratvaṃ yāntīva śaktyantaraparigrahāt ।। 

indriyādivikāreṇa dṛṣṭaṃ grāhyeṣu vastuṣu 
ātmatyāgād ṛte bhinnaṃ grahaṇaṃ sa kramaḥ śrutau ।। 

abhidhānakriyābhedāc chabdeṣv avikṛteṣv api 
rūpam atyantabhedena tad evaikaṃ prakāśate ।। 

ṛco vā gītimātraṃ vā sāma dravyāntaraṃ na tu 
gītibhedāt tu gṛhyante tā eva vikṛtā ṛcaḥ ।। 

upāyāc chrutisaṃhāre bhinnānām ekaśeṣiṇām 
tantreṇoccāraṇe teṣāṃ śāstre sādhutvam ucyate ।। 

parigṛhya śrutiṃ caikāṃ rūpabhedavatām api 
tantreṇoccāraṇaṃ kāryam anyathā te na sādhavaḥ ।। 

sarūpāṇāṃ ca vākyānāṃ śāstreṇāpratipāditam 
tantreṇoccāraṇād ekaṃ rūpaṃ sādhūpalabhyate ।। 

ekasyānekarūpatvaṃ nālikādiparigrahāt 
yathā tathaiva tantrāt syād bahūnām ekarūpatā ।। 

yathā padasarūpāṇāṃ vākyānāṃ saṃbhavaḥ pṛthak 
tathā vākyāntarābhāve syād eṣāṃ pṛthagarthatā ।। 

abhidheyaḥ padasyārtho vākyasyārthaḥ prayojanam 
yasya tasya na saṃbandho vākyānām upapadyate ।। 

tatra kriyāpadāny eva vyapekṣante parasparam 
kriyāpadānuṣaktas tu saṃbandho atha pratīyate ।। 

āvṛttir anuvādo vā padārthavyaktikalpane 
pratyekaṃ tu samāpto arthaḥ sahabhūteṣu vartate ।। 

avikalpitavākyārthe vikalpā bhāvanāśrayāḥ 
atrādhikaraṇe vādāḥ pūrveṣāṃ bahudhā matāḥ ।। 

abhyāsāt pratibhāhetuḥ sarvaḥ śabdo aparaiḥ smṛtaḥ 
bālānāṃ ca tiraścāṃ ca yathārthapratipādane ।। 

anāgamaś ca so abhyāsaḥ samayaḥ kaiś cid iṣyate 
anantaram idaṃ kāryam asmād ity upadarśakaḥ ।। 

asty arthaḥ sarvaśabdānāṃ iti pratyāyyalakṣaṇam 
apūrvadevatāsvargaiḥ samam āhur gavādiṣu ।। 

prayogadarśanābhyāsād ākārāvagrahas tu yaḥ 
na sa śabdasya viṣayaḥ sa hi yatnāntarāśrayaḥ ।। 

ke cid bhedāḥ prakāśyante śabdais tadabhidhāyibhiḥ 
anuniṣpādinaḥ kāṃś cic chabdārthān iti manyate ।। 

jāteḥ pratyāyake śabde yā vyaktir anuṣaṅgiṇī 
na tadvyaktigatān bhedāñ jātiśabdo avalambate ।। 

ghaṭādīnāṃ na cākārān pratyāyayati vācakaḥ 
vastumātraniveśitvāt tadgatir nāntarīyakā ।। 

kriyā vinā prayogeṇa na dṛṣṭā śabdacoditā 
prayogas tv anuniṣpādī śabdārtha iti gamyate ।। 

niyatās tu prayogā ye niyataṃ yac ca sādhanam 
teṣāṃ śabdābhidheyatvam aparair anugamyate ।। 

samudāyo abhidheyo vāpy avikalpasamuccayaḥ 
asatyo vāpi saṃsargaḥ śabdārthaḥ kaiś cid iṣyate ।। 

asatyopādhi yat satyaṃ tad vā śabdanibandhanām 
śabdo vāpy abhijalpatvam āgato yāti vācyatām ।। 

so ayam ity abhisaṃbandhād rūpam ekīkṛtaṃ yatā 
śabdasyārthena taṃ śabdam abhijalpaṃ pracakṣate ।। 

tayor apṛthagātmatve rūḍhir avyabhicāriṇī 
kiṃ cid eva kva cid rūpaṃ prādhānyenāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

loke artharūpatāṃ śabdaḥ pratipannaḥ pravartate 
śāstre tūbhayarūpatvaṃ pravibhaktaṃ vivakṣayā ।। 

aśakteḥ sarvaśakter vā śabdair eva prakalpitā 
ekasyārthasya niyatā kriyādiparikalpanā ।। 

yo vārtho buddhiviṣayo bāhyavastunibandhanaḥ 
sa bāhyaṃ vastv iti jñātaḥ śabdārtha iti gamyate ।। 

ākāravantaḥ saṃvedyā vyaktismṛtinibandhanāḥ 
ete pratyavabhāsante saṃvinṃātraṃ tv ato anyathā ।। 

yathendriyaṃ saṃnipatad vaicitreṇopadarśakaṃ 
tathaiva śabdād arthasya pratipattir anekadhā ।। 

vaktrānyathaiva prakrānto bhinneṣu pratipattṛṣu 
svapratyayānukāreṇa śabdārthaḥ pravibhajyate ।। 

ekasminn api dṛśye arthe darśanaṃ bhidyate pṛthak 
kālāntareṇa caiko api taṃ paśyaty anyathā punaḥ ।। 

ekasyāpi ca śabdasya nimittair avyavasthitaiḥ 
ekena bahubhiś cārtho bahudhā parikalpyate ।। 

tasmād adṛṣṭatattvānāṃ sāparādhaṃ bahucchalaṃ 
darśanaṃ vacanaṃ vāpi nityam evānavasthitam ।। 

ṛṣīṇāṃ darśanaṃ yac ca tattve kiṃ cid avasthitam 
na tena vyavahāro asti na tac chabdanibandhanaṃ ।। 

talavad dṛśyate vyoma khadyoto havyavāḍ iva 
naiva cāsti talaṃ vyomni na khadyote hutāśanaḥ ।। 

tasmāt pratyakṣam apy arthaṃ vidvān īkṣeta yuktitaḥ 
na darśanasya prāmāṇyād dṛśyam arthaṃ prakalpayet ।। 

asamākhyeyatattvānām arthānāṃ laukikair yathā 
vyavahāre samākhyānaṃ tat prajño na vikalpayet ।। 

vicchedagrahaṇe arthānāṃ pratibhānyaiva jāyate 
vākyārtha iti tām āhuḥ padārthair upapāditām ।। 

idaṃ tad iti sānyeṣām anākyeyā kathaṃ cana 
pratyātmavṛtti siddhā sā kartrāpi na nirūpyate ।। 

upaśleṣam ivārthānāṃ sā karoty avicāritā 
sārvarūpyam ivāpannā viṣayatvena vartate ।। 

sākśāc chabdena janitāṃ bhāvanānugamena vā 
itikartavyatāyāṃ tāṃ na kaś cid ativartate ।। 

pramāṇatvena tāṃ lokaḥ sarvaḥ samanugacchati 
samārambhāḥ pratāyante tiraścām api tadvaśāt ।। 

yathā dravyaviśeṣāṇāṃ paripākair ayatnajāḥ 
madādiśaktayo dṛṣṭāḥ pratibhās tadvatāṃ tathā ।। 

svaravṛttiṃ vikurute madhau puṃskokilasya kaḥ 
jantvādayaḥ kulāyādikaraṇe śikṣitāḥ katham ।। 

āhāraprītyapadveṣaplavanādikriyāsu kaḥ 
jātyanvayaprasiddhāsu prayoktā mṛgapakṣiṇām ।। 

bhāvanānugatād etad āgamād eva jāyate 
āsattiviprakarṣābhyām āgamas tu viśiṣyate ।। 

svabhāvavaraṇābhāsayogādṛṣṭopapāditām 
viśiṣṭopahitāṃ ceti pratibhāṃ ṣaḍvidhāṃ viduḥ ।। 

yathā saṃyogibhir dravyair lakṣite arthe prayujyate 
gośabdo na tv asau teṣāṃ viśeśāṇāṃ prakāśakaḥ ।। 

ākāravarṇāvayavaiḥ saṃsṛṣṭeṣu gavādiṣu 
śabdaḥ pravartamāno api na tān aṅgīkaroty asau ।। 

saṃsthānavarṇāvayavair viśiṣṭe arthe prayujyate 
śabdo na tasyāvayave pravṛttir upalabhyate ।। 

durlabhaṃ kasya cil loke sarvāvayavadarśanaṃ 
kaiś cit tv avayavair dṛṣṭair arthaḥ kṛtso anumīyate ।। 

tathā jātyutpalādīnāṃ gandhena sahacāriṇām 
nityasaṃbandhināṃ dṛṣṭaṃ guṇānām avadhāraṇam ।। 

saṃkhyāpramāṇasaṃsthānanirapekṣaḥ pravartate 
bindau ca samudāye ca vācakaḥ salilādiṣu ।। 

saṃskārādiparicchinne tailādau yo vyavasthitaḥ 
āhaikadeśaṃ tattvena tasyāvayavavartinā ।। 

yenārthenābhisaṃbaddham abhidhānaṃ prayujyate 
tadarthāpagame tasya prayogo vinivartate ।। 

yāṃs tu saṃbhavino dharmān antarṇīya prayujyate 
śabdas teṣāṃ na sāṃnidhyaṃ niyamena vyapekṣate ।। 

yathā romaśaphādīnāṃ vyabhicāre api dṛśyate 
gośabdo na tathā jāter viprayoge pravartate ।। 

tasmāt saṃbhavino arthasya śabdāt saṃpratyaye sati 
adṛṣṭaviprayogārthaḥ saṃbandhitvena gamyate ।। 

vācikā dyotikā va syur dvitvādīnāṃ vibhaktayaḥ 
syād vā saṃkhyāvato arthasya samudāyo abhidhāyakaḥ ।। 

vinā saṃkhyābhidhānād vā saṃkhyābhedasamanvitān 
arthān svarūpabhedena kāmś cid āhur gavādayaḥ ।। 

ye śabdā nityasaṃbandhā viveke jñātaśaktayaḥ 
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ teṣām artho vibhajyate ।। 

yāvac cāvyabhicāreṇa tayoḥ śakyaṃ prakalpanam 
niyamas tatra na tv evaṃ niyamo nuṭśabādiṣu ।। 

saṃbhave nābhidhānasya lakṣaṇatvaṃ prakalpate 
āpekṣikyo hi saṃsarge niyatāḥ śabdaśaktayaḥ ।। 

na kūpasūpayūpānām anvayo arthasya dṛśyate 
ato arthāntaravācitvaṃ saṃghātasyaiva gamyate ।। 

anvākhyānāni bhidyante śabdavyutpattikarmasu 
bahūnāṃ saṃbhave arthānāṃ nimittaṃ kiṃ cid iṣyate ।। 

vairavāsiṣṭhagiriśās tathaikāgārikādayaḥ 
kaiś cit kathaṃ cid ākhyātā nimittāvadhisaṃkaraiḥ ।। 

yathā pathaḥ samākhyānaṃ vṛkṣavalmīkaparvataiḥ 
aviruddhaṃ gavādīnāṃ bhinnaiś ca sahacāribhiḥ ।। 

anyathā ca samākhyānam avasthābhedadarśibhiḥ 
kriyate kiṃśukādīnām ekadeśāvadhāraṇaṃ ।। 

kaiś cin nirvacanaṃ bhinnaṃ girater garjater gameḥ 
gavater gadater vāpi gaur ity atrānudarśitam ।। 

gaur ity eva svarūpād vā gośabdo goṣu vartate 
vyutpādyate na vā sarvaṃ kaiś cic cobhayatheṣyate ।। 

sāmānyenopadeśaś ca śāstre laghvartham āśritaḥ 
jātyantaravad anyasya viśeṣāḥ pratipādakāḥ ।। 

arthāntare ca yad vṛttaṃ tat prakṛtyantaraṃ viduḥ 
tulyarūpaṃ na tad rūḍhāv anyasminn anuṣajyate ।। 

bhinnāv ijiyajī dhātū niyatau viṣayāntare 
kaiś cit kathaṃ cid uddiṣṭau citraṃ hi pratipādanam ।। 

evaṃ ca vālavāyādi jitvarīvad upācaret 
bhedābhedābhyupagame na virodho asti kaś cana ।। 

aḍādīnāṃ vyavasthārthaṃ pṛthaktvena prakalpanam 
dhātūpasargayoḥ śāstre dhātur eva tu tādṛśaḥ ।। 

tathā hi saṃgrāmayateḥ sopasargād vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ 
kriyāviśeṣāḥ samghāte prakramyante tathāvidhāḥ ।। 

kāryāṇām antaraṅgatvam evaṃ dhātūpasargayoḥ 
sādhanair yāti saṃbandhaṃ tathābhūtaiva sā kriyā ।। 

prayogārtheṣu siddhaḥ san bhettavyo artho viśiṣyate 
prāk ca sādhanasaṃbandhāt kriyā naivopajāyate ।। 

dhātoḥ sādhanayogasya bhāvinaḥ prakramād yathā 
dhātutvaṃ karmabhāvaś ca tathānyad api dṛśyatām ।। 

bījakāleṣu saṃbandhād yathā lākṣārasādayaḥ 
varṇādipariṇāmena phalānām upakurvate ।। 

buddhisthād abhisaṃbandhāt tathā dhātūpasargayoḥ 
abhyantarīkṛtād bhedaḥ padakāle prakāśate ।। 

kva cit saṃbhavino bhedāḥ kevalair anidarśitāḥ 
upasargeṇa saṃbandhe vyajyante pranirādinā ।। 

sa vācako viśeṣāṇāṃ saṃbhavād dyotako api vā 
śaktyādhānāya vā dhātoḥ sahakārī prayujyate ।। 

sthādibhiḥ kevalair yac ca gamanādi na gamyate 
tatrānumānād dvividhāt taddharmā prādir ucyate ।। 

aprayoge adhiparyoś ca yāvad dṛṣṭaṃ kriyāntaram 
tasyābhidhāyako dhātuḥ saha tābhyām anarthakaḥ ।। 

tathaiva svārthikāḥ ke cit saṃghātāntaravṛttayaḥ 
anarthakena saṃsṛṣṭāḥ prakṛtyarthānuvādinaḥ ।। 

nipātā dyotakāḥ ke cit pṛthagarthaprakalpane 
āgamā iva ke cit tu saṃbhūyārthasya sādhakāḥ ।। 

upariṣṭāt purastād vā dyotakatvaṃ na bhidyate 
teṣu prayujyamāneṣu bhinnārtheṣv api sarvathā ।। 

cādayo na prayujyante padatve sati kevalāḥ 
pratyayo vācakatve api kevalo na prayujyate ।। 

samuccitābhidhāne tu vyatireko na vidyate 
asattvabhūto bhāvaś ca tiṅpadair abhidhīyate ।। 

samuccitābhidhāne api viśiṣṭārthābhidhāyinām 
guṇair padānāṃ saṃbandhaḥ paratantrās tu cādayaḥ ।। 

janayitvā kriyā kā cit saṃbandhaṃ vinivartate 
śrūyamāṇe kriyāśabde saṃbandho jāyate kva cit ।। 

tatra ṣaṣṭhī pratipadaṃ samāsasya nivṛttaye 
vihitā darśanārthaṃ tu kārakaṃ pratyudāhṛtam ।। 

sa copajātaḥ saṃbandho vinivṛtte kriyāpade 
karmapravacanīyena tatra tatra niyamyate ।। 

yena kriyāpadākṣepaḥ sa kārakavibhaktibhiḥ 
yujyate vir yathā tasya likhāv anupasargatā ।। 

tiṣṭhater aprayogaś ca dṛṣṭo apraty ajayann iti 
sunv abhīty ābhimukhye ca kevalo api prayujyate ।। 

karmapravacanīyatvaṃ kriyāyoge vidhīyate 
ṣatvādivinivṛttyarthaṃ svatyādīnāṃ vidharmaṇām ।। 

hetuhetumator yogaparicchede anunā kṛte 
ārambhād bādhyate prāptā tṛtīyā hetulakṣaṇā ।। 

kriyāyā dyotako nāyaṃ na saṃbandhasya vācakaḥ 
nāpi kriyāpadākṣepi saṃbandhasya tu bhedakaḥ ।। 

anarthakānāṃ saṃghātaḥ sārthako anarthakas tathā 
varṇānāṃ padam arthena yuktaṃ nāvayavāḥ pade ।। 

padānām arthayuktānāṃ saṃghāto bhidyate punaḥ 
arthāntarāvabodhena saṃbandhavigamena ca ।। 

sārthakānarthakau bhede saṃbandhaṃ nādhigacchataḥ 
adhigacchata ity eke kuṭīrādinidarśanāt ।। 

arthavadbhyo viśiṣṭārthaḥ saṃghāta upajāyate 
nopajāyata ity eke samāsasvārthikādiṣu ।। 

ke cid dhi yutasiddhārthā bhede nirjñātaśaktayaḥ 
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ ke cit kalpitaśaktayaḥ ।। 

śāstrārtha eva varṇānām arthavattve pradarśitaḥ 
dhātvādīnāṃ hi śuddhānāṃ laukiko artho na vidyate ।। 

kṛttaddhitānām arthaś ca kevalānām alaukikaḥ 
prāg vibhaktes tadantasya tathaivārtho na vidyate ।। 

abhivyaktataro yo arthaḥ pratyayānteṣu lakṣyate 
arthavattāprakaraṇād āśritaḥ sa tathāvidhaḥ ।। 

ātmabhedo na cet kaś cid varṇebhyaḥ padavākyayoḥ 
anyonyāpekṣayā śaktyā varṇaḥ syād abhidhāyakaḥ ।। 

varṇena kena cin nyūnaḥ saṃghāto yo abhidhāyakaḥ 
na cec chabdāntaram asāv anyūnas tena gamyate ।। 

sa tasmin vācake śabde nimittāt smṛtim ādadhat 
sākṣād iva vyavahitaṃ śabdenārtham upohate ।। 

padavācyo yathā nārthaḥ kaś cid gaurakharādiṣu 
saty api pratyaye atyantaṃ samudāye na gamyate ।। 

samanvita ivārthātmā padārthair yaḥ pratīyate 
padārthadarśanaṃ tatra tathaivānupakārakam ।। 

samudāyāvayavayor bhinnārthatve ca vṛttiṣu 
yugapad bhedasaṃsargau viruddhāv anuṣaṅgiṇau ।। 

kaś ca sādhanamātrārthān adhyādīn parikalpayet 
aprayuktapadaś cārtho bahuvrīhau kathaṃ bhavet ।। 

prajñusaṃjñvādyavayavair na cāsty arthāvadhāraṇam 
tasmāt saṃghāta evaiko viśiṣṭārthanibandhanam ।। 

gargā ity eka evāyaṃ bahuṣv artheṣu vartate 
dvandvasaṃjño api saṃghāto bahūnām abhidhāyakaḥ ।। 

yathaikaśeṣe bhujyādiḥ pratyekam avatiṣṭhate 
kriyaivaṃ dvandvavācye arthe pratyekaṃ pravibhajyate ।। 

yac ca dvandvapadārthasya tacchabdena vyapekṣaṇam 
sāpi vyāvṛttarūpe arthe sarvanāmasarūpatā ।। 

yathā ca khadiracchede bhāgeṣu kramavāṃs chidiḥ 
tathā dvandvapadārthasya bhāgeṣu kramadarśanam ।। 

saṅghaikadeśe prakrāntān yathā saṅghānupātinaḥ 
kriyāviśeṣān manyante sa dvandvāvayave kramaḥ ।। 

pratipādayatā vṛttim abuddhān vākyapūrvikām 
vṛttau padārthabhedena prādhānyam upadarśitam ।। 

abhedād abhidheyasya nañsamāse vikalpitam 
prādhānyaṃ bahudhā bhāṣye doṣās tu prakriyāgatāḥ ।। 

jahatsvārthavikalpe ca sarvārthatyāgam icchatā 
bahuvrīhipadārthasya tyāgaḥ sarvasya darśitaḥ ।। 

śāstre kva cit prakṛtyarthaḥ pratyayenābhidhīyate 
prakṛtau vinivṛttāyāṃ pratyayārthaś ca dhātubhiḥ ।। 

yam artham āhatur bhinnau pratyayāv eka eva tam 
kva cid āha pacantīti dhātus tābhyāṃ vinā kva cit ।। 

anvākhyānasmṛter ye ca pratyayārthā nibandhanam 
nirdiṣṭās te prakṛtyarthāḥ smṛtyantara udāhṛtāḥ ।। 

prasiddher udvamikarīty evaṃ śāstre abhidhīyate 
vyavahārāya manyante śāstrārthaprakriyā yataḥ ।। 

śāstreṣu prakriyābhedair avidyaivopavarṇyate 
anāgamavikalpā tu svayaṃ vidyopavartate ।। 

anibaddhaṃ nimitteṣu nirupākhyaṃ phalaṃ yathā 
tathā vidyāpy anākhyeyā śāstropāyeva lakṣyate ।। 

yathābhyāsaṃ hi vāg arthe pratipattiṃ samīhate 
svabhāva iva cānādir mithyābhyāso vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

utprekṣate sāvayavaṃ paramāṇum apaṇḍitaḥ 
tathāvayavinaṃ yuktam anyair avayavaiḥ punaḥ ।। 

ghaṭādidarśanāl lokaḥ paricchinno avasīyate 
samārambhāc ca bhāvānām ādimad brahma śāśvatam ।। 

upāyāḥ śikṣamāṇānāṃ bālānām upalāpanāḥ 
asatye vartmani sthitvā tataḥ satyaṃ samīhate ।। 

anyathā pratipadyārthaṃ padagrahaṇapūrvakam 
punar vākye tam evārtham anyathā pratipadyate ।। 

upāttā bahavo apy arthā yeṣv ante pratiṣedhanam 
kriyate te nivartante tasmāt tāṃs tatra nāśrayet ।। 

vṛkṣo nāstīti vākyaṃ ca viśiṣṭābhāvalakṣaṇam 
nārthe na buddhau saṃbandho nivṛtter avatiṣṭhate ।। 

vicchedapratipattau ca yady astīty avadhāryate 
aśabdavācyā sā buddhir nivartyeta sthitā katham ।। 

atha yaj jñānam utpannaṃ tan mithyeti nañā kṛtam 
naño vyāpārabhede asminn abhāvāvagatiḥ katham ।। 

nirādhārapravṛttau ca prākpravṛttir naño bhavet 
athādhāraḥ sa evāsya niyamārthā śrutir bhavet ।। 

niyamadyotanārthā vāpy anuvādo yathā bhavet 
kaś cid evārthavāṃs tatra śabdaḥ śeṣās tv anarthakāḥ ।। 

viruddhaṃ cābhisaṃbandham udāhāryādibhiḥ kṛtam 
vākye samāpte vākyārtham anyathā pratipadyate ।। 

stutinindāpradhāneṣu vākyeṣv artho na tādṛśaḥ 
padānāṃ pravibhāgena yādṛśaḥ parikalpyate ।। 

athāsaṃsṛṣṭa evārthaḥ padeṣu samavasthitaḥ 
vākyārthasyābhyupāyo asāv ekasya pratipādane ।। 

pūrvaṃ padeṣv asaṃsṛṣṭo yaḥ kramād upacīyate 
chinnagrathitakalpatvāt tad viśiṣṭataraṃ viduḥ ।। 

ekam āhur anekārthaṃ śabdam anye parīkṣakāḥ 
nimittabhedād ekasya sārvārthyaṃ tasya bhidyate ।। 

yaugapadyam atikramya paryāye vyavatiṣṭhate 
arthaprakaraṇābhyāṃ vā yogāc chabdāntareṇa vā ।। 

yathā sāsnādimān piṇḍo gośabdenābhidhīyate 
tathā sa eva gośabdo vāhīke api vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

sarvaśaktes tu tasyaiva śabdasyānekadharmaṇaḥ 
prasiddhibhedād gauṇatvaṃ mukhyatvaṃ copajāyate ।। 

eko mantras tathādhyātmam adhidaivam adhikratu 
asaṃkareṇa sarvārtho bhinnaśaktir avasthitaḥ ।। 

gotvānuṣaṅgo vāhīke nimittāt kaiś cid iṣyate 
arthamātraṃ viparyastaṃ śabdaḥ svārthe vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

tathā svarūpaṃ śabdānāṃ sarvārtheṣv anuṣajyate 
arthamātraṃ viparyastaṃ svarūpe tu śrutiḥ sthitā ।। 

ekatvaṃ tu sarūpatvāc chabdayor gauṇamukhyayoḥ 
prāhur atyantabhede api bhedamārgānudarśinaḥ ।। 

sāmidhenyantaraṃ caivam āvṛttāv anuṣajyate 
mantrās ca viniyogena labhante bhedam ūhavat ।। 

tāny āmnāyāntarāṇy eva paṭhyate kiṃ cid eva tu 
anarthakānāṃ pāṭho vā śeṣas tv anyaḥ pratīyate ।। 

śabdasvarūpam arthas tu pāṭhe anyair upavarṇyate 
atyantabhedaḥ sarveṣāṃ tatsaṃbandhāt tu tadvatām ।। 

anyā saṃskārasāvitrī karmaṇy anyā prayujyate 
anyā japaprabandheṣu sā tv ekaiva pratīyate ।। 

arthasvarūpe śabdānāṃ svarūpād vṛttim icchataḥ 
vākyarūpasya vākyārthe vṛttir anyānapekṣayā ।। 

anekārthatvam ekasya yaiḥ śabdasyānugamyate 
siddhyasiddhikṛtā teṣāṃ gauṇamukhyaprakalpanā ।। 

arthaprakaraṇāpekṣo yo vā śabdāntaraiḥ saha 
yuktaḥ pratyāyayaty arthaṃ taṃ gauṇam apare viduḥ ।। 

śuddhasyoccāraṇe svārthaḥ prasiddho yasya gamyate 
sa mukhya iti vijñeyo rūpamātranibandhanaḥ ।। 

yas tv anyasya prayogeṇa yatnād iva niyujyate 
tam aprasiddhaṃ manyante gauṇārthābhiniveśinam ।। 

svārthe pravartamāno api yasyārthaṃ yo avalambate 
nimittaṃ tatra mukhyaṃ syān nimittī gauṇa iṣyate ।। 

purārād iti bhinne arthe yau vartete virodhini 
arthaprakaraṇāpekṣaṃ tayor apy avadhāraṇam ।। 

vākyasyārthāt padārthānām apoddhāre prakalpite 
śabdāntareṇa saṃbandhaḥ kasyaikasyopapadyate ।। 

yac cāpy ekaṃ padaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ caritāstikriyaṃ kva cit 
tad vākyāntaram evāhur na tad anyena yujyate ।। 

yac ca ko ayam iti praśne gaur aśva iti cocyate 
praśna eva kriyā tatra prakrāntā darśanādikā ।। 

naivādhikatvaṃ dharmāṇāṃ nyūnatā vā prayojikā 
ādhikyam api manyante prasiddher nyūnatāṃ kva cit ।। 

jātiśabdo antareṇāpi jātiṃ yatra prayujyate 
saṃbandhisadṛśād dharmāt taṃ gauṇam apare viduḥ ।। 

viparyāsād ivārthasya yatrārthāntaratām iva 
manyante sa gavādis tu gauṇa ity ucyate kva cit ।। 

niyatāḥ sādhanatvena rūpaśaktisamanvitāḥ 
yathā karmasu gamyante sīrāsimusalādayaḥ ।। 

kriyāntare na caiteṣāṃ vibhavanti na śaktayaḥ 
rūpād eva tu tādarthyaṃ niyamena pratīyate ।। 

tathaiva rūpaśaktibhyām utpattyā samavasthitaḥ 
śabdo niyatatādarthyaḥ śaktyānyatra prayujyate ।। 

śrutimātreṇa yatrāsya sāmarthyam avasīyate 
taṃ mukhyam arthaṃ manyante gauṇaṃ yatnopapāditam ।। 

goyuṣmanmahatāṃ cvyarthe svārthād arthāntare sthitau 
arthāntarasya tadbhāvas tatra mukhyo api dṛśyate ।। 

mahattvaṃ śuklabhāvaṃ ca prakṛtiḥ pratipadyate 
bhedenāpekṣitā sā tu gauṇatvasya prasādhikā ।। 

agnisomādayaḥ śabdā ye svarūpapadārthakāḥ 
saṃjñibhiḥ saṃprayujyante aprasiddhes teṣu gauṇatā ।। 

agnidattas tu yo agniḥ syāt tatra svārthopasarjanaḥ 
śabdo dattārthavṛttitvād gauṇatvaṃ pratipadyate ।। 

nimittabhedāt prakrānte śabdavyutpattikarmaṇi 
hariścandrādiṣu suṭo bhāvābhāvau vyavasthitau ।। 

ṛṣyādau prāptasaṃskāro yaḥ śabdo anyena yujyate 
tatrāntaraṅgasaṃskāro bāhye arthe na nivartate ।। 

atyantaviparīto api yathā yo artho avadhāryate 
yathāsaṃpratyayaṃ śabdas tatra mukhyaḥ prayujyate ।। 

yady api pratyayādhīnam arthatattvāvadhāraṇam 
na sarvaḥ pratyayas tasmin prasiddha iva jāyate ।। 

darśanaṃ salile tulyaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇādidarśanaiḥ 
bhedāt tu sparśanādīnāṃ na jalaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇikā ।। 

yad asādhāraṇaṃ kāryaṃ prasiddhaṃ rajjusarpayoḥ 
tena bhedaparicchedas tayos tulye api darśane ।। 

prasiddhārthaviparyāsanimittaṃ yac ca dṛśyate 
yas tasmāl lakṣyate bhedas tam asatyaṃ pracakṣate ।। 

yac ca nimnonnataṃ citre sarūpaṃ parvatādibhiḥ 
na tatra pratighātādi kāryaṃ tadvat pravartate ।। 

sparśaprabandho hastena yathā cakrasya saṃtataḥ 
na tathālātacakrasya vicchinnaṃ spṛśyate hi tat ।। 

vapraprākārakalpaiś ca sparśanāvaraṇe yathā 
nagareṣu na te tadvad gandharvanagareṣv api ।। 

mṛgapaśvādibhir yāvān mukhyair arthaḥ prasādhyate 
tāvān na mṛnmayeṣv asti tasmāt te viṣayaḥ kanaḥ ।। 

mahān āvriyate deśaḥ prasiddhaiḥ parvatādibhiḥ 
alpadeśāntarāvasthaṃ pratibimbaṃ tu dṛśyate ।। 

maraṇādinimittaṃ ca yathā mukhyā viṣādayaḥ 
na te svapnādiṣu svasya tadvad arthasya sādhakāḥ ।। 

deśakālendriyagatair bhedair yad dṛśyate anyathā 
yathā prasiddhir lokasya tathā tad avasīyate ।। 

yac copaghātajaṃ jñānaṃ yac ca jñānam alaukikam 
na tābhyāṃ vyavahāro asti śabdā lokanibandhanāḥ ।। 

ghaṭādiṣu yathā dīpo yenārthena prayujyate 
tato anyasyāpi sāṃnidhyāt sa karoti prakāśanam ।। 

saṃsargiṣu tathārtheṣu śabdo yena prayujyate 
tasmāt prayojakād anyān api pratyāyayaty asau ।। 

nirmanthanaṃ yathāraṇyor agnyartham upapāditam 
dhūmam apy anabhipretaṃ janayaty ekasādhanam ।। 

tathā śabdo api kasmiṃś cit pratyāyye arthe vivakṣite 
avivakṣitam apy arthaṃ prakāśayate saṃnidheḥ ।। 

yathaivātyantasaṃsṛṣṭas tyaktum artho na śakyate 
tathā śabdo api saṃbandhī pravivaktuṃ na śakyate ।। 

arthānāṃ saṃnidhāne api sati caiṣāṃ prakāśane 
prayojako arthaḥ śabdasya rūpābhede api gamyate ।। 

kva cid guṇapradhānatvam arthānām avivakṣitam 
kva cit sāṃnidhyam apy eṣāṃ pratipattāv akāraṇam ।। 

yac cānupāttaṃ śabdena tat kasmiṃś cit pratīyate 
kva cit pradhānam evārtho bhavaty ayasya lakṣaṇam ।। 

ākhyātaṃ taddhitārthasya yat kiṃ cid upadarśakam 
guṇapradhānabhāvasya tatra dṛṣṭo viparyayaḥ ।। 

nirdeśe liṅgasaṃkhyānāṃ saṃnidhānam akāraṇam 
pramāṇam ardhahrasādāv anupāttaṃ pratīyate ।। 

hrasvasyārdhaṃ ca yad dṛṣṭaṃ tat tasyāsaṃnidhāv api 
hrasvasya lakṣaṇārthatvāt tadvad evābhidhīyate ।। 

dīrghaplutābhyāṃ tasya syān mātrayā vā viśeṣaṇam 
jāter vā lakṣaṇāya syāt sarvathā saptaparṇavat ।। 

gantavyaṃ dṛśyatāṃ sūrya iti kālasya lakṣaṇe 
jñāyatāṃ kāla ity etat sopāyam abhidhīyate ।। 

vidhyaty adhanuṣety atra viśeṣeṇa nidarśyate 
sāmānyam āśrayaḥ śakter yaḥ kaś cit pratipādakaḥ ।। 

kākebhyo rakṣyatāṃ sarpir iti bālo api coditaḥ 
upaghātapare vākye na śvādibhyo na rakṣati ।। 

prakṣālane śarāvāṇāṃ sthānanirmārjanaṃ tathā 
anuktam api rūpeṇa bhujyaṅgatvāt pratīyate ।। 

vākyāt prakaraṇād arthād aucityād deśakālataḥ 
śabdārthāḥ pravibhajyante na rūpād eva kevalāt ।। 

saṃsargo viprayogaś ca sāhacaryaṃ virodhitā 
arthaḥ prakaraṇaṃ liṅgaṃ śabdasyānyasya saṃnidhiḥ ।। 

sāmarthyam aucitī deśaḥ kālo vyaktiḥ svarādayaḥ 
śabdārthasyānavacchede viśeṣasmṛtihetavaḥ ।। 

bhedapakṣe api sārūpyād bhinnārthāḥ pratipattṛṣu 
niyatā yānty abhivyaktiṃ śabdāḥ prakaraṇādibhiḥ ।। 

nāmākhyātasarūpā ye kāryāntaranibandhanāḥ 
śabdā vākyasya teṣv artho na rūpād adhigamyate ।। 

yā pravṛttinivṛttyarthā stutinindāprakalpanā 
kuśalaḥ pratipattā tām ayathārthāṃ samīhate ।। 

vidhīyamānaṃ yat krarma dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaprayojanam 
stūyate sā stutis tasya kartur eva prayojikā ।। 

vyāghrādivyapadeśena yathā bālo nivartyate 
asatyo api tathā kaś cit pratyavāyo abhidhīyate ।। 

na saṃvidhānāṃ kṛtvāpi pratyavāye tathāvidhe 
śāstreṇa pratiṣiddhe arthe vidvān kaś cit pravartate ।। 

sarpeṣu saṃvidhāyāpi siddhair mantrauṣadhādibhiḥ 
nānyathā pratipattavyaṃ na dato gamayed iti ।। 

kva cit tattvasamākhyānaṃ kriyate stutinindayoḥ 
tatrāpi ca pravṛttiś ca nivṛttiś copadiśyate ।। 

rūpaṃ sarvapadārthānāṃ vākyārthopanibandhanam 
sāpekṣā ye tu vākyārthāḥ padārthair eva te samāḥ ।। 

vākyaṃ tad api manyante yat padaṃ caritakriyam 
antareṇa kriyāśabdaṃ vākyāder dvitvadarśanāt ।। 

ākhyātaśabde niyataṃ sādhanaṃ yatra gamyate 
tad apy ekaṃ samāptārthaṃ vākyam ity abhidhīyate ।। 

śabdavyavahitā buddhir aprayuktapadāśrayā 
anumānaṃ tadarthasya pratyaye hetur ucyate ।। 
[this verse is only in rau] 
apare tu padasyaiva tam arthaṃ pratijānate 
śabdāntarābhisaṃbandham antareṇa vyavasthitam ।। 

yasminn uccarite śabde yadā yo arthaḥ pratīyate 
tam āhur arthaṃ tasyaiva nānyad arthasya lakṣaṇam ।। 

kriyārthopapadeśv evaṃ sthānināṃ gamyate kriyā 
vṛttau nirādibhiś caivaṃ krāntādyarthaḥ pratīyate ।। 

tāni śabdāntarāṇy eva paryāyā iva laukikāḥ 
arthaprakaraṇābhyāṃ tu teṣāṃ svārtho niyamyate ।। 

pratibodhābhyupāyās tu ye taṃ taṃ puruṣaṃ prati 
nāvaśyaṃ te abhisaṃbaddhāḥ śabdā jñeyena vastunā ।। 

asatyāṃ pratipattau vā mithyā vā pratipādane 
svair arthair nityasaṃbandhās te te śabdā vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

yathāprakaraṇaṃ dvāram ity asyāṃ karmaṇaḥ śrutau 
badhāna dehi vety etad upāyād avagamyate ।। 

tatra sādhanavṛttir yaḥ śabdaḥ sattvanibandhanaḥ 
na sa pradhānabhūtasya sādhyasyārthasya vācakaḥ ।। 

svārthamātraṃ prakāśyāsau sāpekṣo vinivartate 
arthas tu tasya saṃbandhī prakalpayati saṃnidhim ।। 

pārārthyasyāviśiṣṭatvān na śabdāc chabdasaṃnidhiḥ 
nārthāc chabdasya sāṃnidhyaṃ na śabdād arthasaṃnidhiḥ ।। 

naṣṭarūpam ivākhyātam ākṣiptaṃ karmavācinā 
yadi prāptaṃ pradhānatvaṃ yugapad bhāvasattvayoḥ ।। 

tais tu nāmasarūpatvam ākhyātasyāsya varṇyate 
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ vyavahāro vibhajyate ।। 

na cāpi rūpāt saṃdehe vācakatvaṃ nivartate 
ardhaṃ paśor iti yathā sāmarthyāt tad dhi kalpate ।। 

sarvaṃ sattvapadaṃ śuddhaṃ yadi bhāvanibandhanam 
saṃsarge ca vibhakto asya tasyārtho na pṛthag yadi ।। 

kriyāpradhānam ākhyātaṃ nāmnāṃ sattvapradhānatā 
catvāri padajātāni sarvam etad virudhyate ।। 

vākyasya buddhau nityatvam arthayogaṃ ca laukikam 
dṛṣṭvā catuṣṭvaṃ nāstīti vadaty audumbarāyaṇaḥ ।। 

vyāptimāṃś ca laghuś caiva vyavahāraḥ padāśrayaḥ 
loke śāstre ca kāryārthaṃ vibhāgenaiva kalpitaḥ ।। 

na loke pratipattṝṇām arthayogāt prasiddhayaḥ 
tasmād alaukiko vākyād anyaḥ kaś cin na vidyate ।। 

anyatra śrūyamāṇaiś ca liṅgair vākyaiś ca sūcitāḥ 
svārthā eva pratīyante rūpābhedād alakṣitāḥ ।। 

utsargavākye yat tyaktam aśabdam iva śabdavat 
tad bādhakeṣu vākyeṣu śrutam anyatra gamyate ।। 

brāhmaṇānāṃ śrutir dadhni prakrāntā māṭharād vinā 
māṭharas takrasaṃbandhāt tatrācaṣṭe yathārthatām ।। 

anekākhyātayoge api vākyaṃ nyāyāpavādayoḥ 
ekam eveṣyate kaiś cid bhinnarūpam iva sthitam ।। 

niyamaḥ pratiṣedhaś ca vidhiśeṣas tathā sati 
dvitīye yo lug ākhyātas taccheṣam alukaṃ viduḥ ।। 

nirākāṅkṣāṇi nirvṛttau pradhānāni parasparam 
teṣām anupakāritvāt kathaṃ syād ekavākyatā ।। 

viśeṣavidhinārthitvād vākyaśeṣo anumīyate 
vidheyavan nivartye arthe tasmāt tulyaṃ vyapekṣaṇam ।। 

saṃjñāśabdaikadeśo yas tasya lopo na vidyate 
viśiṣṭarūpā sā saṃjñā kṛtā ca na nivartate ।। 

saṃjñāntarāc ca dattāder nānyā saṃjñā pratīyate 
saṃjñinaṃ devadattākhyaṃ dattaśabdaḥ kathaṃ vadet ।। 

sarvair avayavais tulyaṃ saṃbandhaṃ samudāyavat 
ke cic chabdasvarūpāṇāṃ manyante sarvasaṃjñibhiḥ ।। 

varṇānām arthavattvaṃ tu saṃjñānāṃ saṃjñibhir bhavet 
saṃbaddho avayavaḥ saṃjñāpraviveke na kalpate ।। 

sarvasvarūpair yugapat saṃbandhe sati saṃjñinaḥ 
naikadeśasarūpebhyas tatpratyāyanasaṃbhavaḥ ।। 

ekadeśāt tu saṃghāte keṣāṃ cij jāyate smṛtiḥ 
smṛtes tu viṣayāc chabdāt saṃghātārthaḥ pratīyate ।। 

ekadeśāt smṛtir bhinne saṃghāte niyatā katham 
kathaṃ pratīyamānaḥ syāc chabdo arthasyābhidhāyakaḥ ।। 

ekadeśasarūpās tu tais tair bhedaiḥ samanvitāḥ 
anuniṣpādinaḥ śabdāḥ saṃjñāsu samavasthitāḥ ।। 

sādhāraṇatvāt saṃdhigdhāḥ sāmarthyān niyatāśrayāḥ 
teṣāṃ ye sādhavas teṣu śāstre lopādi śiṣyate ।। 

tulyāyām anuniṣpattau jye-drā-ghā ity asādhavaḥ 
na hy anvākhyāyake śāstre teṣu dattādivat smṛtiḥ ।। 

kṛtaṇatvāś ca ye śabdā nityāḥ kharaṇasādayaḥ 
ekadravyopadeśitvāt tān sādhūn saṃpracakṣate ।। 

gotrāṇy eva tu tāny āhuḥ saṃjñāśaktisamanvayāt 
nimittāpekṣaṇaṃ teṣu svārthe nāvaśyam iṣyate ।। 

vyavahārāya niyamaḥ saṃjñānāṃ saṃjñini kva cit 
nitya eva tu saṃbandho ḍitthādiṣu gavādivat ।। 

kṛtakatvād anityatvaṃ saṃbandhasyopapadyate 
saṃjñāyāṃ sā hi puruṣair yathākāmaṃ niyujyate ।। 

yathā hi pāṃsulekhānāṃ bālakair madhukrādayaḥ 
saṃjñāḥ kriyante sarvāsu saṃjñāsv eṣaiva kalpanā ।। 

vṛddhyādīnāṃ ca śāstre asmiñ chaktyavacchedalakṣaṇaḥ 
akṛtrimo hi saṃbandho viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyavat ।। 

saṃjñā svarūpam āśritya nimitte sati laukikī 
kā cit pravartate kā cin nimittāsaṃnidhāv api ।। 

śāstre api mahatī saṃjñā svarūpopanibandhanā 
anumānaṃ nimittasya saṃnidhāne pratīyate ।। 

āvṛtter anumānaṃ vā sārūpyāt tatra gamyate 
śabdabhedānumānaṃ vā śaktibhedasya vā gatiḥ ।। 

kva cid viṣayabhedena kṛtrimā vyavatiṣṭhate 
saṃkhyāyām ekaviṣayaṃ vyavasthānaṃ dvayor api ।। 

viṣayaṃ kṛtrimasyāpi laukikaḥ kva cid uccaran 
vyāpnoti dūrāt saṃbuddhau tathā hi grahaṇaṃ dvayoḥ ।। 

saṅghaikaśeṣadvandveṣu ke cit sāmarthyalakṣaṇam 
pratyāśrayam avasthānaṃ kriyāṇāṃ pratijānate ।। 

bhojanaṃ phalarūpābhyām ekaikasmin samāpyate 
anyathā hi vyavasthāne na tadarthaḥ prakalpyate ।। 

annādānādi rūpāṃ ca sarve tṛptiphalāṃ bhujim 
pratyekaṃ pratipadyante na tu nāṭyakriyām iva ।। 

pādyavat sā vibhāgena sāmarthyād avatiṣṭhate 
bhujiḥ karoti bhujyarthaṃ na tantreṇa pradīpavat ।। 

dṛśyādis tu kriyaikāpi tathābhūteṣu karmasu 
āvṛttim antareṇāpi samudāyāśrayā bhavet ।। 

bhinnavyāpārarūpāṇāṃ vyavahārādidarśane 
kartṝṇāṃ darśanaṃ bhinnaṃ saṃbhūyārthasya sādhakam ।। 

lakṣyasya lokasiddhatvāc chāstre liṅgasya darśanāt 
arthiṣv ādaikṣu bhedena vṛddhisaṃjñā samāpyate ।। 

śatādānapradhānatvād daṇḍane śatakarmake 
arthināṃ guṇabhede api saṃkhyeyo artho na bhidyate ।। 

saṅghasyaiva vidheyatvāt kāryavat pratipādane 
tatra tantreṇa saṃbandhaḥ samāsābhyastasaṃjñayoḥ ।। 

lakṣaṇārthā śrutir yeṣāṃ kāṃ cid eva kriyāṃ prati 
tair vyastaiś ca samastaiś ca sa dharma upalakṣyate ।। 

vṛṣalair na praveṣṭavyam ity etasmin gṛhe yathā 
pratyekaṃ saṃhatānāṃ ca praveśaḥ pratiṣidhyate ।। 

saṃbhūya tv arthalipsādipratiṣedhopadeśane 
pṛthag apratiṣiddhatvāt pravṛttir na virudhyate ।। 

vyavāyalakṣaṇārthātvād aṭkupvāṅādibhis tathā 
pratyekaṃ vā samastair vā ṇatvaṃ na pratiṣidhyate ।। 

anugrahārthā bhoktṝṇāṃ bhujir ārabhyate yadā 
deśakālādyabhedena nānugṛhṇāti tān asau ।। 

pātrādibhedān nānātvaṃ yasyaikasyopadiśyate 
viparyaye vā bhinnasya tasyaikatvaṃ prakalpyate ।। 

saṃhatyāpi ca kurvāṇā bhedena pratipāditāḥ 
svaṃ svaṃ bhojyaṃ vibhāgena prāptaṃ saṃbhūya bhuñjate ।। 

vīpsāyā viṣayābhāvād virodhād anyasaṃkhyayā 
dvidhā samāptyayogāc ca śatam saṅghe avatiṣṭhate ।। 

bhujir dvandvaikaśeṣābhyāṃ yatrānyaiḥ saha śiṣyate 
tatrāpi lakṣaṇārthatvād dvidhā vākyaṃ samāpyate ।। 

vākyāntarāṇāṃ pratyekaṃ samāptiḥ kaiś cid iṣyate 
rūpāntareṇa yuktānāṃ vākyanāṃ tena saṃgrahaḥ ।। 

na vākyasyābhidheyāni bhedavākyāni kāni cit 
tasmiṃs tūccarite bhedāṃs tathānyān pratipadyate ।। 

yeṣāṃ samasto vākyārthaḥ pratibhedaṃ samāpyate 
teṣāṃ tadānīṃ bhinnasya kiṃ padārthasya sattayā ।। 

atha tair eva janitaḥ so artho bhinneṣu vartate 
pūrvasyārthasya tena syād virodhaḥ saha vā sthitiḥ ।। 

sahasthitau virodhitvaṃ syād viśiṣṭāviśiṣṭayoḥ 
vyabhicārī tu saṃbandhas tyāge arthasya prasajyate ।। 

ekaḥ sādhāraṇo vācyaḥ pratiśabdam avasthitaḥ 
saṅghe saṅghiṣu cārthātmā samnidhānanideśakaḥ ।। 

yathā sādhāraṇe svatvaṃ tyāgasya ca phalaṃ dhane 
prītiś cāvikalā tadvat saṃbandho arthena tadvatām ।। 

varṇānām arthavattāyāṃ tenaivārthena tadvati 
samudāye na caikatvaṃ bhedena vyavatiṣṭhate ।। 

ekenaiva pradīpena sarve sādhāraṇaṃ dhanam 
paśyanti tadvad ekena supā saṃkhyābhidhīyate ।। 

nārthavattā pade varṇe vākye caivaṃ viśiṣyate 
abhyāsāt prakramo anyas tu viruddha iva dṛśyate ।। 

viniyogād ṛte śabdo na svārthasya prakāśakaḥ 
arthābhidhānasaṃbandham uktidvāraṃ pracakṣate ।। 

yathā praṇihitaṃ cakṣur darśanāyopakalpate 
tathābhisaṃhitaḥ śabdo bhavaty arthasya vācakaḥ ।। 

kriyāvyavetaḥ saṃbandho dṛṣṭaḥ karaṇakarmabhiḥ 
abhidhāniyamas tasmād abhidhānābhidheyayoḥ ।। 

bahuṣv ekābhidhāneṣu sarveṣv ekārthakāriṣu 
yat prayoktābhisaṃdhatte śabdas tatrāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

āmnāyaśabdān abhyāse ke cid āhur anarthakān 
svarūpamātravṛttīṃś ca pareṣāṃ pratipādane ।। 

abhidhānakriyāyogād arthasya pratipādakān 
niyogabhedān manyante tān evaikatvadarśinaḥ ।। 

teṣām atyantanānātvaṃ nānātvavyavahāriṇaḥ 
akṣādīnām iva prāhur ekajātisamanvayāt ।। 

prayogād abhisaṃdhānam anyad eṣu na vidyate 
viṣaye yataśaktitvāt sa tu tatra vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

nānātvasyaiva saṃjñānam arthaprakaraṇādibhiḥ 
na jātv arthāntare vṛttir anyārthānāṃ kathaṃ cana ।। 

padarūpam ca yad vākyam astitvopanibandhanam 
kāmaṃ vimarśas tatrāyaṃ na vākyāvayave pade ।। 

yathaivānarthakair varṇair viśiṣṭo artho abhidhīyate 
padair anarthakair evaṃ viśiṣṭo artho abhidhīyate ।। 

yad antarāle jñānaṃ tu padārtheṣūpajāyate 
pratipatter upāyo asau prakramānavadhāraṇāt ।। 

pūrvair arthair anugato yathārthātmā paraḥ paraḥ 
saṃsarga eva prakrāntas tathānyeṣv arthavastuṣu ।। 

aṅgīkṛte tu keṣāṃ cit sādhyenārthena sādhane 
ārādhaniyamārthaiva sādhanānāṃ punaḥ śrutiḥ ।। 

ādhāre niyamābhāvāt tadākṣepo na vidyate 
sāmarthyāt saṃbhavas tasya śrutis tv anyanivṛttaye ।। 

kriyā kriyāntarād bhinnā niyatādhārasādhanā 
prakrāntā pratipattṝṇāṃ bhedāḥ saṃbodhahetavaḥ ।। 

avibhāgaṃ tu śabdebhyaḥ kramavadbhyo apadakramam 
prakāśate tadanyeṣāṃ vākyaṃ vākyārtha eva ca ।। 

svarūpaṃ vidyate yasya tasyātmā na nirūpyate 
nāsti yasya svarūpaṃ tu tasyaivātmā nirūpyate ।। 

aśabdam apare arthasya rūpanirdhāraṇaṃ viduḥ 
arthāvabhāsarūpā ca śabdebhyo jāyate smṛtiḥ ।। 

anyathaivāgnisaṃbandhād dāhaṃ dagdho abhimanyate 
anyathā dāhaśabdena dāhārthaḥ saṃpratīyate ।। 

pṛthaṅniviṣṭatattvānāṃ pṛthagarthānupātinām 
indriyāṇāṃ yathā kāryam ṛte dehān na kalpate ।। 

tathā padānāṃ sarveṣāṃ pṛthagarthaniveśinām 
vākyebhyaḥ pravibhaktānām arthavattā na vidyate ।। 

saṃsargarūpaṃ saṃsṛṣṭeṣv arthavastuṣu gṛhyate 
nātropākhyāyate tattvam apadārthasya darśanāt ।। 

darśanasyāpi yat satyaṃ na tathā darśanaṃ sthitam 
vastu saṃsargarūpeṇa tad arūpaṃ nirūpyate ।। 

astitvenānuṣakto vā nivṛttyātmani vā sthitaḥ 
artho abhidhīyate yasmād ato vākyaṃ prayujyate ।। 

kriyānuṣaṅgeṇa vinā na padārthaḥ pratīyate 
satyo vā viparīto vā vyavahāre na so asty ataḥ ।। 

sad ity etat tu yad vākyaṃ tad abhūd asti neti vā 
kriyābhidhānasaṃbandham antareṇa na gamyate ।। 

ākhyātapadavācye arthe sādhanopanibandhane 
vinā sattvābhidhānena nākāṅkṣā vinivartate ।। 

prādhānyāt tu kriyā pūrvam arthasya pravibhajyate 
sādhyaprayuktāny aṅgāni phalaṃ tasya prayojakam ।। 

prayoktaivābhisaṃdhatte sādhyasādhanarūpatām 
arthasya cābhisaṃbandhakalpanāṃ prasamīhate ।। 

pacikriyāṃ karotīti karmatvenābhidhīyate 
paktiḥ karaṇarūpaṃ tu sādhyatvena pratīyate ।। 

yo aṃśo yenopakāreṇa prayoktṝṇāṃ vivakṣitaḥ 
arthasya sarvaśaktitvāt sa tathaiva vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

ārādvṛttiṣu saṃbandhaḥ kadā cid abhidhīyate 
āśliṣṭo yo anupaśliṣṭaḥ sa kadā cit pratīyate ।। 

saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ vibhaktatvaṃ saṃsargaś ca vivekinām 
nānātmakānām ekatvaṃ nānātvaṃ ca viparyaye ।। 

sarvātmakatvād arthasya nairātmyād vā vyavasthitam 
atyantayataśaktitvāc chabda eva nibandhanam ।। 

vastūpalakṣaṇaḥ śabdo nopakārasya vācakaḥ 
na svaśaktiḥ padārthānāṃ saṃspraṣṭuṃ tena śakyate ।। 

saṃbandhidharmā saṃyogaḥ svaśabdenābhidhīyate 
saṃbandhaḥ samavāyas tu saṃbandhitvena gamyate ।। 

lakṣaṇād vyavatiṣṭhante padārthā na tu vastutaḥ 
upakārāt sa evārthaḥ kathaṃ cid anugamyate ।। 

vākyārtho yo abhisaṃbandho na tasyātmā kva cit sthitaḥ 
vyavahāre padārthānāṃ tam ātmānaṃ pracakṣate ।। 

padārthe samudāye vā samāpto naiva vā kva cit 
padārtharūpabhedena tasyātmā pravibhajyate ।। 

anvākhyānāya yo bhedaḥ pratipattinibandhanam 
sākāṅkṣāvayavaṃ bhede tenānyad upavarṇyate ।। 

anekaśakter ekasya pravibhāgo anugamyate 
ekārthatvaṃ hi vākyasya mātrayāpi pratīyate ।। 

saṃpratyayārthād bāhyo arthaḥ sann asan vā vibhajyate 
bāhyīkṛtya vibhāgas tu śaktyapoddhāralakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

pratyayārthātmaniyatāḥ śaktayo na vyavasthitāḥ 
anyatra ca tato rūpaṃ na tāsām upalabhyate ।। 

bahuśv api tiṅanteṣu sākāṅkṣeṣv ekavākyatā 
tiṅā tiṅbhyo nighātasya paryudāsas tathārthavān ।। 

ekatiṅ yasya vākyaṃ tu śāstre niyatalakṣaṇam 
tasyātiṅgrahaṇenārtho vākyabhedān na vidyate ।। 

tiṅantāntarayukteṣu yuktayukteṣu vā punaḥ 
mṛgaḥ paśyata yātīti bhedābhedau na tiṣṭhataḥ ।। 

itikartavyatārthasya sāmarthyād yatra kāṅkṣyate 
aśabdalakṣaṇākāṅkṣaṃ samāptārthaṃ tad ucyate ।। 

tattvānvākhyānamātre tu yāvān artho anuṣajyate 
vināpi tatprayogeṇa śruter vākyaṃ samāpyate ।। 

ciṅkramyamāṇo adhīṣvātra japaṃś caṅkramaṇaṃ kuru 
tādarthyasyāviśeṣe api śabdād bhedaḥ pratīyate ।। 

phalavantaḥ kriyābhedāḥ kriyāntaranibandhanāḥ 
asaṃkhyātāḥ kramoddeśair ekākhyātanidarśitāḥ ।। 

nivṛtabhedā sarvaiva kriyākhyāte abhidhīyate 
śruter aśakyā bhedānāṃ pravibhāgaprakalpanā ।। 

aśvamedhena yakṣyante rājānaḥ sattram āsate 
brāhmaṇā iti nākhyātarūpād bhedaḥ pratīyate ।। 

sakṛc chrutā saptadaśasv anāvṛttāpi yā kriyā 
prajāpatyeṣu sāmarthyāt sā bhedaṃ pratipadyate ।। 

devadattādiṣu bhujiḥ pratyekam avatiṣṭhate 
pratisvatantraṃ vākyaṃ vā bhedena pratipadyate ।। 

uccāraṇe tu vākyānām anyad rūpaṃ na gṛhyate 
pratipattau tu bhinnānām anyad rūpaṃ pratīyate ।। 

ekaṃ grahaṇavākyaṃ ca sāmānyenābhidhīyate 
kartarīti yathā tac ca paśvādiṣu vibhajyate ।। 

yadi ākāṅkṣā nivarteta tadbhūtasya sakṛc chrutau 
naivānyenābhisaṃbandhaṃ tad upeyāt kathaṃ cana ।। 

ekarūpam anekārthaṃ tasmād upanibandhanam 
yonir vibhāgavākyānāṃ tebhyo ananyad iva sthitam ।। 

kva cit kriyā vyaktibhāgair upakāre pravartate 
sāmānyabhāga evāsyāḥ kva cid arthasya sādhakaḥ ।। 

kālabhinnāś ca ye bhedā ye cāpy uṣṭrāsikādiṣu 
prakrame jātibhāgasya śabdātmā tair na bhidyate ।। 

ekasaṃkhyeṣu bhedeṣu bhinnā jātyādibhiḥ kriyāḥ 
bhedena viniyujyante tacchabdasya sakṛc chrutau ।। 

akṣādeṣu yathā bhinnā bhakṣibhañjidivikriyāḥ 
prayogakālābhede api pratibhedaṃ pṛthak sthitāḥ ।। 

akṣiṇāṃ tantriṇāṃ tantram upāyas tulyarūpatā 
eṣāṃ kramo vibhaktānāṃ tannibaddhā sakṛc chrutiḥ ।। 

dvāv apy upāyau śabdānāṃ prayoge samavasthitau 
kramo vā yaugapadyaṃ vā yau loko nātivartate ।। 

krame vibhajyate rūpaṃ yaugapadye na bhidyate 
kriyā tu yaugapadye api kramarūpānupātinī ।। 

bhedasaṃsargaśaktī dve śabdād bhinne iva sthite 
yaugapadye apy anekena prayoge bhidyate śrutiḥ ।। 

abhinno rūpabhedena ya eko artho vivakṣitaḥ 
tasyāvayavadharmeṇa samudāyo anugamyate ।। 

bhedanirvacane tv asya pratyedaṃ vā samāpyate 
śrutir vacanabhinnā vā vākyabhede avatiṣṭhate ।। 

tatraikavacanānto vā so akṣaśabdaḥ prayujyate 
pratyekaṃ vā bahutvena pravibhāgo yathāśruti ।। 

dviṣṭhāni yāni vākyāni teṣv apy ekatvadarśinām 
anekaśakter ekasya svaśaktiḥ pravibhajyate ।। 

atyantabhinnayor vā syāt prayoge tantralakṣaṇaḥ 
upāyas tatra saṃsargaḥ pratipattṛṣu bhidyate ।। 

bhedenādhigatau pūrvaṃ śabdau tulyaśrutī punaḥ 
tantreṇa pratipattāraḥ prayoktrā pratipāditāḥ ।। 

ekasyāpi vivakṣāyām anuniṣpadyate paraḥ 
vinābhisaṃdhinā śabdaḥ śaktirūpaḥ prakāśate ।। 

anekā śaktir ekasya yugapac chrūyate kva cit 
agniḥ prakāśadāhābhyām ekatrāpi niyujyate ।। 

āvṛttiśaktibhinnārthe vākye sakṛd api śrute 
liṅgād vā tantradharmād vā vibhāgo vyavatiṣṭhate ।। 

saṃprasāraṇasaṃjñāyāṃ liṅgābhyāṃ varṇavākyayoḥ 
pravibhāgas tathā sūtra ekasminn eva jāyate ।। 

tathā dvirvacane acīti tantropāyād alakṣaṇaḥ 
ekaśeṣeṇa nirdeśo bhāṣya eva pradarśitaḥ ।। 

prāyeṇa saṃkṣeparucīn alpavidyāparigrahān 
saṃprāpya vaiyākaraṇān saṃgrahe astam upāgate ।। 

kṛte atha pātañjalinā guruṇā tīrthadarśinā 
sarvesaṃ nyāyabījānāṃ mahābhāṣye nibandhane ।। 

alabdhagādhe gāmbhīryād uttāna iva sauṣṭhavāt 
tasminn akṛtabuddhīnām naivāvāsthita niścayaḥ ।। 

vaijisaubhavaharyakṣaiḥ śuṣkatarkānusāribhiḥ 
ārṣe viplāvite granthe saṃgrahapratikañcuke ।। 

yaḥ pātañjaliśiṣyebhyo bhraṣṭo vyākaraṇāgamaḥ 
kālena dākṣiṇātyeṣu granthamātro vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

parvatād āgamaṃ labdhvā bhāṣyabījānusāribhiḥ 
sa nīto bahuśākhatvaṃ cāndrācāryādibhiḥ punaḥ ।। 

nyāyaprasthānamārgāṃs tān abhyasya svam ca darśanam 
praṇīto guruṇāsmākam ayam āgamasaṃgrahaḥ ।। 

vartmanām atra keṣām cid vastumātram udāhṛtam 
kāṇḍe tṛtīye nyakṣena bhaviṣyati vicāraṇā ।। 

prajñā vivekaṃ labhate bhinnair āgamadarśanaiḥ 
kiyad vā śakyam unnetuṃ svatarkam anudhāvatā ।। 

tat tad utprekṣamāṇānāṃ purāṇair āgamair vinā 
anupāsitavṛddhānāṃ vidyā nātiprasīdati ।। 

jātisamuddeśa

dvidhā kaiś cit padaṃ bhinnaṃ caturdhā pañcadhāpi vā 
apoddhṛtyaiva vākyebhyaḥ prakṛtipratyayādivat ।। 

padārthānām apoddhāre jātir vā dravyam eva vā 
padārthau sarvaśabdānāṃ nityāv evopavarṇitau ।। 

keṣāṃ cit sāhacaryeṇa jātiḥ śaktyupalakṣaṇam 
khadirādiṣv aśakteṣu śaktaḥ pratinidhīyate ।। 

asvātantryaphalo bandhiḥ pramāṇādīva śiṣyate 
ato jātyabhidhāne api śaktihīnaṃ na gṛhyate ।। 

saṃśleṣamātraṃ badhnātir yadi syāt tu vivakṣitaḥ 
śaktyāśraye tato liṅgaṃ pramāṇādyanuśāsanam ।। 

svā jātiḥ prathamaṃ śabdaiḥ sarvair evābhidhīyate 
tato arthajātirūpeṣu tadadhyāropakalpanā ।। 

yathā rakte guṇe tattvaṃ kaṣāye vyapadiśyate 
saṃyogisannikarṣāc ca vastrādiṣv api gṛhyate ।। 

tathā śabdārthasaṃbandhāc chabde jātir avasthitā 
vyapadeśe arthajātīnāṃ jātikāryāya kalpate ।। 

jātiśabdaikaśeṣe sā jātīnāṃ jātir iṣyate 
śabdajātaya ity atra tajjātiḥ śabdajātiṣu ।। 

yā śabdajātiḥ śabdeṣu śabdebhyo bhinnalakṣaṇā 
jātiḥ sā śabdajātitvam avyatikramya vartate ।। 

arthajātyabhidhāne api sarve jātyabhidhāyinaḥ 
vyāpāralakṣaṇā yasmāt padārthāḥ samavasthitāḥ ।। 

jātau padārthe jātir vā viśeṣo vāpi jātivat 
śabdair apekṣyate yasmād atas te jātivācinaḥ ।। 

dravyadharmā padārthe tu dravye sarvo artha ucyate 
dravyadharmāśrayād dravyam ataḥ sarvo artha iṣyate ।। 

anupravṛttidharmo vā jātiḥ syāt sarvajātiṣu 
vyāvṛttidharmasāmānyaṃ viśeṣe jātir iṣyate ।। 

saṃyogidharmabhedena deśe ca parikalpite 
teṣu deśeṣu sāmānyam ākāśasyāpi vidyate ।। 

adeśānāṃ ghaṭādīnāṃ deśāḥ saṃbandhino yathā 
ākāśasyāpy adeśasya deśāḥ saṃbandhinas tathā ।। 

bhinnavastvāśrayā buddhiḥ saṃyogiṣv anuvartate 
samavāyiṣu bhedasya grahaṇaṃ vinivartate ।। 

ataḥ saṃyogideśānāṃ gauṇatvaṃ parikalpyate 
avivekāt pradeśebhyo mukhyatvaṃ samavāyinām ।। 

anupravṛttirūpā yā prakhyā tām ākṛtiṃ viduḥ 
ke cid vyāvṛttirūpāṃ tu dravyatvena pracakṣate ।। 

bhinnā iti paropādhir abhinnā iti vā punaḥ 
bhāvātmasu prapañco ayaṃ saṃsṛṣṭeṣv eva jāyate ।। 

naikatvaṃ nāpi nānātvaṃ na sattvam na ca nāstitā 
ātmatattveṣu bhāvānām asaṃsṛṣṭeṣu vidyate ।। 

sarvaśaktyātmabhūtatvaṃ ekasyaiveti nirṇaye 
bhāvānām ātmabhedasya kalpanā syād anarthikā ।। 

tasmād dravyādayaḥ sarvāḥ śaktayo bhinnalakṣaṇāḥ 
saṃsṛṣṭāḥ puruṣārthasya sādhikā na tu kevalāḥ ।। 

yathaiva cendriyādīnām ātmabhūtā samagratā 
tathā saṃbandhisaṃbandhasaṃsarge api pratīyate ।। 

na tad utpadyate kiṃ cid yasya jātir na vidyate 
ātmābhivyaktaye jātiḥ kāraṇānāṃ prayojikā ।। 

kāraṇeṣu padaṃ kṛtvā nityānityeṣu jātayaḥ 
kva cit kāryeṣv abhivyaktim upayānti punaḥ punaḥ ।। 

nirvarttyamānaṃ yat karma jātis tatrāpi sādhanam 
svāśrayasyābhiniṣpattyai sā kriyāṇāṃ prayojikā ।। 

vidhau vā pratiṣedhe vā brāhmaṇatvādi sādhanam 
vyaktyāśritāsritā jāteḥ saṃkhyājātir viśeṣikā ।। 

yathā jalādibhir vyaktaṃ mukham evābhidhīyate 
tathā dravyair abhivyaktā jātir evābhidhīyate ।। 

yathendriyagato bheda indriyagrahaṇād ṛte 
indriyārtheṣv adṛśyo api jñānabhedāya kalpate ।। 

tathātmarūpagrahaṇāt keṣāṃ cid vyaktayo vinā 
sāmānyajñānabhedānām upayānti nimittatām ।। 

satyāsatyau tu yau bhāgau pratibhāvaṃ vyavasthitau 
satyaṃ yat tatra sā jātir asatyā vyaktayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 

saṃbandhibhedāt sattaiva bhidyamānā gavādiṣu 
jātir ity ucyate tasyāṃ sarve śabdā vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

tāṃ prātipadikārthaṃ ca dhātvarthaṃ ca pracakṣate 
sā nityā sā mahān ātmā tām āhus tvatalādayaḥ ।। 

prāptakramā viśeṣeṣu kriyā saivābhidhīyate 
kramarūpasya saṃhāre tat sattvam iti kathyate ।। 

saiva bhāvavikāreṣu ṣaḍ avasthāḥ prapadyate 
krameṇa śaktibhiḥ svābhir evaṃ pratyavabhāsate ।। 

ātmabhūtaḥ kramo apy asyā yatredaṃ kāladarśanam 
paurvāparyādirūpeṇa pravibhaktam iva sthitam ।। 

tirobhāvābhyupagame bhāvānāṃ saiva nāstitā 
labdhakrame tirobhāve naśyatīti pratīyate ।। 

pūrvasmāt pracyutā dharmād aprāptā cottaraṃ padam 
tadantarāle bhedānām āśrayāj janma kathyate ।। 

āśrayaḥ svātmamātrā vā bhāvā vā vyatirekinaḥ 
svaśaktayo vā sattāyā bhedadarśanahetavaḥ ।। 

pṛthivyādiṣv abhivyaktau na saṃsthānam apekṣate 
anucchinnāśrayāj jātir anitye apy āśraye sthitā ।। 

anucchedyāśrayām eke sarvāṃ jātiṃ pracakṣate 
na yaugapadyaṃ pralaye sarvasyeti vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

prakṛtau pravilīneṣu bhedeṣv ekatvadarśinām 
dravyasattvaṃ prapadyante svāśrayā eva jātayaḥ ।। 

brāhmaṇatvādayo bhāvāḥ sarvaprāṇiṣv avasthitāḥ 
abhivyaktāḥ svakāryāṇāṃ sādhakā ity api smṛtiḥ ।। 

citrādiṣv apy abhivyaktir jātīnāṃ kaiścid iṣyate 
prāṇyāśritās tu tāḥ prāptau nimittaṃ puṇyapāpayoḥ ।। 

jñānaṃ tv asmad viśiṣṭānāṃ tāsu sarvendriyam viduḥ 
ābhyāsān maṇirūpyādiviśeṣeṣv iva tadvidām ।। 

jātyutpalādigandhādau bhedatattvaṃ yad āśritam 
tad bhāvapratyayair loke anityatvān nābhidhīyate ।। 

asvaśabdābhidhānās tu narasiṃhādijātayaḥ 
sarūpāvayavevānyā tāsu śrutir avasthitā ।। 

jātyavasthāparicchede saṃkhyā saṃkhyātvam eva vā 
viprakarṣe api saṃsargād upakārāya kalpate ।। 

lakṣaṇā śabdasaṃskāre vyāpāraḥ kāryasiddhaye 
saṃkhyākarmādiśaktīnāṃ śrutisāmye api dṛśyate ।। 

na vinā saṃkhyayā kaś cit sattvabhūto artha ucyate 
ataḥ sarvasya nirdeśe saṃkhyā syād avivakṣitā ।। 

ekatvaṃ vā bahutvaṃ vā keṣāṃ cid avivakṣitam 
tad dhi jātyabhidhānāya dvitvaṃ tu syād vivakṣitam ।। 

yady etau vyādhitau syātāṃ deyaṃ syād idam auṣadham 
ity evaṃ lakṣaṇe arthasya dvitvaṃ syād avivakṣitam ।। 

ekādiśabdavācyāyāḥ karmasv aṅgatvam iṣyate 
saṃkhyāyāḥ khanati dvābhyām iti rūpād dhi sāśritā ।। 

yajeta paśunety atra saṃskārasyāpi saṃbhave 
yathā jātis tathaikatvaṃ sādhanatvena gamyate ।। 

liṅgāt tu syāt dvitīyādes tad ekatvaṃ vivakṣitam 
ekārthaviṣayatve ca tal liṅgaṃ jātisaṃkhyayoḥ ।। 

anyatrāvihitasyaiva sa vidhiḥ prathamaṃ paśoḥ 
kriyāyām aṅgabhāvaś ca tat tv etasmād vivakṣitam ।। 

grahās tv anyatra vihitā bhinnasaṃkhyāḥ pṛthak pṛthak 
prājāpatyā navety evamādibhedasamanvitāḥ ।। 

aṅgatvena pratītānāṃ saṃmārge tv aṅgināṃ punaḥ 
nirdeśaṃ prati yā saṃkhyā sā kathaṃ syād vivakṣitā ।। 

nānyatra vidhir astīti saṃskāro nāpi cāṅgitā 
hetuḥ saṃkhyāvivakṣāyā yatnāt sā hi vivakṣitā ।। 

saṃmārjane viśeṣaś ca na grahe kva cid āśritaḥ 
vihitās te ca saṃskāryāḥ sarveṣām āśrayas tataḥ ।। 

pratyāśrayaṃ samāptāyāṃ jātāv ekena cet kriyā 
paśunā na prakalpeta tat syād eva prakalpanam ।। 

ekena ca prasiddhāyāṃ kriyāyāṃ yadi saṃbhavāt 
paśvantaram upādeyam upādānam anarthakam ।। 

yathaivāhitagarbhāyāṃ garbhādhānām anarthakam 
tathaikena prasiddhāyāṃ paśvantaram anarthakam ।। 

tāvatārthasya siddhatvād ekatvasyāvyatikramam 
ke cid icchanti na tv atra saṃkhyāṅgatvena gṛhyate ।। 

dvitīyādi tu yal liṅgam uktanyāyānuvādi tat 
na saṃkhyā sādhanatvena jātivat tena gamyate ।। 

anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ saṃkhyābhyupagame sati 
yuktaṃ yat sādhanatvaṃ syān na tv anyārthopalakṣaṇaṃ ।। 

sādhanatve padārthasya sāmarthyaṃ na prahīyate 
saṃkhyāvyāpāradharmo atas tena liṅgena gamyate ।। 

apūrvasya vidheyatvāt prādhānyam avasīyate 
vihitasya parārthatvāc cheśabhāvaḥ pratīyate ।। 

saṃmārgasya vidheyatvāt anyatra vihite grahe 
vidhivākye śrutā saṃkhyā lakṣaṇāyāṃ na bādhyate ।। 

vidhivākyāntare saṃkhyā paśor nāsti virodhinī 
tasmāt saguṇa evāsau sahaikatvena gamyate ।। 

nirjñātadravyasaṃbandhe yaḥ karmaṇy upadiśyate 
gunas tenārthitā tasya dravyeṇeva pratīyate ।। 

kaścid eva guṇo dravye yathā sāmarthyalakṣaṇaḥ 
ādhāro api guṇasyaivaṃ prāptaḥ sāmarthyalakṣaṇaḥ ।। 

tayos tu pṛthagarthitve saṃbandho yaḥ pratīyate 
na tasminn upaghāto asti kalpyam anyan na cāśrutam ।। 

kriyayā yo abhisaṃbandhaḥ sa śrutiprāpitas tayoḥ 
āśrayāśrayiṇor vākyān niyamas tv avatiṣṭhate ।। 

tatra dravyaguṇābhāve pratyekaṃ syād vikalpanam 
śrutiprāpto hi saṃbandho balavān vākyalakṣaṇāt ।। 

yadā tu jātiḥ śaktir vā kriyāṃ praty upadiśyate 
sāmarthyāt saṃnidhīyete tatra dravyaguṇau tadā ।। 

jātīnāṃ ca guṇānāṃ ca tulye aṅgatve kriyāṃ prati 
guṇāḥ pratinidhīyante chāgādīnāṃ na jātayaḥ ।। 

vyaktiśakteḥ samāsannā jātayo na tathā guṇāḥ 
sākṣād dravyaṃ kriyāyogi guṇas tasmād vikalpate ।। 

sāmyenānyatarābhāve vikalpaḥ kaiścid iṣyate 
atadguṇo ataś chāgaḥ syān meṣo vā tadguṇo bhavet ।। 

jāter āśritasaṃkhyāyāḥ pravṛttir upalabhyate 
saṃkhyāviśeṣam utsṛjya kvacit saiva pravartate ।। 

parāṅgabhūtaṃ sāmānyaṃ yujyate dravyasaṃkhyayā 
svārthaṃ pravartamānaṃ tu na saṃkhyām avalambate ।। 

yajeta paśunety atra yajyarthāyāṃ paśuśrutau 
kṛtārthaikena paśunā pradhānaṃ bhavati kriyā ।। 

yāvatāṃ saṃbhavo yasya sa kuryāt tāvatāṃ yadi 
ālambhanaṃ guṇais tena pradhānaṃ syāt prayojitam ।। 

saṃmṛjyamānatantre tu grahe yatra kriyāśrutiḥ 
saṃkhyāviśeṣagrahaṇaṃ naiva tatrādriyāmahe ।। 

śiṣyamāṇapare vākye yad ekagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam 
śeṣe viśiṣṭasaṃkhye api vyaktaṃ tal liṅgadarśanam ।। 

samāsapratyayavidhau yathā nipatitā śrutiḥ 
guṇānāṃ paratantrāṇāṃ nyāyenaivopapadyate ।। 

guṇe api nāṅgīkriyate pradhānāntarasiddhaye 
saṃkhyā kartā tathā karmaṇy aviśiṣṭaḥ pratīyate ।। 

yasyānyasya prasaktasya niyamārthā punaḥ śrutiḥ 
nivṛttau caritārthatvāt saṃkhyā tatrāvivakṣitā ।। 

sarūpasamudāyāt tu vibhaktir yā vidhīyate 
ekas tatrārthavān siddhaḥ samudāyasya vācakaḥ ।। 

pratyayasya pradhānasya samāsasyāpi vā vidhau 
siddhaḥ saṃkhyāvivakṣāyāṃ sarvathānugraho guṇe ।। 

abhedarūpaṃ sādṛśyam ātmabhūtāś ca śaktayaḥ 
jātiparyāyavācitvam eṣām apy upavarṇyate ।। 

daṇḍopāditsayā daṇḍaṃ yady api pratipadyate 
na tasmād eva sāmarthyāt sa daṇḍīti pratīyate ।। 

necchānimittād icchāvān iti jñānam pravartate 
tasmāt saty api sāmarthye buddhir arthāntarāśrayā ।। 

svabhāvo vyapadeśyo vā sāmarthyaṃ vāvatiṣṭhate 
sarvasyānte yatas tasmād vyavahāro na kalpate ।। 

yadā bhedān parityajya buddhyaika iva gṛhyate 
vyaktyātmaiva tadā tatra buddhir ekā pravartate ।। 

bhedarūpair anusyūtaṃ yadaikam iva manyate 
samūhāvagrahā buddhir bahubhyo jāyate tadā ।। 

yadā sahavivakṣāyām ekabuddhinibandhanaḥ 
baddhāvayavavicchedaḥ samudāyo abhidhīyate ।। 

pratikriyaṃ samāptatvād eko bhedasamanvitaḥ 
dvandve dvitvādibhedena tadāsāv upagamyate ।। 

sakṛtpravṛttāv ekatvam āvṛttau sadṛśātmatām 
bhinnātmakānāṃ vyaktīnāṃ bhedāpohāt prapadyate ।। 

anupravṛtteti yathābhinnā buddhiḥ pratīyate 
artho vyāvṛttarūpo api tathā tattvena gṛhyate ।। 

sarūpāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ na bhedopanipātinaḥ 
vidyante vācakāḥ śabdā nāpi bhedo avadhāryate ।। 

jñānaśabdārthaviṣayā viśeṣā ye vyavasthitāḥ 
teṣāṃ duravadhāratvāj jñānādyekatvadarśanam ।। 

jñāneṣv api yathārtheṣu tathā sarveṣu jātayaḥ 
saṃsargadarśane santi tāś cārthasya prasādhikāḥ ।। 

jñeyastham eva sāmānyaṃ jñānānām upakārakam 
na jātu jñeyavaj jñānaṃ pararūpeṇa rūpyate ।। 

yathā jyotiḥ prakāśena nānyenābhiprakāśyate 
jñānākāras tathānyena na jñānenopagṛhyate ।। 

na cātmasamavetasya sāmānyasyāvadhāraṇe 
jñānaśaktiḥ samarthā syāj jñātasyānyasya vastunaḥ ।। 

ayaugapadye jñānānām asyety agrahaṇaṃ na ca 
yathopalabdhi smaraṇam upalabdhe ca jāyate ।। 

ghaṭajñānam iti jñānaṃ ghaṭajñānavilakṣaṇam 
ghaṭa ity api yaj jñānaṃ viṣayopanipāti tat ।। 

yato viṣayarūpeṇa jñānarūpaṃ na gṛhyate 
artharūpaviviktaṃ ca svarūpaṃ nāvadhāryate ।। 
dravyasamuddeśaḥ 
ātmā vastu svabhāvaś ca śarīraṃ tattvam ity api 
dravyam ity asya paryāyās tac ca nityam iti smṛtam ।। 

satyaṃ vastu tadākārair asatyair avadhāryate 
asatyopādhibhiḥ śabdaiḥ satyam evābhidhīyate ।। 

adhruveṇa nimittena devadattagṛhaṃ yathā 
gṛhītaṃ gṛhaśabdena śuddham evābhidhīyate ।। 

suvarṇādi yathā yuktam svair ākārair apāyibhiḥ 
rucakādyabhidhānānāṃ śuddham evaiti vācyatām ।। 

ākāraiś ca vyavacchedāt sārvārthyam avarudhyate 
yathaiva cakṣurādīnāṃ sāmarthyaṃ nālikādibhiḥ ।। 

teṣv ākāreṣu yaḥ śabdas tathābhūteṣu vartate 
tattvātmakatvāt tenāpi nityam evābhidhīyate ।। 

na tattvātattvayor bheda iti vṛddhebhya āgamaḥ 
atattvam iti manyante tattvam evāvicāritam ।। 

vikalparūpaṃ bhajate tattvam evāvikalpitam 
na cātra kālabhedo asti kālabhedaś cagṛhyate ।। 

yathā viṣayadharmāṇāṃ jñāne atyantam asaṃbhavaḥ 
tadātmeva ca tat siddham atyantam atadātmakam ।। 

tathā vikārarūpāṇāṃ tattve atyantam asaṃbhavaḥ 
tadātmeva ca tat tattvam atyamntam atadātmakam ।। 

satyam ākṛtisaṃhāre yad ante vyavatiṣṭhate 
tan nityaṃ śabdavācyaṃ tac chabdāt tac ca na bhidyate ।। 

na tad asti na tan nāsti na tad ekaṃ na tat pṛthak 
na saṃsṛṣṭaṃ vibhaktaṃ vā vikṛtaṃ na ca nānyathā ।। 

tan nāsti vidyate tac ca tad ekaṃ tat pṛthak pṛthak 
saṃsṛṣṭaṃ ca vibhaktaṃ ca vikṛtaṃ tat tad anyathā ।। 

tasya śabdārthasaṃbandharūpam ekasya dṛśyate 
tad dṛśyaṃ darśanaṃ draṣṭā darśane ca prayojanam ।। 

vikārāpagame satyaṃ suvarṇaṃ kuṇḍale yathā 
vikārāpagame satyāṃ tathāhuḥ prakṛtiṃ parām ।। 

vācyā sā sarvaśabdānāṃ śabdāś ca na pṛthak tataḥ 
apṛthaktve ca saṃbandhas tayor nānātmanor iva ।। 

ātmā paraḥ priyo dveṣyo vaktā vācyaṃ prayojanam 
viruddhāni yathaikasya svapne rūpāṇi cetasaḥ ।। 

ajanmani tathā nitye paurvāparyavivarjite 
tattve janmādirūpatvaṃ viruddham upalabhyate ।। 
saṃbandhasamuddeśa 
jñānaṃ prayoktur bāhyo arthaḥ svarūpaṃ ca pratīyate 
śabdair uccaritais teṣāṃ saṃbandhaḥ samavasthitaḥ ।। 

pratipattur bhavaty arthe jñāne vā saṃśayaḥ kvacit 
svarūpeṣūpalabhyeṣu vyabhicāro na vidyate ।। 

asyāyaṃ vācako vācya iti ṣaṣṭhyā pratīyate 
yogaḥ śabdārthayos tattvam apy ato vyapadiśyate ।। 

nābhidhānaṃ svadharmeṇa saṃbandhasyāsti vācakam 
atyantaparatantratvād rūpaṃ nāsyāpadiśyate ।। 

upakārāt sa yatrāsti dharmas tatrānugamyate 
śaktīnām api sā śaktir guṇānām apy asau guṇaḥ ।। 

taddharmaṇos tu tācchabdyaṃ saṃyogasamavāyayoḥ 
tayor apy upakārārthā niyatās tadupādhayaḥ ।। 

kā cid eva hi sāvasthā kāryaprasavasūcitā 
kasya cit kena cid yasyāṃ saṃyoga upajāyate ।। 

nirātmakānām utpattau niyamaḥ kvacid eva yaḥ 
tenaivāvyapavargaś ca prāptabhede sa yatkṛtaḥ ।। 

ātmāntarasya yenātmā tadātmevāvadhāryate 
yataś caikatvanānātvaṃ tattvaṃ nādhyavasīyate ।। 

tāṃ śaktiṃ samavāyākhyāṃ śaktīnām upakāriṇīm 
hedābhedāv atikrāntām anyathaiva vyavasthitām ।। 

dharmaṃ sarvapadārthānām atītaḥ sarvalakṣaṇaḥ 
anugṛhṇāti saṃbandha iti pūrvebhya āgamaḥ ।। 

padārthīkṛta evānyaiḥ sarvatrābhyupagamyate 
saṃbandhas tena śabdārthaḥ pravibhaktuṃ na śakyate ।। 

samavāyāt sva ādhāraḥ svā ca jātiḥ pratīyate 
ekārthasamavāyāt tu guṇāḥ svādhāra eva ye ।। 

dravyatvasattāsaṃyogāḥ svānyādhāropabandhanāḥ 
tatpradeśavibhāgāś ca guṇā dvitvādayaś ca ye ।। 

ke cit svāśrayasaṃyuktāḥ ke cit tatsamavāyinaḥ 
saṃyuktasamaveteṣu samavetās tathāpare ।। 

svāśrayeṇa tu saṃyuktaiḥ saṃyuktaṃ vibhu gamyate 
samavāyasya saṃbandho nāparas tatra dṛśyate ।। 

saṃbandhasyāviśiṣṭatvān na cātra niyamo bhavet 
tasmācchabdārthayor naivaṃ saṃbandhaḥ parikalpyate ।।
