adṛṣṭavṛttilābhena yathā saṃyoga ātmanaḥ 
kva cit svasvāmiyogākhyo abhede anyatrāpi sa kramaḥ ।। 

prāptiṃ tu samavāyākhyāṃ vācyadharmātivartinīm 
prayoktā pratipattā vā na śabdair anugacchati ।। 

avācyam iti yad vācyaṃ tad avācyatayā yadā 
vācyam ityavasīyeta vācyam eva tadā bhavet ।। 

athāpy avācyam ity evaṃ, na tad vācyaṃ pratīyate 
vivakṣitāsya yāvasthā saiva nādhyavasīyate ।। 

tathānyathā sarvathā ca yasyāvācyatvam ucyate 
tatrāpi naiva sāvasthā taiḥ śabdaiḥ pratiṣidhyate ।। 

na hi saṃśayarūpe arthe śeṣatvena vyavasthite 
avyudāse svarūpasya saṃśayo anyaḥ pravartate ।। 

yadā ca nirṇayajñāne nirṇayatvena nirṇayaḥ 
prakramyate tadā jñānaṃ svadharme nāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

sarvaṃ mithyā bravīmīti naitad vākyaṃ vivakṣyate 
tasya mithyābhidhāne hi prakrānto artho na gamyate ।। 

na ca vācakarūpeṇa pravṛttasyāsti vācyatā 
pratipādyaṃ na tat tatra yenānyat pratipādyate ।। 

asādhikā pratijñeti neyam evābhidhīyate 
yathā, tathāsya dharmo api nātra kaścit pratīyate ।। 

vyāpārasyāparo yasmān na vyāpāro asti kaścana 
virodham anavasthāṃ vā tasmāt sarvatra nāśrayet ।। 

indriyāṇāṃ svaviṣayeṣv anādir yogyatā yathā 
anādir arthaiḥ śabdānāṃ saṃbandho yogyatā tathā ।। 

asādhur anumānena vācakaḥ kaiścid iṣyate 
vācakatvāviśeṣe vā niyamaḥ puṇyapāpayoḥ ।। 

saṃbandhaśabde saṃbandho yogyatāñṃ prati yogyatā 
samayād yogyatāsaṃvin mātāputrādiyogavat ।। 

śabdaḥ kāraṇam arthasya sa hi tenopajanyate 
tathā ca buddhiviṣayād arthāc chabdaḥ pratīyate ।। 

bhojanādy api manyante buddhyarthe yad asaṃbhavi 
buddhyarthād eva buddhyarthe jāte tad api dṛśyate ।। 

anityeṣv api nityatvam abhidheyātmanā sthitam 
anityatvaṃ svaśaktir vā sā ca nityān na bhidyate ।। 

śabdenārthasya saṃskāro dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaprayojanaḥ 
kriyate so abhisaṃbandham antareṇa kathaṃ bhavet ।। 

nāvaśyam abhidheyeṣu saṃskāraḥ sa tathāvidhaḥ 
dṛsyate na ca saṃbandhas tathābhūto vivakṣitaḥ ।। 

sati pratyayahetutvaṃ saṃbandha upapadyate 
śabdasyārthe yatas tatra saṃbandho astīti gamyate ।। 

nitye anitye api vāpy arthe puruṣeṇa kathaṃcana 
saṃbandho akṛtasaṃbandhaiḥ śabdaiḥ kartuṃ na śakyate ।। 

vyapadeśe padārthānām anyā sattaupacārikī 
sarvāvasthāsu sarveṣām ātmarūpasya darśikā ।। 

sphaṭikādi yathā dravyaṃ bhinnarūpair upāśrayaiḥ 
svaśaktiyogāt saṃbandhaṃ tādrūpyeṇeva gacchati ।। 

tadvac chabdo api sattāyām asyāṃ pūrvaṃ vyavasthitaḥ 
dharmair upaiti saṃbandham avirodhivirodhibhiḥ ।। 

evaṃ ca pratiṣedhyeṣu pratiṣedhaprakḷptaye 
āśriteṣūpacāreṇa pratiṣedhaḥ pravartate ।। 

ātmalābhasya janmākhyā satā labhyaṃ ca labhyate 
yadi saj jāyate kasmād athāsaj jāyate katham ।। 

sato hi gantur gamanaṃ, sati gamye pravartate 
gantṛvac cen na janmārtho, na cet tadvan na jāyate ।। 

upacarya tu kartāram abhidhānapravṛttaye 
punaś ca karmabhāvena tāṃ kriyāṃ ca tadāśrayām ।। 

athopacārasattaivaṃ vidheyas tatra lādayaḥ 
janmanā tu virodhitvān mukhyā sattā na vidyate ।। 

ātmānam ātmanā bibhrad astīti vyapadiśyate 
antarbhāvāc ca tenāsau karmaṇā na sakarmakaḥ ।। 

prāk ca sattābhisaṃbandhān mukhyā sattā kathaṃ bhavet 
asaṃś ca nāsteḥ kartā syād upacāras tu pūrvavat ।। 

tasmād bhinneṣu dharmeṣu virodhiṣv avirodhinīm 
virodhikhyāpanāyaiva śabdais tais tair upāśritām ।। 

abhinnakālām artheṣu bhinnakāleṣv avasthitām 
pravṛttihetuṃ sarveṣāṃ śabdānām aupacārikīm ।। 

etāṃ sattāṃ padārtho hi na kaś cid ativartate 
sā ca saṃpratisattāyāḥ pṛthag bhāśye nidarśitā ।। 

pradeśasyaikadeśaṃ vā parato vā nirūpaṇam 
viparyayam abhāvaṃ vā vyavahāro anuvartate ।। 

yathendriyasya vaiguṇyān mātrādhyāropavān iva 
jāyate pratyayo arthebhyas tathaivoddeśajā matiḥ ।। 

akṛtsnaviṣayābhāsaṃ śabdaḥ pratyayam āśritaḥ 
artham āhānyarūpeṇa svarūpeṇānirūpitam ।। 

rūpaṇavyapadeśābhyāṃ laukike vartmani sthitau 
jñānaṃ praty abhilāpaṃ ca sadṛśau bālapaṇḍitau ।। 

sarvārtharūpatā śuddhir jñānasya nirupāśrayā 
tato apy asya parāṃ śuddhim eke prāhur arūpikām ।। 

upaplavo hi jñānasya bāhyākārānupātitā 
kāluṣyam iva tat tasya saṃsarge vyatibhedajam ।। 

yathā ca jñānam ālekhād aśuddhau vyavatiṣṭhate 
tathopāśrayavān arthaḥ svarūpād viprakṛṣyate ।। 

evam arthasya śabdasya jñānasya ca viparyaye 
bhāvābhāvāv abhedena vyavahārānupātinau ।। 

yathā bhāvam upāśritya tadabhāvo anugamyate 
tathābhāvam upāśritya tadbhāvo apy anugamyate ।। 

nābhāvo jāyate bhāvo naiti bhāvo anupākhyatām 
ekasmād ātmano ananyau bhāvābhāvau vikalpitau ।। 

abhāvasyānupākhyatvāt kāraṇaṃ na prasādhakam 
sopākhyasya tu bhāvasya kāraṇaṃ kiṃ kariśyati ।। 

tasmāt sarvam abhāvo vā bhāvo vā sarvam iṣyate 
na tv avasthāntaraṃ kiṃ cid ekasmāt satyataḥ sthitam ।। 

tasmān nābhāvam icchanti ye loke bhāvavādinaḥ 
abhāvavādino vāpi na bhāvaṃ tattvalakṣaṇam ।। 

advaye caiva sarvasmin svabhāvād ekalakṣaṇe 
parikalpeṣu maryādā vicitraivopalabhyate ।। 

catasro hi yathāvasthā nirupākhye prakalpitāḥ 
evaṃ dvaividhyam apy etad bhāvābhāvavyapāśrayam ।। 

avirodhī virodhī vā sann asan vāpi yuktitaḥ 
kramavān akramo vāpi nābhāva upapadyate ।। 

avirodhī virodhī vā sann asan vāpi tattvataḥ 
kramavān akramo vāpi tena bhāvo na vidyate ।। 

abhāve triṣu kāleṣu na bhedasyāsti saṃbhavaḥ 
tasminn asati bhāve api traikālyaṃ nāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

ātmatattvaparityāgaḥ parato nopapadyate 
ātmatattvaṃ tu parataḥ svato vā nopakalpate ।। 

tattve virodho nānātva upakāro na kaś cana 
tattvānyatvaparityāge vyavahāro nivartate ।। 

yatra draṣṭā ca dṛśyaṃ ca darśanaṃ cāvikalpitam 
tasyaivārthasya satyatvaṃ śritās trayyantavedinaḥ ।। 

sāmānyaṃ vā viśeṣaṃ vā yasmād āhur viśeṣavat 
śabdās tasmād asatyeṣu bhedeṣv eva vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

na hy abhāvasya sadbhāve bhāvasyātmā prahīyate 
na cābhāvasya nāstitve bhāvasyātmā prasūyate ।। 

na śābaleyasyāstitvaṃ bāhuleyasya bādhakam 
na śābaleyo nāstīti bāhuleyaḥ prakalpate ।। 

abhāvo yadi vastu syāt tatreyaṃ syāt vicāraṇā 
tataś ca tadabhāve api syād vicāryam idaṃ punaḥ ।। 

avastu syād atītaṃ yad vyavahārasya gocaram 
tatra vastugato bhedo na nirvacanam arhati ।। 

apade arthe padanyāsaḥ kāraṇasya na vidyate 
atha ca prāgasadbhāvaḥ kāraṇe sati dṛṣyate ।। 

kā tasya prāgavastheti vastvāśritam idaṃ punaḥ 
prāg avastheti na hy etad dvayam apy asty avastuni ।। 

na cordhvam asti nāstīti vacanāyānibandhanam 
alaṃ syād apadasthānam etad vācaḥ pracakṣate ।। 

atyadbhutā tv iyaṃ vṛttir yad abhāgaṃ yad akramam 
bhāvānāṃ prāg abhūtānām ātmatattvaṃ prakāśate ।। 

vikalpotthāpitenaiva sarvo bhāvena laukikaḥ 
mukhyeneva padārthena vyavahāro vidhīyate ।। 

bhāvaśaktim ataś caināṃ manyante nityavādinaḥ 
bhāvam eva kramam prāhur na bhāvād aparaḥ kramaḥ ।। 

kramān na yaugapadyasya kaś cid bhedo asti tattvataḥ 
yathaiva bhāvān nābhāvaḥ kaś cid anyo avasīyate ।। 

kālasyāpy aparaṃ kālaṃ nirdiśanty eva laukikāḥ 
na ca nirdeśamātreṇa vyatireko anugamyate ।। 

ādhāraṃ kalpayan buddhyā nābhāve vyavatiṣṭhate 
avastuṣv api notprekṣā kasya cit pratibadhyate ।। 

tasmāc chaktivibhāgena nityaḥ sadasadātmakaḥ 
eko arthaḥ śabdavācyatve bahurūpaḥ prakāśate ।। 

vyavahāraś ca lokasya padārthaiḥ parikalpitaiḥ 
śāstre padārthaḥ kāryārthaṃ laukikaḥ pravibhajyate ।। 
bhūyodravyasamuddeśaḥ 
saṃsargarūpāt saṃbhūtāḥ saṃvidrūpād apoddhṛtāḥ 
śāstre vibhaktā vākyārthāt prakṛtipratyayārthavat ।। 

nimittabhūtāḥ sādhutve śāstrād anumitātmakāḥ 
ke cit padārthā vakṣyante saṃkśepeṇa yathāgamam ।। 

vastūpalakṣaṇaṃ yatra sarvanāma prayujyate 
dravyam ity ucyate so arto bhedyatvena vivakśitaḥ ।। 
guṇasamudeśa 
saṃsargi bhedakaṃ yad yat savyāpāraṃ pratīyate 
guṇatvaṃ paratantratvāt tasya śāstra udāhṛtam ।। 

dravyasyāvyapadeśasya ya upādīyate guṇaḥ 
bhedako vyapadeśāya tatprakarṣo abhidhīyate ।। 

sarvasyaiva pradhānasya na vinā bhedahetunā 
prakarṣo vidyate nāpi aśabdasyopaiti vācyatām ।। 

vidyamānāḥ pradhāneṣu na sarve bhedahetavaḥ 
viśeṣaśabdair ucyante vyāvṛttārthābhidhāyibhiḥ ।। 

vastūpalakṣaṇe tatra viśeṣo vyāpṛto yadi 
prakarṣo niyamābhāvāt syād avijñātahetukaḥ ।। 

sarvaṃ ca sarvato avaśyaṃ niyamena prakṛṣyate 
saṃsargiṇā nimittena nikṛṣṭenādhikena vā ।। 

nāpekṣate nimittaṃ ca prakarṣe vyāpṛtaṃ yadi 
dravyasya syād upādānaṃ prakarṣaṃ praty anarthakaṃ ।। 

savyāpāro guṇas tasmāt svaprakarṣanibandhanaḥ 
dravyātmānaṃ bhinatty eva svaprakarṣaṃ niveśayan ।। 

arūpaṃ pararūpeṇa dravyam ākhyāyate yathā 
aprakarṣaṃ prakarṣeṇa guṇasyāviśyate tathā ।। 
diksamuddeśa 
dik sādhanam kriyā kāla iti vastvabhidhāyinaḥ 
śaktirūpe padārthānām atyantam anavasthitāḥ ।। 

vyatirekasya yo hetur avadhipratipādyayoḥ 
ṛjv ity evam yato anyena vinā buddhiḥ pravartate ।। 

karmano jātibhedānām abhivyaktir yadāśrayā 
sā svair upādhibhir bhinnā śaktir dig iti kathyate ।। 

parāparatve mūrtināṃ deśabhedanibandhane 
tata eva prakalpete kramarūpe tu kālataḥ ।। 

ākāśasya pradeśena bhāgaiś cānyaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak 
sā saṃyogavibhāgānām upādhitvāya kalpate ।। 

diśo vyavasthā deśānāṃ digvyavasthā na vidyate 
śaktayaḥ khalu bhāvānām upakāraprabhāvitāḥ ।। 

pratyastarūpā bhāveṣu dik pūrvety abhidhīyate 
pūrvabuddhir yato dik sā samākhyāmātram anyathā ।। 

svāṅgād vyavasthā yā loke na tasyām niyatā diśaḥ 
pratyaṅmukhasya yat paścāt tat purastād viparyaye ।। 

deśavyavasthāniyamo dikṣu na vyavatiṣṭhate 
rūḍham apy aparatvena pūrvam ity abhidhīyate ।। 

ato bhāṣitapuṃskatvāt puṃvadbhāvo na sidhyati 
asminn arthe na śabdena prasavaḥ kva cid ucyate ।। 

dikśakter abhidhāne tu niyataṃ diśi darśanam 
pūrvādināṃ yathā ṣaṣṭer jīvitasyāvadhāraṇe ।। 

chāyābhābhyāṃ nagādīnām bhāgabhedaḥ prakalpate 
ataddharmasu bhāveṣu bhāgabhedo na kalpate ।। 

paramāṇor abhāgasya diśā bhāgo vidhīyate 
bhāgaprakalpanāśaktiṃ prathamāṃ tāṃ pracakṣate ।। 

adeśāś cāpy abhāgāś ca niṣkramā nirupāśrayāḥ 
bhāvāḥ saṃsargirūpāt tu śaktibhedaḥ prakalpate ।। 

nirbhāgātmakatā tulyā paramāṇor ghaṭasya ca 
bhāgaḥ śaktyantaraṃ tatra parimāṇaṃ ca yat tayoḥ ।। 

yataḥ prakalpate bhedo bhedas tatrāpi dṛśyate 
adṛṣṭoparatiṃ bhedam ato ayuktataraṃ viduḥ ।। 

sarvatra tasya kāryasya darśanād vibhur iṣyate 
vibhutvam etad evāhur anyaḥ kāyavatāṃ vidhiḥ ।। 

caitanyavat sthitā loke dikkālaparikalpanā 
prakṛtiṃ prāṇināṃ tāṃ hi ko anyathā sthāpayiṣyati ।। 

saṃkaro vyavahārāṇāṃ prakṛteḥ syād viparyaye 
tasmāt tyajann imān bhāvān punar evāvalambate ।। 

tasyās tu śakteḥ pūrvādibhedo bhāvāntarāśrayaḥ 
bhinnā dik tena bhedena bhedāyaivopakalpate ।। 

avadhitvena cāpekṣāyoge diglakṣaṇo vidhiḥ 
pūrvam asyeti ṣaṣṭhy eva dṛṣṭā dharmāntarāśraye ।। 

pūrvādināṃ viparyāso adṛṣṭaś cāvadhyasaṃkare 
ṛjv etad asyety etac ca liṅgaṃ na vyatikīryate ।। 

antaḥkaraṇadharmo vā bahir evaṃ prakāśate 
asyāṃ tv antarbahirbhāvaḥ prakriyāyāṃ na vidyate ।। 

ekatvam āsāṃ śaktīnāṃ nānātvaṃ veti kalpane 
avastupatite jñātvā satyato na parāmṛśet ।। 

vikalpātītatattveṣu saṃketopanibandhanāḥ 
bhāveṣu vyavahārā ye lokas tatrānugamyate ।। 

naikatvam asty anānātvaṃ vinaikatvena netarat 
paramārthe tayor eṣa bhedo atyantaṃ na vidyate ।। 

na śaktīnāṃ tathā bhedo yathā śaktimatām sthitiḥ 
na ca laukikam ekatvaṃ tāsām ātmasu vidyate ।। 

naikatvaṃ vyavatiṣṭheta nānātvaṃ cen na kalpayet 
nānātvaṃ cāvahīyeta yady ekatvaṃ na kalpayet ।। 
sādhanasamuddeśa 
svāśraye samavetānāṃ tadvad evāśrayāntare 
kriyāṇām abhiniṣpattau sāmarthyaṃ sādhanaṃ viduḥ ।। 

śaktimātrāsamūhasya viśvasyānekadharmaṇaḥ 
sarvadā sarvathā bhāvāt kva cit kiṃ cid vivakṣyate ।। 

sādhanavyavahāraś ca buddhyavasthānibandhanaḥ 
sann asan vārtharūpeṣu bhedo buddhyā prakalpyate ।। 

buddhyā samīhitaikatvān pañcālān kurubhir yadā 
punar vibhajate vaktā tadāpāyaḥ pratīyate ।। 

śabdopahitarūpāṃś ca buddher viṣayatāṃ gatān 
pratyakṣam iva kaṃsādīn sādhanatvena manyate ।। 

buddhipravṛttirūpaṃ ca samāropyābhidhātṛbhiḥ 
artheṣu śaktibhedānāṃ kriyate parikalpanā ।। 

vyaktau padārthe śabdāder janyamānasya karmaṇaḥ 
sādhanatvaṃ tathā siddhaṃ buddhirūpaprakalpitam ।। 

svatantraparatantratve kramarūpaṃ ca darśitam 
nirīheṣv api bhāveṣu kalpanopanibandhanam ।। 

śaktayaḥ śaktimantaś ca sarve saṃsargavādinām 
bhāvās teṣv asvaśabdeṣu sādhanatvaṃ nirūpyate ।। 

ghaṭasya dṛśikarmatve mahattvādīni sādhanam 
rūpasya dṛśikarmatve rūpatvādīni sādhanam ।। 

svaiḥ sāmānyaviśeṣaiś ca śaktimanto rasādayaḥ 
niyatagrahaṇā loke śaktayas tās tathāśrayaiḥ ।। 

indriyārthamanaḥkartṛsaṃbandhaḥ sādhanaṃ kva cit 
yad yadā yadanugrāhi tat tadā tatra sādhanam ।। 

svaśabdair abhidhāne tu sa dharmo nābhidhīyate 
vibhaktyādibhir evāsāv upakāraḥ pratīyate ।। 

nimittabhāvo bhāvānām upakārārtham āśritaḥ 
natir āvarjanety evaṃ siddhaḥ sādhanam iṣyate ।। 

sa tebhyo vyatirikto vā teṣām ātmaiva vā tathā 
vyatirekam upāśritya sādhanatvena kalpyate ।। 

saṃdarśanaṃ prārthanāyāṃ vyavasāye tv anantarā 
vyavasāyas tathārambhe sādhanatvāya kalpate ।। 

pūrvasmin yā kriyā saiva parasmin sādhanaṃ matā 
saṃdarśane tu caitanyaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ viduḥ ।। 

niṣpattimātre kartṛtvaṃ sarvatraivāsti kārake 
vyāpārabhedāpekṣāyāṃ karaṇatvādisaṃbhavaḥ ।। 

putrasya janmani yathā pitroḥ kartṛtvam ucyate 
ayam asyām iyaṃ tv asmād iti bhedo vivakṣayā ।। 

guṇakriyāṇāṃ kartāraḥ kartrā nyakkṛtaśaktayaḥ 
nyaktāyām api saṃpūrṇaiḥ svair vyāpāraiḥ samanvitāḥ ।। 

karaṇatvādibhir jñātāḥ kriyābhedānupātibhiḥ 
svātantryam uttaraṃ labdhvā pradhāne yānti kartṛtām ।। 

yathā rājñā niyukteṣu yoddhṛtvaṃ yoddhṛṣu sthitam 
teṣu vṛttau tu labhate rājā jayaparājayau ।। 

tathā kartrā niyukteṣu sarveṣv ekārthakāriṣu 
kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvāder uttaraṃ na virudhyate ।। 

anāśrite tu vyāpāre nimittaṃ hetur iṣyate 
āśritāvadhibhāvaṃ tu lakṣaṇe lakṣaṇaṃ viduḥ ।। 

dravyādiviṣayo hetuḥ kārakaṃ niyatakriyam 
kartā kartrantarāpekṣaḥ kriyāyāṃ hetur iṣyate ।। 

kriyāyai karaṇaṃ tasya dṛṣṭaḥ pratinidhis tathā 
hetvarthā tu kriyā tasmān na sa pratinidhīyate ।। 

prātilomyānulomyābhyāṃ hetur arthasya sādhakaḥ 
tādarthyam ānulomyena hetutvānugataṃ tu tat ।। 

sarvatra sahajā śaktir yāvaddravyam avasthitā 
kriyākāle tv abhivyakter āśrayād upakāriṇī ।। 

kuḍyasyāvaraṇe śaktir asyādīnāṃ vidāraṇe 
sarvadā sa tu san dharmaḥ kriyākāle nirūpyate ।। 

svā"ngasaṃyoginaḥ pāśā daityānāṃ vāruṇā yathā 
vyajyante vijigīṣūṇāṃ dravyāṇāṃ śaktayas tathā ।। 

taikṣṇyagauravakāṭhinyasaṃsthānaiḥ svair asir yadā 
chedyaṃ prati vyāpriyate śaktimān gṛhyate tadā ।। 

prā"n nimittāntarodbhūtaṃ kriyāyāḥ kaiś cid iṣyate 
sādhanaṃ sahajaṃ kaiś cit kriyānyaiḥ pūrvam iṣyate ।। 

pravṛttir eva prathamaṃ kva cid apy anapāśritā 
śaktīr ekādhikaraṇe srotovad apakarṣati ।। 

apūrvaṃ kālaśaktiṃ vā kriyāṃ vā kālam eva vā 
tam evamlaksanam bhāvam ke cid āhuh katham ca na ।। 

nityāḥ ṣaṭ śaktayo aanyeṣāṃ bhedābhedasamanvitāḥ 
kriyāsaṃsiddhaye artheṣu jātivat samavasthitāḥ ।। 

dravyākārādibhedena tāś cāparimitā iva 
dṛśyante tattvam āsāṃ tu ṣaṭ śaktīr nātivartate ।। 

nimittabhedād ekaiva bhinnā śaktiḥ pratīyate 
ṣoḍhā kartṛtvam evāhus tatpravṛtter nibandhanam ।। 

tattve vā vyatireke vā vyatiriktaṃ tad ucyate 
śabdapramāṇako lokaḥ sa śāstreṇānugamyate ।। 

paramārthe tu naikatvaṃ pṛthaktvād bhinnalakṣaṇam 
pṛthaktvaikatvarūpeṇa tattvam eva prakāśate ।। 

yat pṛthaktvam asaṃdigdhaṃ tad ekatvān na bhidyate 
yad ekatvam asaṃdigdhaṃ tat pṛthaktvān na bhidyate ।। 

dyauḥ kṣamā vāyur ādityaḥ sāgarāḥ sarito diśaḥ 
antaḥkaraṇatattvasya bhāgā bahir avasthitāḥ ।। 

kālavicchedarūpeṇa tad evaikam avasthitam 
sa hy apūrvāparo bhāvaḥ kramarūpeṇa lakṣyate ।। 

dṛṣṭo hy avyatireke api vyatireko anvaye asati 
vṛkṣādyarthānvayas tasmād vibhaktyartho anya iṣyate ।। 

sāmānyaṃ kārakaṃ tasya saptādyā bhedayonayaḥ 
ṣaṭ karmākhyādibhedena śeṣabhedas tu saptamī ।। 
[atha karmādhikāraḥ] 
nirvartyaṃ ca vikāryaṃ ca prāpyaṃ ceti tridhā matam 
tatrepsitatamaṃ karma caturdhānyat tu kalpitam ।। 

audāsīnyena yat prāpyaṃ yac ca kartur anīpsitam 
saṃjñāntarair anākhyātaṃ yad yac cāpy anyapūrvakam ।। 

satī vāvidyamānā vā prakṛtiḥ pariṇāminī 
yasya nāśriyate tasya nirvartyatvaṃ pracakṣate ।। 

prakṛtes tu vivakṣāyāṃ vikāryaṃ kaiś cid anyathā 
nirvartyaṃ ca vikāryaṃ ca karma śāstre pradarśitam ।। 

yad asaj jāyate sad vā janmanā yat prakāśyate 
tan nirvartyaṃ vikāryaṃ ca karma dvedhā vyavasthitam ।। 

prakṛtyucchedasaṃbhūtaṃ kiṃ cit kāṣṭhādibhasmavat 
kiṃ cid guṇāntarotpattyā suvarṇādivikāravat ।। 

kriyākṛtā viśeṣāṇāṃ siddhir yatra na gamyate 
darśanād anumānād vā tat prāpyam iti kathyate ।। 

viśeṣalābhaḥ sarvatra vidyate darśanādibhiḥ 
keṣāṃ cit tadabhivyaktisiddhir dṛṣṭiviṣādiṣu ।। 

ābhāsopagamo vyaktiḥ soḍhatvam iti karmaṇaḥ 
viśeṣāḥ prāpyamāṇasya kriyāsiddhau vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

nirvartyādiṣu tat pūrvam anubhūya svatantratām 
kartrantarāṇāṃ vyāpāre karma saṃpadyate tataḥ ।। 

tadvyāpāraviveke api svavyāpāre vyavasthitam 
karmāpadiṣṭāṃllabhate kva cic chāstrāśrayān vidhīn ।। 

nivṛttapreṣaṇaṃ karma svakriyāvayave sthitam 
nivartamāne karmatve sve kartṛtve avatiṣṭhate ।। 

tāni dhātvantarāṇy eva pacisidhyativad viduḥ 
bhede api tulyarūpatvād ekatvaparikalpanā ।। 

ekadeśe samūhe ca vyāpārāṇāṃ pacādayaḥ 
svabhāvataḥ pravartante tulyarūpasamanvitāḥ ।। 

nyagbhāvanā nyagbhavanaṃ ruhau śuddhe pratīyate 
nyagbhāvanā nyagbhavanaṃ ṇyante api pratipadyate ।। 

avasthāṃ pañcamīm āhur ṇyante tāṃ karmakartari 
nivṛttapreṣaṇād dhātoḥ prākṛte arthe ṇij ucyate ।। 

bravīti pacater arthaṃ sidhyatir na vinā ṇicā 
sa ṇyantaḥ pacater arthe prākṛte vyavatiṣṭhate ।। 

keṣāṃ cid devadattāder vyāpāro yaḥ sakarmake 
sa vinā devadattādeḥ kaṭādiṣu vivakṣyate ।। 

nivṛttapreṣaṇaṃ karma svasya kartuḥ prayojakam 
preṣaṇāntarasaṃbandhe ṇyante lenābhidhīyate ।। 

sadṛśādiṣu yat karmakartṛtvaṃ pratipadyate 
āpattyāpādane tatra viṣayatvaṃ prati kriye ।। 

kutaś cid āhṛtya padam evaṃ ca parikalpane 
karmasthabhāvakatvaṃ syād darśanādyabhidhāyinām ।। 

viśeṣadarśanaṃ yatra kriyā tatra vyavasthitā 
kriyāvyavasthā tv anyeṣāṃ śabdair eva prakāśyate ।। 

kālabhāvādhvadeśānām antarbhūtakriyāntaraiḥ 
sarvair akarmakair yoge karmatvam upajāyate ।। 

ādhāratvam iva prāptās te punar dravyakarmasu 
kālādayo bhinnakakṣyaṃ yānti karmatvam uttaram ।। 

atas taiḥ karmabhir dhātur yukto adravyair akarmakaḥ 
lasya karmaṇi bhāve ca nimittatvāya kalpate ।। 

sarvaṃ cākathitaṃ karma bhinnakakṣyaṃ pratīyate 
dhātvarthoddeśabhedena tan nepsitatamaṃ kila ।। 

pradhānakarma kathitaṃ yat kriyāyāḥ prayojakam 
tatsiddhaye kriyāyuktam anyat tv akathitaṃ smṛtam ।। 

duhyādivan nayatyādau karmatvam akathāśrayam 
ākhyātānupayoge tu niyamāc cheṣa iṣyate ।। 

antarbhūtaṇijarthānāṃ duhyādīnāṃ ṇijantavat 
siddhaṃ pūrveṇa karmatvaṃ ṇijantaniyamas tathā ।। 

karaṇasya svakakṣyāyāṃ na prakarṣāśrayo yathā 
karmaṇo api svakakṣyāyāṃ na syād atiśayas tathā ।। 

karmaṇas tv āptum iṣṭatva āśrite atiśayo yataḥ 
āśrīyate tato atyantaṃ bhedaḥ pūrveṇa karmaṇā ।। 

ṇijante ca yathā kartā sakriyaḥ san prayujyate 
na duhyādau tathā kartā niṣkriyo api prayujyate ।। 

bhedavākyaṃ tu yan ṇyante nīduhiprakṛtau ca yat 
śabdāntaratvān naivāsti saṃsparśas tasya dhātunā ।। 

yathaivaikam apādānaṃ śāstre bhedena darśitam 
tathaikam eva karmāpi bhedena pratipāditam ।। 

nirvartyo vā vikāryo vā prāpyo vā sādhanāśrayaḥ 
kriyāṇām eva sādhyatvāt siddharūpo abhidhīyate ।। 

ahiteṣu yathā laulyāt kartur icchopajāyate 
viṣādiṣu bhayādibhyas tathaivāsau pravartate ।। 

pradhānetarayor yatra dravyasya kriyayoḥ pṛthak 
śaktir guṇāśrayā tatra pradhānam anurudhyate ।। 

pradhānaviṣayā śaktiḥ pratyayenābhidhīyate 
yadā guṇe tadā tadvad anuktāpi prakāśate ।। 

pacāv anuktaṃ yat karma ktvānte bhāvābhidhāyini 
bhujau śaktyantare apy ukte tat taddharma prakāśate ।। 

iṣeś ca gamisaṃsparśād grāme yo lo vidhīyate 
tatreṣiṇaiva nirbhogaḥ kriyate gamikarmaṇaḥ ।। 

paktvā bhujyata ity atra keṣāṃ cin na vyapekṣate 
odanaṃ pacatiḥ so asāv anumānāt pratīyate ।। 

tathābhiniviśau karma yat ti"nante abhidhīyate 
ktvānte adhikaraṇatve api na tatrecchanti saptamīm ।। 

yan nirvṛttāśrayaṃ karma prāpter apracitaṃ punaḥ 
bhakṣyādiviṣayāpattyā bhidyamānaṃ tad īpsitam ।। 

dhātor arthāntare vṛtter dhātvarthenopasaṃgrahāt 
prasiddher avivakṣātaḥ karmaṇo akarmikā kriyā ।। 

bhedā ya ete catvāraḥ sāmānyena pradarśitāḥ 
te nimittādibhedena bhidyante bahudhā punaḥ ।। 
[iti karmādhikāraḥ] [atha karaṇādhikāraḥ] 
kriyāyāḥ pariniṣpattir yadvyāpārād anantaram 
vivakṣyate yadā tatra karaṇatvaṃ tadā smṛtam ।। 

vastutas tad anirdeśyaṃ na hi vastu vyavasthitam 
sthālyā pacyata ity eṣā vivakṣā dṛśyate yataḥ ।। 

karaṇeṣu tu saṃskāram ārabhante punaḥ punaḥ 
viniyogaviśeṣāṃś ca pradhānasya prasiddhaye ।। 

svakakṣyāsu prakarṣaś ca karaṇānāṃ na vidyate 
āśritātiśayatvaṃ tu paratas tatra lakṣaṇam ।। 

svātantrye api prayoktāra ārād evopakurvate 
karaṇena hi sarveṣāṃ vyāpāro vyavadhīyate ।। 

kriyāsiddhau prakarṣo ayaṃ nyagbhāvas tv eva kartari 
siddhau satyāṃ hi sāmānyaṃ sādhakatvaṃ prakṛṣyate ।। 

asyādīnāṃ tu kartṛtve taikṣṇyādi karaṇaṃ viduḥ 
taikṣṇyādīnāṃ svatantratve dvedhātmā vyavatiṣṭhate ।। 

ātmabhede api saty evam eko arthaḥ sa tathā sthitaḥ 
tadāśrayatvād bhede api kartṛtvaṃ bādhakaṃ tataḥ ।। 

yathā ca saṃnidhānena karaṇatvaṃ pratīyate 
tathaivāsaṃnidhāne api kriyāsiddheḥ pratīyate ।। 

stokasya vābhinirvṛtter anirvṛtteś ca tasya vā 
prasiddhiṃ karaṇatvasya stokādīnāṃ pracakṣate ।। 

dharmāṇāṃ tadvatā bhedād abhedāc ca viśiṣyate 
kriyāvadher avacchedaviśeṣād bhidyate yathā ।। 
[iti karaṇādhikāraḥ] [atha kartradhikāraḥ] 
prāg anyataḥ śaktilābhān nyagbhāvāpādanād api 
tadadhīnapravṛttitvāt pravṛttānāṃ nivartanāt ।। 

adṛṣṭatvāt pratinidheḥ praviveke ca darśanāt 
ārād apy upakāritve svātantryaṃ kartur ucyate ।। 

dharmair abhyuditaiḥ śabde niyamo na tu vastuni 
kartṛdharmavivakṣāyāṃ śabdāt kartā pratīyate ।। 

ekasya buddhyavasthābhir bhede ca parikalpite 
kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ ca karmatvaṃ copajāyate ।। 

utpatteḥ prāg asadbhāvo buddhyavasthānibandhanaḥ 
aviśiṣṭaḥ satānyena kartā bhavati janmanaḥ ।। @

kāraṇaṃ kāryabhāvena yadā vāvyavatiṣṭhate 
kāryaśabdaṃ tadā labdhvā kāryatvenopajāyate ।। 

yathāheḥ kuṇḍalībhāvo vyagrāṇāṃ vā samagratā 
tathaiva janmarūpatvaṃ satām eke pracakṣate ।। 

vibhaktayoni yat kāryaṃ kāraṇebhyaḥ pravartate 
svā jātir vyaktirūpeṇa tasyāpi vyavatiṣṭhate ।। 

bhāveṣv eva padanyāsaḥ prajñāyā vāca eva vā 
nāstīty apy apade nāsti na ca sad bhidyate tataḥ ।। 

buddhiśabdau pravartete yathābhūteṣu vastuṣu 
teṣām anyena tattvena vyavahāro na vidyate ।। 

ākāśasya yathā bhedaś chāyāyāś calanaṃ yathā 
janmanāśāv abhede api tathā kaiś cit prakalpitau ।। 

yathaivākāśanāstitvam asan mūrtinirūpitam 
tathaiva mūrtināstitvam asadākāśaniśrayam ।। 

yathā tadarthair vyāpāraiḥ kriyātmā vyapadiśyate 
abhedagrahaṇād eṣa kāryakāraṇayoḥ kramaḥ ।। 

vikāro janmanaḥ kartā prakṛtir veti saṃśaye 
bhidyate pratipattṛṇāṃ darśanaṃ li"ngadarśanaiḥ ।। 

kḷpi saṃpadyamāne yā caturthī sā vikārataḥ 
suvarṇapiṇḍe prakṛtau vacanaṃ kuṇḍalāśrayam ।। 

vākye saṃpadyateḥ kartā sa"nghaś cvyantasya kathyate 
vṛttau saṅghībhavantīti brāhmaṇānāṃ svatantratā ।। 

atvaṃ saṃpadyate yas tvaṃ na tasmin yuṣmadāśrayā 
pravṛttiḥ puruṣasyāsti prākṛtaḥ sa vidhīyate ।। 

pūrvāvasthām avijahat saṃspṛśan dharmam uttaram 
saṃmūrchita ivārthātmā jāyamāno abhidhīyate ।। 

savyāpārataraḥ kaś cit kva cid dharmaḥ pratīyate 
saṃsṛjyante ca bhāvānāṃ bhedavatyo api śaktayaḥ ।। 

viparītārthavṛttitvaṃ puruṣasya viparyaye 
gamyeta sādhanaṃ hy atra savyāpāraṃ pratīyate ।। 

tvam anyo bhavasīty eṣā tatra syāt parikalpanā 
rājñi bhṛtyatvamāpanne yathā tadvad gatir bhavet ।। 

saṃbhāvanāt kriyāsiddhau kartṛtvena samāśritaḥ 
kriyāyām ātmasādhyāyāṃ sādhanānāṃ prayojakaḥ ।। 

prayogamātre nyagbhāvaṃ svātantryād eva niśritaḥ 
aviśiṣṭo bhavaty anyaiḥ svatantrair muktasaṃśayaiḥ ।। 

nimittebhyaḥ pravartante sarva eva svabhūtaye 
abhiprāyānurodho api svārthasyaiva prasiddhaye ।। 
[iti kartradhikāraḥ][atha hetvadhikāraḥ] 
preṣaṇādhyeṣaṇe kurvaṃs tatsamarthāni cācaran 
kartaiva vihitāṃ śāstre hetusaṃjñāṃ prapadyate ।। 

dravyamātrasya tu praiṣe pṛcchyāder loḍ vidhīyate 
sakriyasya prayogas tu yadā sa viṣayo ṇicaḥ ।। 

guṇakriyāyāṃ svātantryāt preṣaṇe karmatāṃ gataḥ 
niyamāt karmasaṃjñāyāḥ svadharmeṇābhidhīyate ।। 

kriyāyāḥ prerakaṃ karma hetuḥ kartuḥ prayojakaḥ 
karmārthā ca kriyotpattisaṃskārapratipattibhiḥ ।। 
[iti hetvadhikāraḥ] [atha saṃpradānādhikāraḥ] 
anirākaraṇāt kartus tyāgā"ngaṃ karmaṇepsitam 
preraṇānumatibhyāṃ ca labhate saṃpradānatām ।। 

hetutve karmasaṃjñāyāṃ śeṣatve vāpi kārakam 
rucyarthādiṣu śāstreṇa saṃpradānākhyam ucyate ।। 

bhedasya ca vivakṣāyāṃ pūrvāṃ pūrvāṃ kriyāṃ prati 
parasyā"ngasya karmatvān na kriyāgrahaṇaṃ kṛtam ।। 

kriyāṇāṃ samudāye tu yadaikatvaṃ vivakṣitam 
tadā karma kriyāyogāt svākhyayaivopacaryate ।। 

bhedābhedavivakṣā ca svabhāvena vyavasthitā 
tasmād gatyarthakarmatve vyabhicāro na dṛśyate ।। 

vikalpenaiva sarvatra saṃjñe syātām ubhe yadi 
ārambheṇa na yogasya pratyākhyānaṃ samaṃ bhavet ।। 

tyāgarūpaṃ prahātavye prāpye saṃsargadarśanam 
āsthitaṃ karma yat tatra dvairūpyaṃ bhajate kriyā ।। 
[iti saṃpradānādhikāraḥ] [athāpādānādhikāraḥ] 
nirdiṣṭaviṣayaṃ kiṃ cid upāttaviṣayaṃ tathā 
apekṣitakriyaṃ ceti tridhāpādānam ucyate ।। 

saṃyogabhedād bhinnātmā gamir eva bhramir yathā 
dhruvāvadhir apāyo api samavetas tathādhruve ।। 

dravyasvabhāvo na dhrauvyam iti sūtre pratīyate 
apāyaviṣayaṃ dhrauvyaṃ yat tu tāvad vivakṣitam ।। 

saraṇe devadattasya dhrauvyaṃ pāte tu vājinaḥ 
āviṣṭaṃ yad apāyena tasyādhrauvyaṃ pracakṣate ।। 

ubhāv apy adhruvau meṣau yady apy ubhayakarmaje 
vibhāge pravibhakte tu kriye tatra vivakṣite ।। 

meṣāntarakriyāpekṣam avadhitvaṃ pṛthak pṛthak 
meṣayoḥ svakriyāpekṣaṃ kartṛtvaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak ।। 

abhedena kriyaikā tu dvisādhyā ced vivakṣitā 
meṣāv apāye kartārau yady anyo vidyate avadhiḥ ।। 

gatir vinā tv avadhinā nāpāya iti gamyate 
vṛkṣasya parṇaṃ patatīty evaṃ bhāṣye nidarśitam ।। 

bhedābhedau pṛthagbhāvaḥ sthitiś ceti virodhinaḥ 
yugapan na vivakṣyante sarve dharmā balāhake ।। 

dhanuṣā vidhyatīty atra vināpāyavivakṣayā 
karaṇatvaṃ yato nāsti tasmāt tad ubhayaṃ saha ।। 

ekaiva vā satī śaktir dvirūpā vyavatiṣṭhate 
nimittaṃ saṃjñayos tatra parayā bādhyate aparā ।। 

nirdhāraṇe vibhakte yo bhītrādīnāṃ ca yo vidhiḥ 
upāttāpekṣitāpāyaḥ so abudhapratipattaye ।। 
[ity apādānādhikāraḥ] [athādhikaraṇādhikāraḥ] 
kartṛkarmavyavahitām asākṣād dhārayat kriyām 
upakurvat kriyāsiddhau śāstre adhikaraṇaṃ smṛtam ।। 

upaśleṣasya cābhedas tilākāśakaṭādiṣu 
upakārās tu bhidyante saṃyogisamavāyinām ।। 

avināśo gurutvasya pratibandhe svatantratā 
digviśeṣād avaccheda ityādyā bhedahetavaḥ ।। 

ākāśam eva keṣāṃ cid deśabhedaprakalpanāt 
ādhāraśaktiḥ prathamā sarvasaṃyogināṃ matā ।। 

idam atreti bhāvānām abhāvān na prakalpate 
vyapadeśas tam ākāśanimittaṃ saṃpracakṣate ।। 

kālāt kriyā vibhajyanta ākāśāt sarvamūrtayaḥ 
etāvāṃś caiva bhedo ayam abhedopanibandhanaḥ ।। 

yady apy upavasir deśaviśeṣam anurudhyate 
śabdapravṛttidharmāt tu kālam evāvalambate ।। 

vasatāv aprayukte api deśo adhikaraṇaṃ tataḥ 
aprayuktaṃ trirātrādi karma copavasau smṛtam ।। 
[ity adhikaraṇādhikāraḥ] [atha śeṣādhikāraḥ] 
saṃbandhaḥ kārakebhyo anyaḥ kriyākārakapūrvakaḥ 
śrutāyām aśrutāyāṃ vā kriyāyāṃ so abhidhīyate ।। 

dviṣṭho apy asau parārthatvād guṇeṣu vyatiricyate 
tatrābhidhīyamānaḥ san pradhāne apy upayujyate ।। 

nimittaniyamaḥ śabdāt saṃbandhasya na gṛhyate 
karmapravacanīyais tu sa viśeṣo avarudhyate ।। 

sādhanair vyapadiṣṭe ca śrūyamāṇakriye punaḥ 
proktā pratipadaṃ ṣaṣṭhī samāsasya nivṛttaye ।। 

niṣṭhāyāṃ karmaviṣayā ṣaṣthī ca pratiṣidhyate 
śeṣalakṣaṇayā ṣaṣṭhyā samāsastatra neṣyate ।। 

anyena vyapadiṣṭasya yasyānyatropajāyate 
vyatirekaḥ sa dharmau dvau labhate viṣayāntare ।। 

prādhānyaṃ svaguṇe labdhvā pradhāne yāti śeṣatām 
sahayoge svayoge ataḥ pradhānatvaṃ na hīyate ।। 
[iti śeṣādhikāraḥ] 
siddhasyābhimukhībhāvamātraṃ saṃbodhanaṃ viduḥ 
prāptābhimukhyo hy arthātmā kriyāsu viniyujyate ।। 

saṃbodhanaṃ na vākyārtha iti pūrvebhya āgamaḥ 
uddeśena vibhaktyarthā vākyārthāt samapoddhṛtāḥ ।। 

vibhaktyarthe avyayībhāvavacanād avasīyatām 
anyo dravyād vibhaktyarthaḥ so avyayenābhidhīyate ।। 

dravyaṃ tu yad yathābhūtaṃ tad atyantaṃ tathā bhavet 
kriyāyoge api tasyāsau dravyātmā nāpahīyate ।। 

tasmād yat karaṇaṃ dravyaṃ tat karma na punar bhavet 
sarvasya vānyathābhāvas tasya dravyātmano bhavet ।। 
kriyāsamuddeśa 
yāvat siddham asiddhaṃ vā sādhyatvenābhidhīyate 
āśritakramarūpatvāt tat kriyeti pratiyate ।। 

kāryakāraṇabhāvena dhvanatīty āśritakramaḥ 
dhvaniḥ kramanivṛttau tu dhvanir ity eva kathyate ।। 

śvete śvetata ity etac chvetatvena prakāśate 
āśritakramarūpatvād abhidhānaṃ pravartate ।। 

guṇabhūtair avayavaiḥ samūhaḥ kramajanmanām 
buddhyā prakalpitābhedaḥ kriyeti vyapadiśyate ।। 

samūhaḥ sa tatbābhūtaḥ pratibhedam samūhisu 
samāpyate tato bhede kālabhedasya saṃbhavaḥ ।। 

kramāt sadasatāṃ teṣām ātmāno na samūhinām 
sadvastuviṣayair yānti saṃbandhaṃ cakṣurādibhiḥ ।। 

yathā gaur iti samghātaḥ sarvo nendriyagocaraḥ 
bhāgaśas tūpalabdhasya buddhau rūpaṃ nirūpyate ।। 

indriyair anyathāprāptau bhedāmśopanipātibhiḥ 
alātacakravad rūpaṃ kriyāṇāṃ parikalpyate ।। 

yathā ca bhāgāḥ pacater udakāsecanādayaḥ 
udakāsecanādināṃ jñeyā bhāgās tathāpare ।। 

yaś cāpakarṣaparyantam anuprāptaḥ pratīyate 
tatraikasmin kriyāśabdaḥ kevale na prayujyate ।। 

pūrvottarais tathā bhāgaiḥ samavasthāpitakramaḥ 
ekaḥ so apy asadadhyāsād ākhyātair abhidhīyate ।। 

kālānupāti yad rūpaṃ tad astīty anugamyate 
paritas tu paricchinnaṃ bhāva ity eva kathyate ।। 

vyavahārasya siddhatvān na ceyaṃ guṇakalpanā 
upacāro hi mukhyasya saṃbhavād avatiṣṭhate ।। 

āhitottaraśaktitvāt pratyekaṃ vā samūhinaḥ 
anekarūpā lakṣyante kramavanta ivākramāḥ ।। 

anantaraṃ phalaṃ yasyāḥ kalpate tām kriyām viduḥ 
pradhānabhūtāṃ tādarthyād anyāsāṃ tu tadākhyatā ।। 

kriyāpravṛttau yo hetus tadarthaṃ yad viceṣṭitam 
anapekṣya prayuñjīta gacchatīty avadhārayan ।। 

satsu pratyayarūpo asau bhāvo yāvan na jāyate 
tāvat pareṣāṃ rūpeṇa sādhyaḥ sann abhidhīyate ।। 

siddhe tu sādhanākāṅkṣā kṛtārthatvān nivartate 
na kriyāvācināṃ tasmāt prayogas tatra vidyate ।। 

sa cāpūrvāparibhūta ekatvād akramātmakaḥ 
pūrvāparāṇāṃ dharmeṇa tadarthenānugamyate ।। 

asan nivartate tasmād yat sat tad upalabhyate 
tayoḥ sadasatoś cāsāv ātmaika iva gṛhyate ।। 

jātim anye kriyām āhur anekavyaktivartinīm 
asādhyā vyaktirūpeṇa sā sādhyevopalabhyate ।। 

ante yā vā kriyābhāge jātiḥ saiva kriyā smṛtā 
sā vyakter anuniṣpāde jāyamāneva gamyate ।। 

svavyāpāraviśiṣṭānām sattā vā, kartṛkarmanām 
kriyā vyāpārabhedeṣu sattā vā samavāyinī ।। 

antye vātmani yā sattā sā kriyā kaiś cid iṣyate 
bhāva eva hi dhātvartha ity avicchinna āgamaḥ ।। 

buddhiṃ tajjātim anye tu buddhisattām athāpare 
pratyastarūpāṃ bhāveṣu kriyeti pratijānate ।। 

āvirbhāvatirobhāvau janmanāśau tathāparaiḥ 
ṣaṭsu bhāvavikāreṣu kalpitau vyāvahārikau ।। 

tābhyāṃ sarvapravṛttīnām abhedenopasamgrahaḥ 
janmaivāśritasārūpyaṃ sthitir ity abhidhīyate ।। 

jāyamānān na janrnānyad vināśe apy apadārthatā 
ato bhāvavikāreṣu sattaikā vyavatiṣṭhate ।। 

pūrvabhāgas tu yaj jātāt taj janmety apadiśyate 
āśritakramarūpeṇa nimittatve vivakṣite ।। 

ākhyātaśabdair artho asāv evaṃbhūto abhidhīyate 
nāmaśabdāḥ pravartante saṃharanta iva kramam ।। 

phalaṃ phalāpadeśo vā vastu vā tadvirodhi yat 
tad anyad eva pūrveṣāṃ nāga ity apadiśyate ।। 

naivāsti naiva nāstīti vastuno grahanād vinā 
kalpate pararūpeṇa vastv anyad anugamyate ।। 

bhāvābhāvau ghaṭādinām aspṛśann api pāṇinā 
kaś cid vedāprakāśe api prakāśe tata eva vā ।। 

vyāpi saukṣmyaṃ kva cid yāti kva cit saṃhanyate punaḥ 
akurvāṇo atha vā kiṃ cit svaśaktyaivaṃ prakāśate ।। 

sarvarūpasya tattvasya yat krameṇeva darśanam 
bhāgair iva prakḷptiś ca tāṃ kriyām apare viduḥ ।। 

sattā svaśaktiyogena sarvarūpā vyavasthitā 
sādhyā ca sādhanaṃ caiva phalaṃ bhoktā phalasya ca ।। 

kriyām anye tu manyante kva cid apy anapāśritām 
sādhanaikārthakāritve pravṛttim anapāyinīm ।। 

sāmānyabhūtā sā pūrvaṃ bhāgaśaḥ pravibhajyate 
tato vyāpārarūpeṇa sādhyeva vyavatiṣṭhate ।। 

prakṛtiḥ sādhanānāṃ sā prathamaṃ tac ca kārakam 
vyāpārāṇāṃ tato anyatvam aparair upavarṇyate ।। 

bahūnāṃ saṃbhave arthānāṃ ke cid evopakārinaḥ 
saṃsarge kaś cid esāṃ tu prādhānyena pratīyate ।। 

sādhyatvāt tatra cākhyātair vyāpārāḥ siddhasādhanāḥ 
prādhānyenābhidhīyante phalenāpi pravartitāḥ ।। 

ekatvāvṛttibhāvābhyāṃ bhedābhedasamanvaye 
saṃkhyās tatropalabhyante saṃkhyeyāvayavakriyāḥ ।। 

siddhasyārthasya pākādeḥ kathaṃ sādhanayogitā 
sādhyatve vā tiṅantena kṛtāṃ bhedo na kaś cana ।। 

tatra kārakayogāyā yady ākhyātaṃ nibandhanam 
ṣaṣṭhvāḥ sā lena saṃbandhe vyudastā kartṛkarmanoḥ ।। 

ekābhidhāna eko artho yugapac ca dvidharmabhāk 
na saṃbhavati siddhatve sa sādhyaḥ syāt kathaṃ punaḥ ।। 

etāvat sādhanaṃ sādhyam etāvad iti kalpanā 
śāstra eva na vākye asti vibhāgaḥ paramārthataḥ ।। 

ākhyātaśabde bhāgābhyāṃ sādhyasādhanavartitā 
prakalpitā yathā śāstre sa ghañādisv api kramaḥ ।। 

sādhyatvena kriyā tatra dhāturūpanibandhanā 
sattvabhāvas tu yas tasyāḥ sa ghañādinibandhanaḥ ।। 

bandhutābhedarūpeṇa bandhuśabde vyavasthitā 
samūho bandhvavasthā tu pratyayenābhidhīyate ।। 

tatra yam prati sādhyatvam asiddhā taṃ prati kriyā 
siddhā tu yasmin sādhyatvaṃ na tam eva punaḥ prati ।। 

rājñaḥ putrasya napteti na rājñi vyatiricyate 
putrasyārthaḥ pradhānatvaṃ na cāsya vinivartate ।। 

mṛgo dhāvati paśyeti sādhyasādhanarūpatā 
tathā viṣayabhedena saraṇasyopapadyate ।। 

lakṛtyaktakhalarthānāṃ tathāvyayakṛtām api 
rūḍhiniṣṭhāghañādinām dhātuḥ sādhyasya vācakaḥ ।। 

sādhyasyāpariniṣpatteḥ so ayam ity anupagrahaḥ 
tiṅantair antareṇevam upamānaṃ tato na taiḥ ।। 

sādhanatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ ca tiṅkṣu saṃbandhināṃ yataḥ 
tenādhyāropa eva syād upamā tu na vidyate ।। 

nyūneṣu ca samāptārtham upamānaṃ vidhīyate 
kriyā caivāśraye sarvā tatra tatra samāpyate ।। 

yenaiva hetunā haṃsaḥ patatīty abhidhīyate 
ātau tasya samāptatvād upamārtho na vidyate ।। 

kriyāṇāṃ jātibhinnānāṃ sādṛśyaṃ nāvadhāryate 
siddheś ca prakrame sādhyam upamātum na śakyate ।। 

vanam vṛkṣā iti yathā bhedābhedavyapāśrayāt 
arthātmā bhidyate bhāve sa bāhyābhyantare kramaḥ ।। 

sāmānye bhāva ity atra yal liṅgam upalabhyate 
bhedānāṃ anumeyatvān na tat teṣu vivakṣyate ।। 

nirdeśe caritārthatvāl liṅgaṃ bhāve avivaksitam 
upamānavidhitvāc ca bhāvād anyat pacādisu ।। 

bhavatau yat pacādināṃ tāvad atropadiśyate 
na ca liṅgam pacādināṃ bhavatau samavasthitam ।। 

ekaś ca so arthaḥ sattākhyaḥ katham cit kaiś cid ucyate 
liṅgāni cāsya bhidyante pacirūpādibhedavat ।। 

ācāryo mātulaś ceti yathaiko vyapadiśyate 
sambandhibhedād arthātmā sa vidhiḥ paktibhāvayoḥ ।। 
kālasamuddeśaḥ 
vyāpāravyatirekeṇa kālam eke pracakṣate 
nityam ekaṃ vibhu dravyaṃ parimāṇaṃ kriyāvatām ।। 

diṣṭiprasthasuvarṇādi mūrtibhedāya kalpate 
kriyābhedāya kālas tu saṃkhyā sarvasya bhedikā ।। 

utpattau ca sthitau caiva vināśe cāpi tadvatām 
nimittaṃ kālam evāhur vibhaktenātmanā sthitam ।। 

tam asya lokayantrasya sūtradhāraṃ pracakṣate 
pratibandhābhyanujñābhyāṃ tena viśvaṃ vibhajyate ।। 

yadi na pratibadhnīyāt pratibandhaṃ ca notsṛjet 
avasthā vyatikīryeran paurvāparyavinākṛtāḥ ।। 

tasyātmā bahudhā bhinno bhedair dharmāntarāśrayaiḥ 
na hi bhinnam abhinnaṃ vā vastu kiṃ cana vidyate ।। 

naiko na cāpy aneko asti na śuklo nāpi cāsitaḥ 
dravyātmā sa tu saṃsargād evaṃrūpaḥ prakāśate ।। 

saṃsargināṃ tu ye bhedā viśeṣās tasya te matāḥ 
sa bhinnas tair vyavasthānāṃ kālo bhedāya kalpate ।। 

viśiṣṭakālasaṃbandhād vṛttilābhaḥ prakalpate 
śaktīnāṃ saṃprayogasya hetutvenāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

janmābhivyaktiniyamāḥ prayogopanibandhanāḥ 
nityādhīnasthititvāc ca sthitir niyamapūrvikā ।। 

sthitasyānugrahas tais tair dharmaiḥ saṃsargibhis tataḥ 
pratibandhas tirobhāvaḥ prahāṇam iti cātmanaḥ ।। 

pratyavasthaṃ tu kālasya vyāpāro atra vyavasthitaḥ 
kāla eva hi viśvātmā vyāpāra iti kathyate ।। 

mūrtīnāṃ tena bhinnānām ācayāpacayāḥ pṛthak 
lakṣyante pariṇāmena sarvāsāṃ bhedayoginā ।। 

jalayantrabhramāveśasadṛśībhiḥ pravṛttibhiḥ 
sa kalāḥ kalayan sarvāḥ kālākhyāṃ labhate vibhuḥ ।। 

pratibhaddhāś ca yās tena citrā viśvasya vṛttayaḥ 
tāḥ sa evānujānāti yathā tantuḥ śakuntikāḥ ।। 

viśiṣṭakālasaṃbandhāl labdhapākāsu śaktiṣu 
kriyābhivyajyate nityā prayogākhyena karmaṇā ।। 

jātiprayuktā tasyāṃ tu phalavyaktiḥ prajāyate 
kuto apy adbhutayā vṛttyā śaktibhiḥ sā niyamyate ।। 

tatas tu samavāyākhyā śaktir bhedasya bādhikā 
ekatvam iva tā vyaktīr āpādayati kāraṇaiḥ ।। 

athāsmān niyamād ūrdhvaṃ jātayo yāḥ prayojikāḥ 
tāḥ sarvā vyaktim āyānti svacche chāyā ivāmbhasi ।। 

kāraṇānuvidhāyitvād atha kāraṇa pūrvakāḥ 
guṇās tatropajāyante svajātivyaktihetavaḥ ।। 

āśrayāṇāṃ ca nityatvam āśritānāṃ ca nityatā 
tā vyaktīr anugṛhṇāti sthitis tena prakalpate ।। 

anityasya yathotpāde pāratantryaṃ tathā sthitau 
vināśāyaiva tat śṛṣṭam asvādhīnasthitiṃ viduḥ ।। 

sthitaḥ saṃsargibhir bhāvaiḥ svakriyāsv anugṛhyate 
naiṣāṃ sattām anudgṛhya vṛttir janmavatāṃ smṛtā ।। 

jarākhyā kālaśaktir yā śaktyantaravirodhinī 
sā śaktīḥ pratibadhnāti jāyante ca virodhinaḥ ।। 

prayojakās tu ye bhāvāḥ sthitibhāgasya hetavaḥ 
tirobhavanti te sarve yata ātmā prahīyate ।। 

yathaivādbutayā vṛttyā niṣkramaṃ nirnibandhanam 
apadaṃ jāyate sarvaṃ tathāsyātmā prahīyate ।। 

kriyayor apavargiṇyor nānārthasamavetayoḥ 
saṃbandhinā vinaikena paricchedaḥ kathaṃ bhavet ।। 

yathā tulāyāṃ haste vā nānādravyavyavasthitam 
gurutvaṃ parimīyeta kālād evaṃ kriyāgatiḥ ।। 

jahāti sahavṛttāś ca kriyāḥ sa samavasthitāḥ 
vrīhir yathodakaṃ tena hāyanākhyāṃ prapadyate ।। 

pratibandhābhyanujñābhyāṃ vṛttir yā tasya śāsvatī 
tayā vibhajyamāno asau bhajate kramarūpatāṃ ।। 

kartṛbhedāt tadartheṣu pracayāpacayau gataḥ 
samatvaṃ viṣamatvaṃ vā sa ekaḥ pratipadyate ।। 

kriyābhedād yathaikasmiṃs takṣādyākhyā pravartate 
kriyābhedāt tathaikasminn ṛtvādyākhyopajāyate ।। 

ārambhaś ca kriyā caiva niṣṭhā cety abhidhīyate 
dharmāntarāṇām adhyāsabhedāt sadasadātmanaḥ ।। 

yāvāṃś ca dvyaṇukādīnāṃ tāvān himavato apy asau 
na hy ātmā kasya cid bhettuṃ pracetuṃ vāpi śakyate ।। 

anyais tu bhāvair anyeṣāṃ pracayaḥ parikalpyate 
śanair idam idaṃ kṣipram iti tena pratīyate ।। 

asataś ca kramo nāsti sa hi bhettuṃ na śakyate 
sato api cātmatattvaṃ yat tat tathaivāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

kriyopādhiś ca san bhūtabhaviṣyadvartamānatāḥ 
ekādaśābhir ākārair vibhaktāḥ pratipadyate ।। 

bhūtaḥ pañcavidhas tatra bhaviṣyaṃś ca caturvidhaḥ 
vartamāno dvidhākhyāta ity ekādaśa kalpanāḥ ।। 

kāle nidhāya svaṃ rūpaṃ prajñayā yan nigṛhyate 
bhāvās tato nivartante tatra saṃkrāntaśaktayaḥ ।। 

bhāvināṃ caiva yad rūpaṃ tasya ca pratibimbakam 
sunirmṛṣṭa ivādarśe kāla evopapadyate ।। 

tṛṇaparṇalatādīni yathā sroto anukarṣati 
pravartayati kālo api mātrā mātrāvatāṃ tathā ।। 

āviśyevānusaṃdhatte yathā gatimatāṃ gatīḥ 
vāyus tatraiva kālātmā vidhatte kramarūpatām ।। 

ayanapravibhāgaś ca gatīś ca jyotiṣāṃ dhruvā 
nivṛttiprabhavāś caiva bhūtānāṃ tannibandhanāḥ ।। 

mātrāṇāṃ pariṇāmā ye kālavṛttyanupātinaḥ 
nakṣatrākhyā pṛthak teṣu cihnamātraṃ tu tārakāḥ ।। 

rutair mṛgaśakuntānāṃ sthāvarāṇāṃ ca vṛttibhiḥ 
chāyādipariṇāmaiś ca ṛtudhāmā nirūpyate ।। 

nirbhāsopagamo yo ayaṃ kramavān iva dṛśyate 
akramasyāpi viśvasya tat kālasya viceṣṭitam ।। 

dūrāntikavyavasthānam adhvādhikaraṇaṃ yathā 
cirakṣipravyavasthānaṃ kālādhikaraṇaṃ tathā ।। 

tasyābhinnasya kālasya vyavahāre kriyākṛtāḥ 
bhedā iva trayaḥ siddhā yāṃl loko nātivartate ।। 

ekasya śaktayas tisraḥ kālasya samavasthitāḥ 
yatsaṃbandhena bhāvānāṃ darśanādarśane satām ।। 

dvābhyāṃ sa kila śaktibhyāṃ bhāvānāṃ varaṇātmakaḥ 
śaktis tu vartamānākhyā bhāvarūpaprakāśinī ।। 

anāgatā janmaśakteḥ śaktir apratibandhikā 
atītākhyā tu yā śaktis tayā janma virudhyate ।। 

tamaḥprakāśavat tv ete trayo adhvāno vyavasthitāḥ 
akramās teṣu bhāvānāṃ kramaḥ samupalabhyate ।। 

dvau tu tatra tamorūpāv ekasyālokavat sthitiḥ 
atītam api keṣāṃ cit punar viparivartate ।। 

yugapad vartamānatvaṃ taddharmā pratipadyate 
keṣāṃ cid vartamānatvāc caiti tadvad atītatām ।। 

hetupakārād ākṣipto vartamānatvam āgataḥ 
śāntahetūpakāraḥ san punar nopaiti darśanam ।। 

dve eva kālasya vibhoḥ keṣāṃ cic chaktivartmanī 
karoti yābhyāṃ bhāvānām unmīlananimīlane ।। 

kalābhiḥ pṛthagarthābhiḥ pravibhaktaṃ svabhāvataḥ 
ke cid buddhyanusaṃhāralakṣaṇaṃ taṃ pracakṣate ।। 

jñānānugataśaktiṃ vā bāhyaṃ vā satyataḥ sthitam 
kālātmānam anāśritya vyavahartuṃ na śakyate ।। 

tisro bhāvasya bhāvasya keṣāṃ cid bhāvaśaktayaḥ 
tābhiḥ svaśaktibhiḥ sarvaṃ sadaivāsti ca nāsti ca ।। 

sattvād avyatirekeṇa tās tisro api vyavasthitāḥ 
kramas tās tadabhedāc ca sadasattvaṃ na bhidyate ।। 

darśanādarśanenaikaṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaṃ tad eva tu 
adhvanām ekatā nāsti na ca kiṃ cin nivartate ।। 

śaktyātmadevatāpakṣair bhinnaṃ kālasya darśanam 
prathamaṃ tad avidyāyāṃ yad vidyāyāṃ na vidyate ।। 

abhede yadi kālasya hrasvadīrghaplutādiṣu 
dṛśyate bhedanirbhāsaḥ sa cirakṣiprabuddhivat ।। 

hrasvadīrghaplutāvṛttyā nālikāsalilādiṣu 
kathaṃ pracayayogaḥ syāt kalpanāmātrahetukaḥ ।। 

abhivyaktinimittasya pracayena pracīyate 
abhinnam api śabdasya tattvam apracayātmakam ।। 

evaṃ mātrāturīyasya bhedo dāśatayasya vā 
parimāṇavikalpena śabdātmani na vidyate ।। 

anuniṣpādikalpena ye antarāla iva sthitāḥ 
śabdās te pratipattṝṇām upāyāḥ pratipattaye ।। 

viśiṣṭam avadhiṃ taṃ tam upādāya prakalpate 
kālaḥ kālavatām ekaḥ kṣaṇamāsartubhedabhāk ।। 

buddhyavagrahabhedāc ca vyavahārātmani sthitaḥ 
tāvān eva kṣaṇaḥ kālo yugamanvantarāṇi vā ।। 

pratibandhābhyanujñābhyāṃ nālikāvivarāśrite 
yad ambhasi prakṣaraṇaṃ tat kālasyaiva ceṣṭitam ।। 

alpe mahati vā chidre tatsaṃbandhe na bhidyate 
kālasya vṛttir ātmāpi tam evāsyānuvartate ।। 

ākrīḍa iva kālasya dṛśyate yaḥ svaśaktibhiḥ 
bahurūpasya bhāveṣu bahudhā tena bhidyate ।। 

tvacisārasya vā vṛddhiṃ tṛṇarājasya vā dadhat 
tāvat tadvṛddhiyogena kālatattvaṃ vikalpate ।। 

vyatikrame api mātrāṇāṃ tasya nāsti vyatikramaḥ 
na gantṛgatibhedena mārgabhedo asti kaś cana ।। 

udayāstamayāvṛttyā jyotiṣāṃ lokasiddhayā 
kālasyāvyatipāte api tāddharmyam iva lakṣyate ।। 

ādityagrahanakṣatraparispandam athāpare 
bhinnam āvṛttibhedena kālaṃ kālavido viduḥ ।। 

kriyāntaraparicchedapravṛttā yā kriyāṃ prati 
nirjñātaparimāṇā sā kāla ity abhidhīyate ।। 

jñāne rūpasya saṃkrāntir jñānenaivānusaṃhṛtiḥ 
ataḥ kriyāntarābhāve sā kriyā kāla iṣyate ।। 

bhūto ghaṭa itīyaṃ ca sattāyā eva bhūtatā 
bhūtā satteti sattāyāḥ sattā bhūtābhidhīyate ।। 

parato bhidyate sarvam ātmā tu na vikalpyate 
parvatādisthitis tasmāt pararūpeṇa bhidyate ।। 

prasiddhabhedā vyāpārā virūpāvayavakriyāḥ 
sāhacaryeṇa bhidyante sarūpāvayavakriyāḥ ।। 

vyavadhānam ivopaiti nivṛtta iva dṛśyate 
kriyāsamūho bhujyādir antarālapravṛttibhiḥ ।। 

na ca vicchinnarūpo api so avirāmān nivartate 
sarvaiva hi kriyānyena samkīrṇevopalabhyate ।। 

tadantarāladṛṣṭā vā sarvaivāvayavakriyā 
sādṛśyāt sati bhede tu tadaṅgatvena gṛhyate ।। 

sad asad vāpi vastu syāt tṛtīyaṃ nāsti kiṃ cana 
tena bhūtabhaviṣyantau muktvā madhyaṃ na vidyate ।। 

nirvṛttirūpam ekasya bhedābhāvān na kalpate 
sad asad vāpi tenaikaṃ kramarūpaṃ kathaṃ bhavet ।। 

bahūnāṃ cānavasthānād ekam evopalabhyate 
yathopalabdhi smaraṇaṃ tatra cāpy upapadyate ।। 

sadasadrūpam ekaṃ syād sarvasyaikatvakalpane 
nirvṛttirūpaṃ nirvṛtteḥ sāmānyam atha vā bhavet ।। 

kāryotpattau samarthaṃ vā svena dharmeṇa tat tathā 
ātmatattvena gṛhyeta sā cāsmin vartamānatā ।। 

kriyāprabandharūpaṃ yad adhyātmaṃ vinigṛhyate 
saṃkrāntarūpam ekatra tām āhur vartamānatām ।। 

kriyātipattir atyantaṃ kriyānutpattilakṣaṇā 
na ca bhūtam anutpannaṃ na bhaviṣyat tathāvidham ।। 

prāg viruddhakriyotpādān nirvṛtte vā virodhini 
vyāpāre avadhibhedena viṣayas tatra bhidyate ।। 

vyabhicāre nimittasya sādhutvaṃ na prakalpate 
bhāvy āsīd iti sūtreṇa tat kāle anyatra śiṣyate ।। 

svakāla eva sādhutve kālabhede gatiḥ katham 
vākyārthād atadartheṣu viśiṣṭatvaṃ na sidhyati ।। 

tadarthaś ced avayavo bhāvino bhūtatāgatiḥ 
na syād atyantabhūtatvam evaikaṃ tatra saṃbhavet ।। 

viśiṣṭakālatā pūrvaṃ tathāpi tu viśeṣaṇe 
āśrayāt so antaraṅgatvāt tatra sādhur bhaviṣyati ।। 

āmiśra eva prakrāntaḥ sa padārthas tathāvidhaḥ 
kevalasya vimiśratvaṃ nitye arthe nopapadyate ।। 

śuddhe ca kāle vyākhyātam āmiśre na prasidhyati 
sādhutvam ayathākālaṃ tat sūtreṇopadiśyate ।। 

ākhyātapadavācye arthe nirvartyatvāt pradhānatā 
viśeṣaṇaṃ tadākṣepāt tatkāle vyavatiṣṭhate ।। 

saṃpratyayānukāro vā śabdavyāpāra eva vā 
adhyasyate viruddhe arthe na ca tena virudhyate ।। 

bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyad ity etau pratyayau vartamānatām 
atyajantau prapadyete viruddhāśrayarūpatām ।। 

adhvano vartamānasya viṣayeṇa bhaviṣyatā 
bhāṣye bhaviṣyatkāleti kāryārthaṃ vyapadiśyate ।। 

icchā cikīrśatīty atra svakālam anurudhyate 
bhaviṣyati prakṛtyarthe tatkālaṃ nānurudhyate ।। 

āśāsyamānatantratvād āśaṃsāyāṃ viparyayaḥ 
prayoktṛdharmaḥ śabdārthe śabdair evānuśajyate ।। 

apchālibījasaṃyoge vartate niṣpadir yadā 
tatrāvayavavṛttitvād bhaviṣyatpratiṣedhanam ।। 

phalaprasavarūpe tu niṣpadau bhūtakālatā 
dharmāntareṣu tad rūpam adhyasya parikalpyate ।। 

upayukte nimittānāṃ vyāpāre phalasiddhaye 
tatra rūpaṃ yad adhyastaṃ tatkālaṃ tat pratīyate ।। 

niṣpattāv avadhiḥ kaś cit kaś cit prativivakṣitaḥ 
hetujanmavyapekṣātaḥ phalajanmeti cocyate ।। 

abahiḥsādhanādhīnā siddhir yatra vivakṣitā 
tat sādhanāntarābhāvāt siddham ity apadiśyate ।। 

tasmād avadhibhedena siddhā mukhyaiva bhūtatā 
anāgatatvam astitvaṃ hetudharmavyapekṣaṇe ।। 

satām indriyasaṃbandhāt saiva sattā viśiṣyate 
bhedena vyavahāro hi vastvantaranibandhanaḥ ।। 

astitvaṃ vastumātrasya buddhyā tu parigṛhyate 
yaḥ samāsādanād bhedaḥ sa tatra na vivakṣitaḥ ।। 

yogād vā strītvapuṃstvābhyāṃ na kiṃ cid avatiṣṭhate 
svasminn ātmani tatrānyad bhūtaṃ bhāvi ca kathyate ।। 
puruṣasamuddeśa 
pratyaktā parabhāvaś cāpy upādhī kartṛkarmanoḥ 
tayoḥ śrutiviśeṣeṇa vācakau madhyamottamau ।। 

sad asad vāpi caitanyam etābhyām avagamyate 
caitanyabhāge prathamaḥ puruṣo na tu vartate ।। 

budhijānāticitibhiḥ prathame puruṣe sati 
samjñānārthair na caitanyasyopayogaḥ prakāśyate ।। 

saṃbodhanārthaḥ sarvatra madhyame kaiś cid iṣyate 
tathā saṃbodhane sarvāṃ prathamāṃ yuṣmado viduḥ ।। 

saṃbodhanaṃ na loke asti vidhātavyena vastunā 
svāhendraśatrur vardhasva yathā rājā bhaveti ca ।। 

yuṣmadarthasya siddhatvān niyatā cādyudāttatā 
yuṣmadaḥ prathamāntasya paraś cen na padād asau ।। 

guṇapradhānatābhedaḥ puruśādiviparyayaḥ 
nirdeśaś cānyathā śāstre nityatvān na virudhyate ।। 

yathānirdeśam arthāḥ syur yesāṃ śāstraṃ vidhāyakam 
kim cit sāmānyam āśritya sthite tu pratipādanam ।। 

yo aśve yaḥ pīṭha ity atra bhūtayor aśvapīṭhayoḥ 
yathopalakṣaṇārthatvaṃ tathārtheṣv anuśāsanam ।। 
saṃkhyāsamuddeśa 
saṃkhyāvān sattvabhūto arthaḥ sarva evābhidhīyate 
bhedābhedavibhāgo hi loke saṃkhyānibandhanaḥ ।। 

sa dharmo vyatirikto vā teṣāṃ ātmaiva vā tathā 
bhedahetutvam āśritya saṃkhyeti vyapadiśyate ।। 

samavetā paricchedye kva cid anyatra sā sthitā 
prakalpayati bhāvānāṃ saṃkhyā bhedaṃ tathātmanaḥ ।। 

paratve cāparatve ca bhede tulyā śrutir yathā 
saṃkhyāśabdābhidheyatvaṃ bhedahetos tathā guṇe ।। 

asvatantre svatantratvaṃ paradharmo yathā guṇe 
abhedye bhedyabhāvo api dravyadharmas tathā guṇe ।। 

svabuddhyā tam apoddhṛtya loko apy āgamam āśritaḥ 
svadharmād anyadharmeṇa vyācaṣṭe pratipattaye ।। 

paropakāratattvānāṃ svātantryenābhidhāyakaḥ 
śabdaḥ sarvapadārthānā svadharmad viprakṛṣyate ।। 

yathaivāviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ na kiṃ cid avabhāsate 
tathā bhāvo apy asaṃsṛṣṭo na kaś cid upalabhyate ।। 

bhedena tu samākhyātaṃ yal loko apy anuvartate 
āgamāc chāstrasadṛśo vyavahāraḥ sa varṇyate ।। 

buddhau sthiteṣu teṣv evam adhyāropo na durlabhaḥ 
paradharmasya na hy atra sadasattvaṃ prayojakam ।। 

sāmānyeṣv api sāmānyaṃ viśeṣeṣu viśiṣṭatā 
saṃkhyāsu saṃkhyā liṅgeṣu liṅgam evaṃ prakalpate ।। 

ato dravyāśritāṃ saṃkhyām āhuḥ saṃsargavādinaḥ 
bhedābhedavyatīteṣu bhedābhedavidhāyinīm ।। 

ātmāntarānāṃ yenātmā tadrūpa iva lakṣyate 
atadrūpeṇa saṃsargāt sā nimittasarūpatā ।। 

saṃsṛṣṭeṣv api nirbhāge bhūteṣv arthakriyā yathā 
sattvādiṣu ca mātrāsu sarvāsv evaṃ pratīyate ।। 

dvitvādiyonir ekatvaṃ bhedās tatpūrvakā yataḥ 
vinā tena na saṃkhyānām anyāsām asti saṃbhavaḥ ।। 

ekatve buddhisahite nimittaṃ dvitvajanmani 
ekatvābhyāṃ samutpannam evaṃ vā tat pratīyate ।। 

ekatvasamudāyo vā sāpekṣe vā pṛthak pṛthak 
ekatve dvitvam ity evaṃ tayor dvivacanaṃ bhavet ।। 

eko api guṇabhedena saṅgho bhedaṃ prakalpayet 
āśrayāśrayibhedo hi tadāśrayanibandhanaḥ ।। 

saṃkhyeyasaṅghasaṃkhyānasaṅghaḥ saṃkhyeti kathyate 
vimśatyādisu sānyasva dravyasaṅghasya bhedikā ।। 

ekaviṃśatisaṃkhvāvāṃ saṃkhyāntarasarūpayoḥ 
ekasyāṃ buddhyanāvṛttyā, bhāgayor iva kalpanā ।। 

asaṃkhyāsamudāyatvāt saṃkhyākāryaṃ vidhīyate 
samūhatve tu tan na syāt svāṅgādisamudāyavat ।। 

saṃkhyeyāntaratantrāsu yā saṃkhyāsu pravartate 
āvṛttivargasaṃkhyeyā tāṃ saṃkhyāṃ tādṛśīṃ viduḥ ।। 

na saṃkhyāyāṃ na saṃkhyeye dvau daśety asti saṃbhavaḥ 
bhedābhāvān na saṃkhyāyāṃ virodhān na tadāśraye ।। 

saṃkhyāyete daśadvargau dvidaśā iti saṃkhyayā 
tadrūpe vāpi saṃkhyeya āvṛttiḥ parigaṇyate ।। 

saṃkhyā nāma na saṃkhyāsti saṃjñaiṣeti yathocyate 
rūpaṃ na rūpam apy evaṃ samjñā sā hi sitādiṣu ।। 

saṃkhyānajātiyogāt tu saṃkhyā saṃkhyeti kathyate 
rūpatvajātiyogāc ca rūpe rūpam iti smṛtam ।। 

nimittam ekam ity atra vibhaktyā nābhidhīyate 
tadvatas tu yad ekatvaṃ vibhaktis tatra vartate ।। 

ekasya pracayo dṛṣṭaḥ samūhaś ca dvayos tathā 
nimittavyatirekeṇa saṃkhyānyā bhedikā tataḥ ।। 

tad ekam api caikatvaṃ vibhaktiśravaṇād ṛte 
nocyate tena śabdena vibhaktyā tu sahocyate ।। 

anvayavyatirekau ca yadi syād vacanāntaram 
syātām asati tasmimś ca prakṛtyartho na kalpyate ।। 

ekatvam eka ity atra śuddhadravyaviśeṣaṇam 
saguṇas tu prakṛtyartho vibhaktyarthena bhidyate ।। 

dvyekayor iti nirdeśāt saṃkhyāmātre api saṃbhavaḥ 
ekādīnāṃ prasiddhyā tu saṃkhyeyārthatvam ucyate ।। 
upagrahasamuddeśa 
ya ātmanepadād bhedaḥ kva cid arthasya gamyate 
anyataś cāpi lādeśān manyante tam upagraham ।। 

kva cit sādhanam evāsau kva cit tasya viśeṣaṇam 
sādhanaṃ tatra karmādi vyaktavāco viśeṣaṇam ।। 

kriyā viṣayabhedena jīvikādiṣu bhidyate 
lādeśaiḥ sa kriyābhedo vākyeṣv api niyamyate ।। 

dhātvarthas tadviśeṣaś cāpy uktaḥ kva cid upagrahaḥ 
dhātvartho gandhanādiḥ syād vyatihāro viśeṣaṇam ।। 

kriyāpravṛttāv ākhyātā kaiś cit svārthaparārthatā 
asati vā sati vāpi vivakṣitanibandhanā ।। 

kesāṃ cit kartrabhiprāye ṇicā saha vikalpate 
ātmanepadam anyesāṃ tadarthā prakṛtir yathā ।। 

krīṇīṣva vapate dhatte cinoti cinute api ca 
āptaprayogā dṛśyante yeṣu ṇyartho abhidhīyate ।। 

saṃvidhānaṃ pacādināṃ kva cid arthaḥ pratīyate 
tannimittā yathānyāpi kriyādhiśrayaṇādikā ।। 

kartrabhiprāyatā sūtre kriyābhedopalakṣaṇam 
tathābhūtā kriyā yā hi tatkartā phalabhāg yataḥ ।। 

yathopalakṣyate kālas tārakādarśanādibhiḥ 
tathā phalaviśeṣeṇa kriyābhedo nidarśyate ।। 

kriyāviśeṣavacane sāmarthyam uparudhyate 
kesāṃ cid anye tu kṛtāḥ svariteto ñitas tathā ।। 

anubandhaś ca siddhe arthe smṛtyartham anuṣajyate 
tulyārtheṣv api cāvaśyaṃ na sarveṣv ekadharmatā ।। 

dṛśīkṣyoḥ sadṛśe apy arthe nābhedaḥ pratipūrvayoḥ 
ṇyarthopādāyinas tasmān na tulyārthāḥ pacādibhiḥ ।। 

umbhyarthe vartamānasya karoter bhinnadharmaṇaḥ 
ṇyarthopādāyitā tasmān niyatāḥ śabdaśaktayaḥ ।। 

tathā hy anuprayogasya karoter ātmanepade 
pūrvavadgrahaṇaṃ prāpte svaritaṃ samupasthitam ।। 

ekatve api kriyākhyāte sādhanāśrayasaṃkhyayā 
bhidyate na tu liṅgākhyo bhedas tatra tadāśritaḥ ।। 

tasmād avasthite apy arthe kasya cit pratibadhyate 
śabdasya śaktiḥ sa tv eṣa śāstre anvākhyāyate vidhiḥ ।। 

yasyārthasya prasiddhyartham ārabhyante pacādayaḥ 
tat pradhānaṃ phalaṃ teṣāṃ na lābhādi prayojanam ।। 

yatrobhau svāmidāsau tu prārabhete saha kriyām 
yugapad dharmabhedena dhātus tatra na vartate ।। 

yatra pratividhānārthaḥ pacis tatrātmanepadam 
parasmaipadam anyatra saṃskārādyabhidhāyini ।। 

saṃvidhātuś ca sāṃnidhyād dāse dharmo anusajyate 
plakṣaśabdasya sāṃnidhyān nyagrodhe plakṣatā yathā ।। 

puroḍāśābhidhānaṃ ca dhānādiṣu yathā sthitam 
chattriṇā cābhisaṃbandhāc chattriśabdābhidheyatā ।। 

arthāt pratītam anyonyaṃ pārārthyam avivakṣitam 
ity ayaṃ śeṣaviṣayaḥ kaiś cid atrānuvarṇyate ।। 

atha pratividhātā yo halaiḥ kṛṣati pañcabhiḥ 
bhāṣye nodāhṛtaṃ kasmāt prāptaṃ tatrātmanepadam ।। 

pratītatvāt tadarthasya śeṣatvaṃ yadi kalpyate 
na syāt prāptavibhāṣāsau svaritetāṃ nivartikā ।। 

śuddhe tu saṃvidhānārthe kaiś cid atreṣyate kṛṣiḥ 
taddharmā yajir ity evaṃ na syāt tatrātmanepadam ।। 

atra tūpapadenāyam arthabhedaḥ pratīyate 
prāpte vibhāṣā kriyate tasmān nātrātmanepadam ।। 
liṅgasamuddeśa 
stanakeśādisaṃbandho viśiṣṭā vā stanādayaḥ 
tadupavyañjanā jātir guṇāvasthā guṇās tathā ।। 

śabdopajanito arthātmā śabdasaṃskāra ity api 
liṅgānāṃ liṅgatattvajñair vikalpāḥ sapta darśitāḥ ।। 

upādānavikalpāś ca liṅgānāṃ sapta varṇitāḥ 
vikalpasaṃniyogābhyāṃ ye śabdeṣu vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

tisro jātaya evaitāḥ kesāṃ cit samavasthitāḥ 
aviruddhā, viruddhābhir gomahiṣyādijātibhiḥ ।। 

hastinyāṃ vaḍavāyāṃ ca strīti buddheḥ samanvayaḥ 
atas tāṃ jātim icchanti dravyādisamavāyinīm ।। 

paratantrasya yal liṅgam apoddhāre vivakṣite 
tatrāsau śabdasaṃskāraḥ śabdair eva vyapāśritaḥ ।। 

buddhyā kalpitarūpeṣu liṅgeṣv api ca saṃbhavaḥ 
strītvādīnāṃ vyavasthā hi sā liṅgair vyapadiśyate ।। 

yathā salilanirbhāsā mṛgatṛṣṇāsu jāyate 
jalopalabdhyanuguṇād bījād buddhir jale asati ।। 

tathaivāvyapadeśyebhyo hetubhyas tārakādiṣu 
mukhyebhya iva liṅgebhyo bhedā loke vyavasthitāḥ ।। 

vyakteṣu vyaktarūpāṇāṃ stanādīnāṃ tu darśanāt 
avyaktavyañjanāvyakter jātir na parikalpyate ।। 

astitvaṃ ca pratijñāya sadādarśanam icchataḥ 
atyantādarśane na syād asattvaṃ prati niścayaḥ ।। 

na cālam anumānāya śabdo adarśanapūrvakaḥ 
siddhe hi darśane kiṃ syād anumānaprayojanam ।। 

āvirbhāvas tirobhāvaḥ sthitiś cety anapāyinaḥ 
dharmā mūrtiṣu sarvāsu liṅgatvenānudarśitāḥ ।। 

sarvamūrtyātmabhūtānāṃ śabdādināṃ guṇe guṇe 
trayaḥ sattvādidharmās te sarvatra samavasthitāḥ ।। 

rūpasya cātmamātrānāṃ śuklādināṃ pratikṣaṇam 
kā cit pralīyate kā cit kathaṃ cid abhivardhate ।। 

kvathitodakavac caiṣām anavasthitavṛttitā 
ajasraṃ sarvabhāvānāṃ bhāṣya evopavarṇitā ।। 

pravṛtter ekarūpatvaṃ sāmyaṃ vā sthitir ucyate 
avirbhāvatirobhāvapravṛttyā vāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

guṇā ity eva buddher vā nimittatvaṃ sthitir matā 
sthiteś ca sarvaliṅgānāṃ sarvanāmatvam ucyate ।। 

sthiteṣu sarvaliṅgeṣu vivakṣāniyamāśrayaḥ 
kasya cic chabdasaṃskāre vyāpāraḥ kva cid iṣyate ।। 

saṃnidhāne nimittānāṃ kiṃ cid eva pravartakam 
yathā takṣādiśabdānāṃ lingeṣu niyamas tathā ।। 

bhāvatattvadṛśaḥ śiṣṭāḥ śabdārtheṣu vyavasthitāḥ 
yad yad dharme aṅgatām eti liṅgaṃ tat tat pracakṣate ।। 

svarabhedād yathā śabdāḥ sādhavo viṣayāntare 
liṅgabhedāt tathā siddhāt sādhutvam anugamyate ।। 

prayogo viprayogaś ca loke yatropalabhyate 
śāstram ārabhyate tatra na prayogāviparyaye ।। 

upādhibhedād artheṣu guṇadharmasya kasya cit 
nimittabhāvaḥ sādhutve vivakṣā ca vyavasthitā ।। 

himāraṇye mahattvena yukte strītvam avasthitam 
hrasvopādhiviśiṣṭāyāḥ kuṭyāḥ prasavayogitā ।। 

śabdāntarānāṃ bhinne artha upāyāḥ pratipattaye 
ekatām iva niścitya laghvartham upadarśitāḥ ।। 

utpattiḥ prasavo anyeṣāṃ nāśaḥ saṃstyānam ity api 
ātmarūpaṃ tu bhāvānāṃ sthitir ity apadiśyate ।। 

dṛṣṭaṃ nimittaṃ kesāṃ cij jātyādivad avasthitam 
dṛṣṭavac chabdasaṃskāramātraṃ tu parikalpitam ।। 

yathā prasiddhe apy ekatve nānātvābhiniveśinaḥ 
nānātvaṃ janayantīva śabdā liṅge api sa kramaḥ ।। 

idaṃ veyam ayaṃ veti śabdasaṃskāramātrakam 
nimittadarśanād arthe kaiś cit sarvatra varṇyate ।। 

nāvaśyaṃ viṣayatvena nimittaṃ vyavatiṣṭhate 
indriyādi yathādṛṣṭaṃ bhedahetus tad iṣyate ।। 
vṛttisamuddeśa 
kutsāpraśaṃsātiśayaiḥ samāptārthaṃ tu yujyate 
padaṃ svārthādayaḥ sarve yasmāt kutsādihetavaḥ ।। 

devadattādikutsāyāṃ vartate kutsitaśrutiḥ 
kutsitasthā tu yā kutsā tadarthaḥ ko vidhīyate ।। 

prakṛṣṭa iti śuklādiprakarṣasyābhidhāyakaḥ 
prakṛṣṭasya prakarṣe tu tarabādir vidhīyate ।। 

kutsitatvena kutsyo vā na samyag vāpi kutsitaḥ 
svaśabdābhihite kena viśiṣṭo arthaḥ pratīyate ।। 

na ca sāṃpratikī kutsā bhedābhāvāt pratīyate 
pūjyate kutsitatvena praśastatvena kutsyate ।। 

viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ padayor upajāyate 
na prātipadikārthaś ca tatraiva vyatiricyate ।। 

viśeṣyaṃ syād anirjñātaṃ nirjñāto artho viśeṣaṇam 
parārthatvena śeṣatvaṃ sarveṣām upakāriṇām ।। 

vibhaktibhedo niyamād guṇaguṇyabhidhāyinoḥ 
sāmānādhikaraṇyasya prasiddhir dravyaśabdayoḥ ।। 

dravye anirjñātajātīye kṛṣṇaśabdaḥ prayujyate 
anirjñātaguṇe caivaṃ tilaśabdaḥ pravartate ।। 

sāmānyānām asaṃbandhāt tau viśeṣe vyavasthitau 
rūpābhedād viśeṣaṃ tam abhivyaṅktuṃ na śaknutaḥ ।। 

tāv eva saṃnipatitau bhedena pratipādane 
avacchedam ivādhāya saṃśayaṃ vyapakarṣataḥ ।। 

dravyātmā guṇasaṃsargabhedād āśrīyate pṛthak 
jātisaṃbandhabhedāc ca dvitīya iva gṛhyate ।। 

nimittair abhisaṃbandhād yā nimittasarūpatā 
tayaikasyāpi nānātvaṃ rūpabhedāt prakalpate ।। 

dravyāvasthā tṛtīyā tu yasyāṃ saṃsṛjyate dvayam 
tayor avasthayor bhedād āśrayatve niyujyate ।। 

buddhyaikaṃ bhidyate bhinnam ekatvaṃ copagacchati 
buddhyāvasthā vibhajyante sā hy arthasya vidhāyikā ।। 

vyapadeśivad ekasmin buddhyā nānātvakalpanā 
tayā kalpitabhedaḥ sann arthātmā vyapadiśyate ।। 

kriyābhedena dṛṣṭānām aśmādīnāṃ punaḥ punaḥ 
kiṃ cid darśanam anyena darśanenāpadiśyate ।। 

prayogabhedād dhātūnāṃ prakalpya bahurūpatām 
bhedābhedāv upādāya kva cid ekāctvam ucyate ।। 

anvayavyatirekābhyām arthavān parikalpitaḥ 
eko dhātvarthavigamād varṇatvenopacaryate ।। 

dravyātmānas trayas tasmād buddhau nānā vyavasthitāḥ 
āśrayāśrayidharmeṇety ayaṃ pūrvebhya āgamaḥ ।। 

sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca śabdayoḥ kaiś cid iṣyate 
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ saṃjñāsaṃjñitvam eva ca ।। 

keṣāṃ cij jātiguṇayor ekārthasamavetayoḥ 
vṛttiḥ kṛṣṇatileṣv iṣṭā śabde dravyābhidhāyini ।। 

saṃs tu rūparasādinām āśrayo nābhidhīyate 
dravyābhidhānena vinā tatas te dvandvabhāvinaḥ ।। 

dravyābhidhāyī kṛṣṇādir ākāṅkṣāvān pravartate 
nimittānuvidhāyitvāt tat tilādau na vidyate ।। 

evaṃ jātimati dravye pratyāsanne kriyāṃ prati 
guṇadharma guṇāviṣṭaṃ dravyaṃ bhedāya kalpate ।। 

guṇamātrābhidhāyitvaṃ ke cid icchanti vṛttiṣu 
ajāśvādiṣu saṃbandhād rūḍhīnām iva rūḍhibhiḥ ।। 

tile pūrvam upātte vā tatraiva matub iṣyate 
sa ca dharmaḥ samāseṣu guṇas tasmād viśeṣaṇam ।। 

[paṭvīmṛdvyoḥ samāse tu yady apy ekārthavṛttitā 
bhinnam atrādhikaraṇaṃ prāg vṛttes tac ca gṛhyate ।। 

anusyūteva bhedābhyām ekā prakhyopajāyate 
yadā sahavivakṣāṃ tām āhur dvandvaikaśeṣayoḥ ।। 

itaretarayogas tu bhinnasaṅghābhidhāyinām 
pratyekaṃ ca samūho asau samūhiṣu samāpyate ।। 

vyāpārasamudāyasya yathādhiśrayaṇādiṣu 
pratyekaṃ jātivad vṛttis tathā dvandvapadeṣv api ।। 

śauṇḍārdharcapuroḍāśacchattriṇo atra nidarśanam 
te viṣṇumitrā iti ca bhinneṣu sahacāriṣu ।। 

arthāntarābhidhāyitvaṃ tathārthāntaravartinām 
yābhyāṃ caikam anekārthaṃ tābhyām evāparaṃ padam ।। 

samudāyāntaratvāc ca tādṛśo artho na laukikaḥ 
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śāstrārtho api na dṛśyate ।। 

duḥkhā durupapādā ca tasmād bhāṣye apy udāhṛtā 
yugapadvācitā sā tu vyavahārārtham āśritā ।। 

samudāyam upakramya padaṃ tasyāṃ prayujyate 
vibhāgena samākhyāne tatas tad dvyartham ucyate ।। 

vākye api niyatā dharmāḥ ke cid vṛttau dvayos tathā 
te tv abhedena sāmarthyamātra evopavarṇitāḥ ।। 

vṛttau viśeṣavṛttitvād bhede sāmānyavācitā 
upamānasamāsādau śyāmādīnām udāhṛtā ।। 

vṛttir anyapadārthe yā tasyā vākyeṣv asaṃbhavaḥ 
cārthe dvandvapadānāṃ ca bhede vṛttir na vidyate ।। 

bhede sati nirādīnāṃ krāntādyartheṣv asaṃbhavaḥ 
prāg vṛtter jātivācitvaṃ na ca gaurakharādiṣu ।। 

krīḍāyā, jīvikāyāś ca vākyenāvacanāt tathā 
na nityagrahaṇaṃ yuktaṃ kauṭilye yaṅvidhau yathā ।। 

nirdhāraṇādiviṣaye vyapekṣaiva yataḥ sthitā 
samāsapratiṣedhānāṃ tato nāsti prayojanam ।। 

vidhibhiḥ pratiṣedhaiś ca bhedābhedanidarśanam 
kṛtaṃ dvandvaikavadbhāve saṅghavṛttyupadeśavat ।। 

sāmarthyam aviśeṣoktam api lokavyavasthayā 
vṛttyavṛttyoḥ prayogajñair vibhaktaṃ pratipattṛbhiḥ ।। 

arthasya vinivṛttatvāl lugādi na virudhyate 
ekārthībhāva evātaḥ samāsākhyā vidhīyate ।। 

vyavasthitavibhāṣā ca sāmānye kaiś cid iṣyate 
tathā vākyaṃ vyapekṣāyāṃ samāso anyatra śiṣyate ।। 

tulyaśrutitvāt tattve api rājādīnām upāśrite 
vṛttau viśeṣaṇākāṅkṣāgamakatvān nivartate ।। 

saṃbandhiśabdaḥ sāpekṣo nityaṃ sarvaḥ prayujyate 
svārthavat sā vyapekṣāsya vṛttāv api na hīyate ।। 

samudāyena saṃbandho yesāṃ gurukulādinā 
saṃspṛśyāvayavāṃs te api yujyante tadvatā saha ।। 

abudhān praty upāyāś ca vicitrāḥ pratipattaye 
śabdāntaratvād atyantabhedo vākyasamāsayoḥ ।। 

asamāse samāse ca gorathādiṣv adarśanāt 
yuktādināṃ na śāstreṇa nivṛttyanugamaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। 

śabdāntaratvād yuktādiḥ kva cid vākye prayujyate 
praparṇaprapalāśādau gataśabdaś ca vṛttiṣu ।। 

viśeṣaṇaviśesyatvaṃ kaiś cid ekas tathāśrayaḥ 
upāye tattvadarśitvād iṣyate vṛttivākyayoḥ ।। 

padaṃ yathaiva vṛkṣādi viśiṣṭe arthe vyavasthitam 
nīlotpalādy api tathā bhāgābhyāṃ vartate vinā ।। 

śrotriyakṣetriyādināṃ na ca vāsiṣṭhagārgyavat 
bhedena pratyayo loke tulyarūpāsamanvayāt ।। 

saptaparṇādivad bhedo na vṛttau vidyate kva cit 
rūḍhyarūḍhivibhāgo api kriyate pratipattaye ।। 

yā sāmānyāśrayā saṃjñā viśeṣaviṣayā ca yā 
bahulagrahaṇān nāsti pravṛttir ubhayos tayoḥ ।। 

susūkṣmajaṭakeśādau samāso avayave yadi 
syāt syāt tatrāntaraṅgatvād bādhako avayavasvaraḥ ।। 

samudāyasya vṛttau ca naikadeśo vibhāṣyate 
bheda eva vibhāṣāyā niyato viṣayo yataḥ ।। 

yataś cāviṣayaḥ so asyās tasmān nāsty akṛtārthatā 
abhedaprakrame atyantaṃ bhedānām apasāraṇāt ।। 

mahākaṣṭaśritety evaṃ na syād bhedaḥ padatraye 
vṛttāv avayavasyāttvaṃ yasmān na pratiṣidhyate ।। 

mahāraṇyam atīte tu tripadād bhidyate svaraḥ 
yasmāt tatrāntaraṅgatvād bādhako avayavasvaraḥ ।। 

satiśiṣṭabaliyastvāt thāthādisvara eva tu 
dvipade tena yagapat tritayaṃ na samasyate ।। 

yeṣām apūjyamānatvaṃ parārthānugamātmake 
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvam api teṣāṃ na kalpate ।। 

viśeṣaḥ śrūyamāṇo api pradhāneṣu guṇeṣu vā 
śabdāntaratvād vākye tu vṛttau nityaṃ na vidyate ।। 

viśeṣakarmasaṃbandhe nirbhukte api kṛtādibhiḥ 
viśeṣanirapekṣo anyaḥ kṛtaśabdaḥ pravartate ।। 

akarmakatve saty evaṃ ktāntaṃ bhāvābhidhāyi tat 
tataḥ kriyāvatā kartrā yogo bhavati karmaṇām ।। 

avigrahā gatādisthā yathā grāmādikarmabhiḥ 
saṃbadhyate kriyā tadvat kṛtapūrvyādiṣu sthitā ।। 

muṇḍisūtrvādayo asadbhir bhāgair anugatā iva 
vibhaktāḥ kalpitātmāno dhātavaḥ kuṭṭicarcivat ।। 

putrīyatau na putro asti viśeṣecchā tu tādṛśī 
vinaiva putrānugamād yā putre vyavatiṣṭhate ।। 

prāṇair vinā yathā dhārir jīvatau prāṇakarmakaḥ 
na cātra dhārir na prāṇā jīvatis tu kriyāntaram ।। 

tathā vineṣiputrābhyāṃ putrīyāyāṃ kriyāntaram 
anvākhyānāya bhedās tu sadṛśāḥ pratipādakāḥ ।। 

ākṣepāc ca prayogena viṣayāntaravartinā 
sad apīcchākyacaḥ karma vākya eva prayujyate ।। 

prasiddhena hṛtaḥ śabdo bhāvagarhābhidhāyinā 
abhyāse tulyarūpatvān na yaṅantaḥ prayujyate ।। 

śabdā yathā vibhajyante bhāgair iva vikalpitaiḥ 
anvākhyeyās tathā śāstram atidūre vyavasthitam ।। 

arthasyānugamaṃ kaṃ cid dṛṣṭvaiva parikalpitam 
padaṃ vākye pade dhātur dhātau bhāgaś ca muṇḍivat ।। 

aviprayogaḥ sādhutve vyutpattir anavasthitā 
upāyān pratipattīnāṃ nābhimanyeta satyataḥ ।। 

yathaiva ḍitthe davatiḥ pācake pacatis tathā 
ḍayatiś ca paciś caiva dvāv apy etāv alaukikau ।। 

prakṛtipratyayāv ūhyau padāt tābhyāṃ padaṃ tathā 
anubandhasvarādibhyaḥ śiṣṭaiḥ śāstraṃ na tān prati ।। 

śāstradṛṣṭis tu śāstrasya prāptimātre apy aniścite 
yujyate pratyavāyena śāstraṃ cakṣur apaśyatām ।। 

arthāntarābhidhānāc ca paurvāparyaṃ na bhidyate 
rājadantāhitāgnyādirājāśvādiṣu sarvathā ।। 

vinaiva pratyayair vṛttau ye bhinnārthābhidhāyinaḥ 
gargādayo lukā teṣāṃ sādhutvam anugamyate ।। 

[so ayam ity abhisaṃbandhāt pratyayena vinā yadi 
bhṛgvādayaḥ prayujyeran nāpatye niyamo bhavet ।। 

so ayam ity abhisaṃbandhe liṅgopavyañjanād ṛte 
praṣṭhādiṣu na jāyaiva niyamena pratīyate ।। 

mānameyābhisaṃbandhaviśeṣe aṅgīkṛte tathā 
prasthādīnām asādhutvaṃ taddhitena vinā bhavet ।। 

taddhito yogabhedena vākyaṃ vā syād vibhāṣitam 
parimāṇādhike tatra prathamā śiṣyate punaḥ ।। 

vyatiriktasya sādhutve tad eva ca nidarśanam 
yujyate aṅgīkṛtādhikyaṃ tat sarvābhir vibhaktibhiḥ ।। 

śuklādiṣu matublopo vyatirekasya darśanāt 
asādhutvanivṛttyarthaṃ sādhavas te bidādivat ।। 

viśeṣaṇād viśeṣye arthe tadbhāvābhyuccaye sati 
punaś ca pratisaṃhāre vṛttim eke pracakṣate ।। 

nimitte pratyayaḥ pūrvo nānuprāpto nimittinā 
nimittavati buddheś ca na nimittasarūpatā ।। 

saṃskārasahitāj jñānān nopaślesaḥ smṛter api 
vyāpāre tannimittānāṃ na grāhyaṃ syāt tathā sthitam ।। 

antaḥkaraṇavṛttau ca vyarthā bāhyārthakalpanā 
tasmād anupakāre vā grāhyaṃ vā na tathā sthitam ।। 

anusyūteva saṃsṛṣṭair arthe buddhiḥ pravartate 
vyākhyātāro vibhajyārthāṃs tān bhedena pracakṣate ।। 

tadātmany avibhakte ca buddhyantaram upāśritāḥ 
vibhāgam iva manyante viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ ।। 

abudhān prati vṛttiṃ ca vartayantaḥ prakalpitām 
āhuḥ parārthavacane tyāgābhyuccayadharmatām ।। 

anvayād gamyate so artho virodhī vā nivartate 
dvyartham arthāntare vāpi tatrāhur upasarjanam ।। 

upāyamātraṃ nānātvaṃ samūhas tv eka eva saḥ 
vikalpābhyuccayābhyāṃ vā bhedasaṃsargakalpanā ।। 

vṛttiṃ vartayatām evam abudhapratipattaye 
bhinnāḥ saṃbodhanopāyāḥ puruṣeṣv anavasthitāḥ ।। 

vācikā dyotikā vāpi saṃkhyānāṃ vā vibhaktayaḥ 
tadrūpe avayave vṛttau saṃkhyābhedo nivartate ।। 

abhedaikatvasaṃkhyā vā tatrānyaivopajāyate 
saṃsargarupaṃ saiṃkhyānām avibhaktaṃ tad ucyate ।। 

yathauṣadhirasāḥ sarve madhuny āhitaśaktayaḥ 
avibhāgena vartante tāṃ saṃkhyāṃ tādṛśīṃ viduḥ ।। 

bhedānāṃ vā parityāgāt saṃkhyātmā sa tathāvidhaḥ 
vyāpārāj jātibhāgasya bhedāpohena vartate ।। 

agṛhītaviśeṣeṇa yathā rūpeṇa rūpavān 
prakhyāyate na śuklādibhedarūpas tu gṛhyate ।। 

bhedarūpasamāveśe tathā saty avivakṣite 
bhāgaḥ prakāśitaḥ kaś cic chāstre aṅgatvena gṛhyate ।। 

saṃkḥyāsāmānyarūpeṇa tadā so amśaḥ pratīyate 
arthasyānekaśaktitve śabdair niyataśaktibhiḥ ।। 

avyayānāṃ ca yo dharmo yaś ca bhedavatāṃ kramaḥ 
abhinnavyapadeśārham antarālaṃ tad etayoḥ ।। 

alukaś caikavadbhāvas tasmin sati na śiṣyate 
sa ca goṣucarādīnāṃ dharmo asti vacanāntare ।। 

jātau dvivacanābhāvāt tad vṛttiṣu na vidyate 
pratyākhyāne tu yogasya dravye goṣucarādayaḥ ।। 

āśrayād bhedavattāyāḥ sarvabhedasamanvayaḥ 
dravyābhidhānapakṣo api jātyākhyāyāṃ na vidyate ।। 

sarvadravyagatiś caivam ekaśeṣaś ca nocyate 
pratyākhyāte anyathā sūtre bhinnadravyagatir bhavet ।। 

vṛttau yo yuktavadbhāvo varaṇādiṣu śiṣyate 
abhedaikatvasaṃkhyāyāṃ godau tatra na sidhyati ।। 

prāg vṛtter yuktavadbhāve ṣaṣṭhī bhedāśrayā bhavet 
vṛttau saṃkhyāviśeṣāṇāṃ tyāgād bhedo nivartate ।। 

vidyamānāsu saṃkhyāsu ke cit saṃkhyāntaraṃ viduḥ 
abhedākhyam upagrāhi vṛttau tac copajāyate ।। 

vyāpāraṃ yāti bhedākhyais tat svair avayavaiḥ kva cit 
ātmā bhedānapekṣo asya kva cid eti nimittatām ।। 

dāsyāḥ patir iti vyakto godāv iti ca dṛśyate 
vyāpārabhedaḥ saṃkhyāyās tasmād eva vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

dvyādināṃ ca dviputrādau bāhyo bhedo nivartate 
vibhaktivācyaḥ svārthatvān nimittaṃ tv avatiṣṭhate ।। 

dvitvopasarjane saṅghe dviśabdas tatra vartate 
so ayam ity abhisaṃbandhād ubhaśabde na tat tathā ।। 

ubhayas tatra tulyārtho vṛttau nityaṃ prayujyate 
sūtre api nityagrahaṇaṃ tadartham abhidhīyate ।। 

āpi ke cāparārthatvān nābheda upajāyate 
ubhe iti tataḥ svārthe bhede vṛttiḥ prayujyate ।। 

strītvābhidhānapakṣe api guṇabhāvaviparyayaḥ 
svabhāvād aparārthatvāt tatra bhedo na hīyate ।। 

tasmād dvivacanāṭ ṭāpaś cobhayo anyatra dṛśyate 
pratyayaṃ tayapaṃ hitvā nāsty uttarapade punaḥ ।। 

prāptiḥ pragṛhyasaṃjñāyā na syāt pratyayalakṣaṇāt 
kumāryagāre na hy asti samāso vacanāntare ।। 

ekadvayor yañādināṃ vibhāṣā luṅ na kalpate 
yauṣmākas tāvakaś ceti bhedābhāvān na sidhyati ।। 

dṛṣṭo gārgyatare bhedas tathā gargatarā iti 
yuṣmatpitā tvatpiteti tathādeśau vyavasthitau ।। 

upādhibhūtā yā saṃkhyā prakṛtau samavasthitā 
ādeśaiḥ samjnayā vāpi vibhaktyā vyajyate vinā ।। 

śaurpike māsajāte ca parimāṇaṃ svabhāvataḥ 
upādhibhūtām āśritya saṃkhyāṃ bhedena vartate ।। 

vayasvini paricchedaḥ krīte cāpi na gamyate 
iṣṭo abhedād ṛte tatra patimāṇam anarthakam ।। 

bhinnasyābhedavacanāt prasthādibhyaḥ śaso vidhiḥ 
taddharmatvād abhedāt tu ghaṭādibhyo na dṛśyate ।। 

śrūyate vacanaṃ yatra bhāvas tatra viśiṣyate 
nivartate yad vacanaṃ tasya bhāvo na vidyate ।। 

kāryaṃ sattāśrayaṃ śāstrād apravṛttir adarśanam 
vākye dṛṣṭaṃ yad atyantam abhāvas tasya vṛttiṣu ।। 

samjñāviṣayabhedārthaṃ prasaktādarśanaṃ smṛtam 
śrūyamānaṃ tu vacanaṃ viśiṣṭam upalabhyate ।। 

abhāvo vā luko yatra rūpavān vā vidhīyate 
vyabhicārān nimittasya tatrāsādhuḥ prasajyate ।। 

bhedaḥ saṃkhyāviśeṣo vā vyākhyāto vṛttivākyayoḥ 
sarvatraiva viśeṣas tu nāvaśyaṃ tādṛśo bhavet ।। 

āteś ca bhedahetutvān na liṅgena viśeṣyate 
pradhānaṃ mṛgadugdhādau gārgīputre na sa kramaḥ ।। 

abhede liṅgasaṃkhyābhyāṃ yogāc chuklaṃ paṭā iti 
prasakte śāstram ārabdhaṃ siddhaye liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ ।। 

parārthaṃ śeṣabhāvaṃ yo vṛttiṣu pratipadyate 
guṇo viśeṣaṇatvena sa sūtre vyapadiśyate ।। 

śabdāntaratvād vākyeṣu viśeṣā yady api śrutāḥ 
vṛtter abhinnarūpatvāt teṣu vṛttir na vidyate ।। 

rūpāc ca śabdasaṃskāraḥ sāmānyaviṣayo yataḥ 
tasmāt tadāśrayaṃ liṅgaṃ vacanaṃ ca prasajyate ।। 

saliṅgaṃ ca sasaṃkhyaṃ ca tato dravyābhidhāyinā 
saṃbadhyate padaṃ tatra tayor bhinnā śrutir bhavet ।। 

bhāvino bahiraṅgasya vacanād āśrayasya ye 
liṅgasaṃkhye guṇānāṃ te sūtreṇa pratipādite ।। 

viśeṣavṛtter api ca rūpābhedād alakṣitaḥ 
yasmād viśeṣas tenātra bhedakāryaṃ na kalpate ।। 

viśeṣa eva sāmānyaṃ viśesād bhidyate yataḥ 
abhedo hi viśeṣāṇām āśrito vinivartakaḥ ।। 

yad yad āśrīyate tat tad anyasya vinivartakam 
bhedābhedavibhāgas tu sāmānye na nirūpyate ।। 

apoddhāraś ca sāmānyam iti tasyopakārinaḥ 
nimittāvastham evātas tat svadharmeṇa gṛhyate ।। 

anirdhāritadharmatvād bhedā eva vikalpitāḥ 
nimittair vyapadiśyante sāmānyākhyāviśesitāḥ ।। 

yadā tu vyapadiśyete liṅgasaṃkhye svabhāvataḥ 
prayogeṣv eva sādhutvaṃ vākye prakramyate tadā ।। 

tatra prayogo aniyato guṇānām āśrayaiḥ saha 
sāmānyaṃ yat tad atyantaṃ tatraiva samavasthitam ।। 

na gotvaṃ śābaleyasya gaur iti vyapadiśyate 
śuklatvaṃ bāhuleyasya śukla ity apadiśyate ।। 

vyatireke ca saty evaṃ matupaḥ śravanaṃ bhavet 
lug anvākhyāyate tasmād rasādibhyaś ca nāsti saḥ ।। 

yat so ayam iti saṃbandhād rūpābhedena vartate 
śuklādivat tato lopas tad rasādau na vidyate ।। 

āveśo liṅgasaṃkhyābhyāṃ kva cin mañcādivat sthitah 
so ayam ity abhisaṃbandhe sa prasthādau na vidyate ।। 

liṅgam liṅgaparityāge sūtraṃ pratyayaśāsanam 
so ayam ity abhisaṃbandhāt puṃśabde stryabhidhāyini ।। 

āśraye liṅgasaṃkhyābhyām āśritaṃ vyapadiśyate 
viśeṣaṇānāṃ cājāter iti śāstravyavasthayā ।। 

nimittānuvidhāyitvād ye dharmā bhedahetuṣu 
ta āśraye api vidyanta iti buddhir nivartyate ।। 

ākhyāyate ca śāstreṇa lokarūḍhā svabhāvataḥ 
nimittatulyā godādau pravṛttir liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ ।। 

haritakyādiṣu vyaktiḥ saṃkhyā khalatikādiṣu 
manuṣyalubviśeṣāṇām abhidheyāśrayaṃ dvayam ।। 

jātiprayoge jātyā cet saṃbandham upagacchati 
viśeṣaṇaṃ tato dharmāñ jātes tat pratipadyate ।। 

lubante saṃnipatitaṃ jāter anyad viśeṣaṇam 
lubantasya pradhānatvāt taddharmair vyapadiśyate ।। 

nañsamāsabahuvrīhidvandvastryatiśayeṣu ye 
bhedā bhāṣyānusāreṇa vācyās te liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ ।। 

yadi ṣaṣṭhīdvitīyāntān nikṛṣṭāt tamabādayaḥ 
nyakkāriṇi syur utkṛṣṭe prakṛteḥ syād viliṅgatā ।। 

kālyāṃ kālād dvitīyāntāt kāle kālyās tarab bhavet 
nyakkāriṇi tathā gārgye gargebhyaḥ pratyayo bhavet ।। 

nyakkartṛṣu ca gargeṣu gārgyāt syāt tac ca neṣyate 
kumāryāḥ svārthike ṅīp syāt prakṛtyartho hi nādhikaḥ ।। 

ṣaṣṭhyantād adhike tasmād guṇe svāśrayavartini 
utkṛṣṭasamavetāyāṃ kriyāyāṃ vā vidhīyate ।। 

upāttaṃ ca prakṛtyartho dravyam evāśrayas tayoḥ 
so ayam ity abhisaṃbandhād abhedena pratīyate ।। 

rūpābhedāc ca tad dravyam ākāṅkṣāvat pratīyate 
viśeṣair bhinnarūpais tad āśrayair iva yujyate ।। 

bhinnarūpesu yal liṅgaṃ viśeṣesu vyavasthitam 
saṃkhyā ca tābhyām dravyātmā so abhinno vyapadiśyate ।। 

āśrayaḥ samavāyi ca nimittaṃ liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ 
kartṛsthabhāvakaḥ śetir ato bhāṣya udāhṛtaḥ ।। 

nimittam āśrayatvena gṛhyeta yadi sādhanam 
karmāpadiṣṭayoḥ prāptis tatra syāl liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ ।। 

śāstre nimittabhāvena samudāyād apoddhṛtaḥ 
stryarthas tasyecchayā yogaḥ prakṛtyā pratyayena vā ।। 

strīśabdo guṇaśabdatvāt tulyadharmā sitādibhiḥ 
guṇamātre prayujyeta saṃstyānavati vāśraye ।। 

stryarthaḥ saṃstyānavad dravyaṃ prakṛtyarthaś ca yady asau 
dravyopalakṣaṇārthatvaṃ saṃstyānasya tathā sati ।। 

saṃstyānena kva cid dravyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yady upalakṣitam 
anaṅgīkṛtasaṃstyānāt tadvṛtteḥ pratyayo bhavet ।। 

bhūtādayaḥ ṣaḍākhyāś ca saṃstyānenopalakṣite 
brāhmaṇyādau yadā vṛttās tebhyaḥ syuḥ pratyayās tadā ।। 

tadvanto hi pradhānatvāt pratyayāṇām prayojakāḥ 
sāmānādhikaraiṇye api tasmāṭ ṭābādisaṃbhavaḥ ।। 

guṇamātrābhidhāyitvaṃ strīśabde varṇyate yadā 
prakṛtyarthaś ca saṃstyānaṃ svārthikāḥ pratyayās tadā ।। 

saṃstyāne kevale vṛttiḥ prakṛtīnām na vidyate 
tadāviṣṭe tato dravye gṛhyante samavasthitāḥ ।। 

upakāri ca saṃstyānaṃ yeṣu śabdeṣv apekṣitam 
tebhyaṣ ṭābādayas tac ca bhūtādiṣv avivakṣitam ।। 

saṃstyānaṃ pratyayasyārthaḥ śuddham āśrīyate yadā 
tadā dvivacanānekapratyayatvaṃ na sidhyati ।। 

jātiś cet strītvam evāsau bhedo anyatrāvivakṣitaḥ 
yasmād bhinnair api dravyais tad ekaṃ sad viśiṣyate ।। 

mātrāṇām hi tirobhāve parimāṇam na vidyate 
kumārya iti tena syāt kumāryāṃ bhedasaṃbhavāt ।। 

jātisaṃkhyāsamāhārair yathaiva sahacāriṇi 
dravye kriyāḥ pravartanta ekātmatve vyapekṣite ।। 

mūrtibhyo mūrtidharmāṇām tathābhedasya darśanāt 
sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca kriyāyogaś ca kalpate ।। 

sāmānādhikaraṇye tu matublopād apekṣite 
luk taddhitalukīti syāl luk tatrāpy upalakṣaṇam ।। 

kesāṃ cit tyaktabhedeṣu dravyeṣv eva vidhīyate 
saṃstyānavatsu ṭābādir abhedena samanvayāt ।। 

sāmānyabhūto dravyātmā paricchinnaparigrahaḥ 
kriyābhir yujyate bhedair bhāgaśaś cāvatiṣṭhate ।। 

śuklādiṣv āśrayadravyaṃ prādhānyenābhidhīyate 
strītvaṃ tu pratyayārthatvād abhidhāviṣayo yataḥ ।। 

so ayam ity abhisaṃbandhād āśrayaṃ pratipadyate 
strītvaṃ svabhāvasiddho vā guṇabhāvaviparyayaḥ ।। 

sākāṅkṣatvād guṇatvena sāmānyaṃ vopadiśyate 
vyaktīnām ātmadharmo asāv ekaprakhyānibandhanaḥ ।। 

evambhūtā ca sāvasthā bhāgabhedaparigrahe 
kṛte buddhyaiva bhedānām āśrayatve ca kalpite ।। 

niskṛṣṭeṣv api bhedeṣu vyaktirūpāśraye tataḥ 
liṅgapratyavamarśena liṅgasaṃkhye prapadyate ।। 

antarena caśabdasya prayogaṃ dvandvabhāvinām 
aviśiṣṭārthavṛttitvaṃ rūpābhedāt pratīyate ।। 

vikalpavati vā vṛttir nivartye atha samuccite 
teṣām ajñātaśaktīnāṃ dyotakena niyamyate ।। 

vṛttau viśiṣṭarūpatvāc caśabdo vinivartate 
arthabhede api sārūpyāt tac cārthenāpadiśyate ।। 

casya cāsattvabhūto arthaḥ sa evāśriyate yadi 
taddharmatvaṃ tato dvandve cādiṣv arthakṛtaṃ hi tat ।। 

cārthaḥ śabde kva cid bhedāt kathaṃ cit samavasthitaḥ 
dyotakāś cādayas tasya vaktā dvandvas tu tadvatām ।। 

vikalpādyabhidheyasya cārthasyānyapadārthatā 
dyotakatvān na kalpeta tasmāt sad upalakṣyate ।। 

tatra svābhāvikaṃ liṅgaṃ śabdadharme vyapekṣite 
śabdaḥ kaś cit tam evārthaṃ kathaṃ cit pratipadyate ।। 

śabdād arthāḥ pratāyante sa bhedānāṃ vidhāyakaḥ 
anumānaṃ vivakṣāyāḥ śabdād anyan na vidyate ।। 

samuccitaḥ syād dvandvārtho guṇabhūtasamuccayaḥ 
samuccayo vāpi bhaved guṇabhūtasamuccitaḥ ।। 

samuccitasya prādhānye liṅgasaṃkhye svabhāvataḥ 
samuccayasya prādhānye śāstraṃ syāt pratipādakam ।। 

samuccayavato arthasya prādhānye apy apare viduḥ 
nimittānuvidhāyitvād asiddhim liṅgasaṃkhyayoḥ ।। 

samuccayo nimittaṃ cet syān nimittānuvartanam 
anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ cārtho dvandvanibandhanaḥ ।। 

samuccitanimittatve cārthasyāpagame api vā 
svabhāvasiddhe dvandvasya liṅgasaṃkhye vyavasthite ।। 

padāntarasthasyārthasya dyotakatvān na yujyate 
nipāto liṅgasaṃkhyābhyāṃ dvandvas tv arthasya vācakaḥ ।। 

nimittānuvidhāne ca dravyadharmānapekṣaṇāt 
guṇapradhānabhāvena kriyāyogo na kalpate ।। 

yasya nāsti kriyāyogaḥ svatantro asau na vidyate 
artho dvandvasya tatra syād upādānam anarthakam ।। 

samuccayavato arthasya vācako nānuvartate 
nimittam api cāsyārthaḥ svadharmair yujyate tataḥ ।। 

bāhyo nāsty āśrayo dvandve viśeṣau tatra hi śrutau 
samuccayas tadādhāras taddharmair vyapadiśyate ।। 

yo vāvayavabhedābhyāṃ bhedavadbhyām ivānvitaḥ 
ekaḥ samūho dharmān sa bhāgayoḥ pratipadyate ।। 

ekaś ca dvyātmako artho asau bhedābhedasamanvitaḥ 
yau bhedāv āśritas tatsthe liṅgasaṃkhye prapadyate ।। 

yathā svaśabdābhihite caitrārthe na prayujyate 
caitraśabdo bahuvrihāv aprayogas tathā bhavet ।। 

yathā gaur iti śuklāder abhidhānaṃ na vidyate 
evaṃ yasyābhisaṃbandho gobhis tāvat pratīyate ।। 

saṃbandhī niyato rūḍhaś citrāṇāṃ na ca vidyate 
gavāṃ yathā vajrapāṇis tryakṣe vā api vyavasthitaḥ ।। 

śabdāntaratvād vākyeṣu viśeṣā yady api śrutāḥ 
vṛttiśabdo anya evāyaṃ sāmānyasyābhidhāyakaḥ ।। 

agor acitragoś caiva rūpabhedān nivartakaḥ 
na citragur viśeṣāṇāṃ rūpābhedāt tu vācakaḥ ।। 

yathā citragur ity etat prayukte na prayujyate 
evaṃ yadi syāt sāmānyaṃ tasya na syāt pratiśrutiḥ ।। 

sarvādayo viśeṣās tu pradeśānāṃ nivartakāḥ 
yathā pradeśāḥ sāmānyapradeśāntarabādhakāḥ ।। 

vibhaktyarthābhidhānād vā ṣaṣṭhī nānuprayujyate 
dravyasyānabhidhānāt tu tacchabdo anuprayujyate ।। 

sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ cen matublopāt prakalpate 
matupo api tadarthatvād anavasthā prasajyate ।। 

saṃbandhasya ca saṃbandī saṃbandho anyaḥ prasajyate 
vibhaktyarthapradhāne ca kriyāyogo na kalpate ।। 

vibhaktyarthapradhānatvāt tatas tatreti na kriyā 
dṛśyādiḥ karmakartrādinimittatvāya kalpate ।। 

antarbhavec ca saṃbandhaḥ prādhānyābhihitaḥ katham 
sa prātipadikārthaś ca tathābhūtaḥ kathaṃ bhatvet ।। 

asaṃbhavāt tu saṃbandhe saṃbandhasahacāriṇi 
jātisaṃkhyāsamāhārakāryāṇām iva saṃbhavaḥ ।। 

so ayam ity abhisaṃbandhād viśiṣṭāśrayavācinām 
śuklādival liṅgasaṃkhye śāstrārambhād bhaviṣyataḥ ।। 

bhedena tu vivakṣāyāṃ sāmānye vā vivakṣite 
saliṅgasya sasaṃkhyasya padārthasyāgatir bhavet ।। 

sādhutvaṃ na vibhaktyarthamātre vṛttasya dṛśyate 
kṛtsnārthavṛtteḥ sādhutvam ity arthagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam ।। 

so ayam ity abhisaṃbandhād dravyavṛttir ayaṃ yadā 
saliṅgasya sasaṃkhyasya tadā sādhutvam ucyate ।। 

antarbhūtavibhaktyarthe ṣaṣṭhī na śrūyate yathā 
tathāśrutiḥ prasajyeta liṅgasaṃkhyābhidhāyinām ।। 

sādharmyam avyayena syād bahuvrīhes tathā sati 
liṅgasaṃkhyānimittasya saṃskārasyāpavartanāt ।। 

prayuktena ca saṃbandhāc caitrādiśravanaṃ bhavet 
vinā vibhaktyā saṃbandho vibhaktyā vidyate vinā ।। 

abhidhāne api saṃkhyāyāḥ saṃkhyātvaṃ na nivartate 
ṣaṣṭhyarthasyābhidhāne tu syāt prātipadikārthatā ।। 

anuprayogasiddhyarthaṃ na vibhaktyarthakalpanā 
vastvantaram upakṣiptam iti ke cit pracakṣate ।। 

saṃbandibhir viśiṣṭānām saṃbandhānāṃ nimittatā 
saṃbandhair vā viśiṣṭānāṃ tadvatāṃ syān nimittatā ।। 

ke cit saṃyogino daṇḍād viṣāṇāt samavāyinaḥ 
tadvati pratyayān āhur bahuvrīhiṃ tathaiva ca ।। 

bhinnaṃ saṃbandhibhedena saṃbandham apare viduḥ 
nimittaṃ sa vibhaktyarthaḥ samāsenābhidhīyate ।। 

pradhānam anyārthatayā bhinnaṃ svair upasarjanaiḥ 
nimittam abbidheyaṃ vā sarvapaścād apekṣyate ।। 

svāmini vyatirekaś ca vākye yady api dṛśyate 
prādhānya eva tasyeṣṭo bahuvrīhir vivakṣite ।। 

gavāṃ viśeṣaṇatvena yadā tadvān pravartate 
asyaitā iti tatrārthe bahuvrīhir na vidyate ।। 

yadā pratyavamarśas tu tāsāṃ svāmī gavām iti 
gobhis tadābhisaṃbandho nimittatvāya kalpate ।। 

apekṣamānaḥ saṃbandhaṃ rūḍhitvasya nivṛttaye 
nimittānuvidhāyitvāt taddharmārthaḥ prasajyate ।। 

nānā citrā iti yathā nimittam anurudhyate 
nānābhūte api vṛttaḥ san bahuvrīhis tathā bhavet ।। 

saṃbandhini nimitte tu dravyadharmo na hīyate 
liṅgābhāvo hi liṅgasya virodhitvena vartate ।। 

saṃkhvāvāṃl liṅgavāmś cārtho abhinnadharmā, nimittataḥ 
āsanna eva dravyatvāt taddharmair na virudhyate ।। 

vibhaktyarthena cāviṣṭaṃ śuddhaṃ ceti dvidhā sthitam 
dravyaṃ śuddhasya yo dharmaḥ sa na syād anyadharmaṇaḥ ।। 

dravyamātrasya nirdeśe bhedo ayam avivakṣitaḥ 
granthe pūrvatra bhedas tu dvitīye anupradarśitaḥ ।। 

dravyasya grahaṇaṃ cātra liṅgasaṃkhyāviśeṣaṇam 
dravyāśritatvaṃ hi tayos tato anyasya na sidhyataḥ ।। 

saṃbandhibhinnasaṃbandhaparichinne pravartate 
samāso dravyasāmānye viśiṣṭārthānupātini ।। 

dravyadharmānatikrānto bhedadharmeṣv avasthitaḥ 
bhaviṣyadāśrayāpekṣe liṅgasaṃkhye prapadyate ।। 

śāstrapravṛttibhede api laukiko artho na bhidyate 
nañsamase yatas tatra trayaḥ pakṣā vicāritāḥ ।। 

śabdāntare api caikatvam āśrityaivaṃ vicāraṇā 
abrahmaṇādiṣu nañaḥ prayogo na hi vidyate ।। 

prāk samāsāt padārthānāṃ nivṛttir dyotyate nañā 
svabhāvato nivṛttānāṃ rūpābhedād alakṣitā ।। 

brāhmaṇādisthayā vākyeṣv ākhyātapadavācyayā 
kriyayā yasya saṃbandho vṛttis tasya na vidyate ।। 

pācakādipadasthā cen nañā saṃbadhyate kriyā 
tatra sattānupādānāt tripakṣī nopapadyate ।। 

sattayaivābhisaṃbandho yadi sarvatra kalpyate 
asann iti samāse asmin sattānyā parikalpyatām ।। 

ktvānte ca tumunante ca nañsamāse na dṛśyate 
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ nañāsattābhidhāyinā ।। 

kriyāyāḥ sādhanādhārasāmānye nañ vyavasthitaḥ 
tato viśiṣṭair ādhārair yujyate brāhmaṇādibhiḥ ।। 

vṛttau yathā gatādyartham upādāya nirādayaḥ 
yujyante sādhanādhārair nañsamāse api sa kramaḥ ।। 

tatrāsati naño vṛtter brāhmaṇakṣatriyādibhiḥ 
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ kalpyate kubjakhañjavat ।। 

kāmacāre ca saty evam asataḥ syāt pradhānatā, 
guṇatvam itareṣāṃ ca teṣāṃ vā syāt pradhānatā ।। 

prādhānyenāśritāḥ pūrvaṃ śruteḥ sāmānyavṛttayaḥ
